### [1] [No evidence for phantom crossing: local goodness-of-fit improvements do not persist under global Bayesian model comparison](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13546)
*Bikash R. Dinda,Roy Maartens,Shun Saito*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文通过比较ΛCDM、w₀wₐ和thawing quintessence三类暗能量模型，利用偏差信息准则（Deviation Information Criterion, DIC）和贝叶斯证据（Bayesian evidence, ln 𝒵）进行统计分析，发现所有模型在统计上不可区分，当前数据并不支持动态暗能量（dynamical dark energy）或幻影穿越（phantom crossing）的稳健检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期宇宙学数据在标准w₀wₐ参数化框架下暗示了偏离ΛCDM（Lambda Cold Dark Matter）模型的迹象，包括幻影穿越和动态暗能量的可能信号。然而，这类推断可能依赖参数化形式（parametrization-dependent），未必具有统计显著性；因此需要更严格的统计检验来评估其可靠性。

Method: 采用偏差信息准则（Deviance Information Criterion, DIC）和贝叶斯证据（Bayesian evidence, ln 𝒵）作为模型选择工具，对ΛCDM、w₀wₐ参数化以及thawing quintessence（解冻型第五元素）三类暗能量模型进行统计比较分析。

Result: w₀wₐ模型在局部拟合上略有改进，但仅限于参数空间（parameter space）的有限区域。全局贝叶斯证据在考虑完整先验体积（prior volume）后不支持该模型。出现ΔDIC < 0但Δln 𝒵 < 0的情况，表明这些改进不具备统计显著性。所有模型在统计上不可区分，且不同数据集之间不存在一致的统计证据支持动态暗能量或幻影穿越。

Conclusion: 当前宇宙学数据尚不能为动态暗能量或幻影穿越提供统计稳健的检测证据，提示相关早期推断可能源于参数化依赖性和先验体积效应，需谨慎解读。

Abstract: Recent cosmological data have been interpreted as indicating deviations from $Λ$CDM within the standard $w_0w_a$ parametrization, including hints of phantom crossing and dynamical dark energy. However, such inferences can be parametrization-dependent and need not imply a statistically robust detection. We test these claims by comparing $Λ$CDM, $w_0w_a$, and thawing quintessence models, using the Deviance Information Criterion (DIC) and the Bayesian evidence $\ln \mathcal{Z}$. We find that $w_0w_a$ can provide a slightly improved local fit, but this improvement is confined to a limited region of parameter space. The global Bayesian evidence does not support it once the full prior volume is taken into account. In particular, cases with $Δ{\rm DIC}<0$ but $Δ\ln \mathcal{Z}<0$ indicate that these improvements are not statistically significant. We show that all models are statistically indistinguishable, and that there is no statistically consistent evidence across different datasets for either dynamical dark energy or phantom crossing.

</details>

# nucl-th [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Spin dynamics and polarization in relativistic systems: recent developments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12554)
*Sourav Dey,Arpan Das,Hiranmaya Mishra,Amaresh Jaiswal*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文综述了相对论性系统中自旋动力学与极化现象的最新理论与实验进展，重点讨论了重离子碰撞中由涡旋性引发的自旋极化、赝规范自由度对自旋张量定义的影响、自旋流体力学的不同构造，以及基于旋转布朗运动的重味自旋动力学框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重离子非对心碰撞中产生的大角动量与强磁场导致夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma）出现涡旋性，进而引发可观测的强子自旋极化现象。本文旨在系统梳理该领域的理论基础与最新进展，推动对自旋现象一致且可预测的描述。

Method: 基于自旋-涡旋耦合（spin-vorticity coupling）的理论框架，涵盖相对论性流体力学（relativistic hydrodynamics）、动理学理论（kinetic theory）以及量子统计方法（如Zubarev密度算符）。通过探讨赝规范自由度（pseudo-gauge freedom）对能量-动量张量与自旋张量定义的影响，分析不同形式的自旋流体力学及其梯度展开、自旋化学势和熵流分析。此外，引入旋转布朗运动（rotational Brownian motion）模型处理重味自旋动力学。

Result: 赝规范自由度的选择会影响极化观测量（polarization observables）的理论预言；不同自旋流体力学构造在梯度展开、自旋化学势及输运系数结构上存在差异；旋转布朗运动框架能够描述自旋弛豫与扩散过程，并将自旋极化与初始几何通过极化谐波（polarization harmonics）联系起来。

Conclusion: 本文为相对论性自旋流体力学与非平衡自旋动力学提供了全面综述，指出了构建强相互作用物质中自旋现象的一致且可预测描述的未来发展方向。

Abstract: We review recent theoretical and experimental developments in spin dynamics and polarization phenomena in relativistic systems, with a particular focus on heavy-ion collisions. The large angular momentum and magnetic field generated in non-central collisions induce vorticity in the quark-gluon plasma, leading to observable spin polarization of emitted hadrons. We discuss the theoretical foundations of spin polarization arising from spin-vorticity coupling, including formulations based on relativistic hydrodynamics, kinetic theory, and quantum statistical approaches such as the Zubarev density operator. A central theme of the review is the role of pseudo-gauge freedom and its implications for defining energy-momentum and spin tensors, which can influence theoretical predictions of polarization observables. We further examine different formulations of spin hydrodynamics, emphasizing the impact of gradient expansions, spin chemical potential, and entropy-current analysis on the structure of the theory and associated transport coefficients. In addition, we discuss the recent developments in heavy flavor spin dynamics within the framework of rotational Brownian motion, where spin degrees of freedom undergo stochastic evolution due to interactions with the medium. This framework provides a complementary perspective on spin relaxation and diffusion by incorporating the effects of strong initial magnetic fields and establishes connections between spin polarization and the initial geometry through the definition of polarization harmonics. This review provides a comprehensive overview of relativistic spin hydrodynamics as well as non-equilibrium spin dynamics, and outlines future directions toward a consistent and predictive description of spin phenomena in strongly interacting matter.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.supr-con'></div>

# cond-mat.supr-con [[Back]](#toc)

### [3] [Yu-Shiba-Rusinov States in Ising Superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12758)
*Michael Hein,Juan Carlos Cuevas,Wolfgang Belzig*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过单磁杂质作为局域探针，从理论上研究了二维过渡金属二硫化物中伊辛超导态的Yu-Shiba-Rusinov束缚态，发现其能谱和隧穿响应具有区别于传统超导体的独特特征，表明磁杂质可灵敏探测非常规超导态的结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维过渡金属二硫化物（two-dimensional transition-metal dichalcogenides）中的超导态本质仍存在争议，常见的“伊辛超导（Ising superconductivity）”描述虽被广泛使用但尚未被充分检验，亟需发展有效的局域探针来揭示其配对结构。

Method: 理论上采用单磁杂质作为超导凝聚体（superconducting condensate）的局域探针，分析在伊辛自旋-轨道耦合（Ising spin-orbit coupling）和面内磁场（in-plane magnetic field）共同作用下Yu-Shiba-Rusinov束缚态的形成，并通过计算其谱学性质来编码配对结构的特征。

Result: 束缚态能谱和隧穿响应（tunneling response）中识别出区别于传统超导体的独特特征，这些特征直接反映了伊辛超导的非常规配对结构。

Conclusion: 磁杂质可作为灵敏探针用于表征超导态的结构，其产生的可实验观测信号为鉴别伊辛超导的非常规方面提供了可行途径。

Abstract: The nature of the superconducting state in two-dimensional transition-metal dichalcogenides remains under active debate. A widely used description invokes so-called Ising superconductivity. In this work, we investigate theoretically this pairing state by employing single magnetic impurities as local probes of the superconducting condensate. We analyze the formation of Yu-Shiba-Rusinov bound states in the presence of Ising spin-orbit coupling and an in-plane magnetic field to study how their spectral properties encode the underlying pairing structure. We identify distinct features in the bound-state spectrum and tunneling response that differentiate this system from conventional superconductors. Our results demonstrate that magnetic impurities provide a sensitive probe of the structure of the superconducting state and yield experimentally accessible signatures of unconventional aspects of Ising superconductivity.

</details>


### [4] [Multiband Superconductivity in the Exactly Solvable Hatsugai-Kohmoto Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13259)
*Nico Hahn,R. Matthias Geilhufe*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文在多带（multiband）Hatsugai-Kohmoto模型中研究超导配对态，利用该可精确求解的关联电子模型分析了强关联、轨道结构和配对对称性的相互作用；针对具有D4h点群对称性的双轨道系统，分类了对称性允许的超导能隙结构，并通过平均场方法计算了临界温度和超导序参量，为关联多带系统中的超导分析提供了系统性框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多带超导（multiband superconductivity）会产生丰富的配对态（pairing states），但强关联效应、轨道自由度与配对对称性之间的相互作用尚缺乏简单可解的理论框架加以探索。

Method: 采用Hatsugai-Kohmoto模型的多带推广（multiband extension），该模型具有动量局域相互作用（momentum-local interactions）并精确可解；针对具有D4h点群对称性的双轨道系统，基于自旋、轨道和动量自由度分类对称性允许的超导能隙结构，并通过平均场（mean-field）方法计算选定配对通道的临界温度和超导序参量。

Result: 给出了轨道Hatsugai-Kohmoto模型中对称性允许的超导能隙结构分类，并得到了临界温度和超导序参量随相互作用强度（interaction strength）和配对强度（pairing strength）的变化关系。

Conclusion: 本文为分析轨道Hatsugai-Kohmoto模型中的超导电性提供了一个系统性框架，并将基于对称性的方法（symmetry-based approaches）推广到了关联多带（correlated multiband）体系中。

Abstract: Multiband superconductivity gives rise to a rich landscape of possible pairing states. Here we study superconductivity in the multiband extension of the Hatsugai-Kohmoto model, an exactly solvable model of correlated electrons with momentum-local interactions, which provides a minimal framework to explore the interplay of strong correlations, orbital structure and pairing symmetry. Focusing on a two-orbital system with point-group symmetry $\rm D_{4h}$, we classify the symmetry-allowed superconducting gap structures, taking into account spin, orbital and momentum degrees of freedom. We further compute the critical temperature and the superconducting order parameter for selected pairing channels as functions of interaction and pairing strength within a mean-field treatment. Our results provide a systematic framework for analyzing superconductivity in the orbital Hatsugai-Kohmoto model and extend symmetry-based approaches to correlated multiband settings.

</details>


### [5] [Singular spin fluctuations in the strange-metal phase of La2-xSrxCuO4](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13573)
*B. Costarella,L. Soriano,I. Vinograd,H. Mayaffre,S. Li,J. Yang,J. Luo,R. Zhou,J. Yao,G. Gu,Q. Li,J. M. Tranquada,M. -H. Julien*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过高磁场抑制超导电性及针对电子不均匀性设计的核磁共振（NMR）方法，发现过掺杂铜氧化物 La2-xSrxCuO4（x=0.25）中低能极限的动力学自旋磁化率（χ''(q,ω)）持续随温度降低而升高，暗示量子临界涨落（quantum-critical fluctuations）的存在，且该行为发生在自旋条纹临界掺杂（x=0.19）之外；数据进一步揭示自旋动力学在空间上不均匀，表明纳米尺度的电子不均匀性可能是这一表面矛盾的原因。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管自旋涨落（spin fluctuation）对高温铜氧化物超导体（high-Tc cuprates）的物理性质至关重要，但自旋涨落在过掺杂区（overdoped regime）与非费米液体奇异金属行为（strange-metal behavior）之间的关联仍不清楚，该研究旨在澄清这一问题。

Method: 利用高磁场抑制超导电性，并采用针对电子不均匀性（electronic inhomogeneity）设计的核磁共振（NMR）协议，测量 La2-xSrxCuO4（x=0.25）样品中低能极限的动力学自旋磁化率（dynamical spin susceptibility）χ''(q,ω)。

Result: 在最低温度下，低能极限的 χ''(q,ω) 持续增加，表现出量子临界涨落的特征，且该行为出现在自旋条纹临界掺杂 x=0.19 之外；同时，自旋动力学存在空间不均匀性（spatially inhomogeneous）。

Conclusion: 这些观测结果暗示，纳米尺度的电子不均匀性（nanoscale electronic inhomogeneity）可能解释了为何量子临界涨落出现在预期之外的掺杂区间，从而为奇异金属行为从何电子态中涌现提供了新的见解。

Abstract: Although spin fluctuations are central to the physics of high-Tc cuprates, their relevance to strange-metal behavior in the overdoped regime remains unclear. Here, we use high magnetic fields to suppress superconductivity and an NMR protocol tailored to electronic inhomogeneity to show that the low-energy limit of the dynamical spin susceptibility χ''(q,omega) at x=0.25 in La2-xSrxCuO4 increases continuously down to our lowest temperatures. This behavior is suggestive of quantum-critical fluctuations, a leading candidate mechanism for strange-metal transport, yet is observed well beyond the spin-stripe critical doping x=0.19. Our data further reveal that the spin dynamics are spatially inhomogeneous, suggesting that nanoscale electronic inhomogeneity may underlie this apparent paradox. These observations provide new insight into the electronic state from which strange-metal behavior emerges.

</details>


### [6] [Nodal Topological Superconductivity Driven by Crystalline Antiunitary Symmetry in Altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13656)
*Xiao Xiao,Arun Bansil*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文在交错磁体（altermagnets）中发现了一种由对称性约束的节线拓扑超导（nodal topological superconductivity）机制，揭示了本征晶体反幺正对称性（antiunitary symmetry）如何强制选择配对结构并产生具有手征对称性（chiral symmetry）的Bogoliubov-de Gennes哈密顿量，进而导致多种稳健的节线拓扑相，包括Majorana平带和手征Majorana边缘态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑超导（topological superconductivity）能够容纳受保护的准粒子，对拓扑量子计算（topological quantum computation）至关重要，但在本征材料中实现拓扑超导仍然极具挑战，通常依赖于人工工程平台。本文旨在探索交错磁体中是否存在一种由对称性约束的、无需人工工程的节线拓扑超导机制。

Method: 作者聚焦于四重旋转共线交错磁体（fourfold rotational collinear altermagnets），通过对称性分析揭示本征晶体反幺正对称性$\mathcal{T}C_{4z}$如何禁止纯自旋单态配对（pure spin-singlet pairing），并选择特定的配对结构，从而导出具有涌现手征对称性（emergent chiral symmetries）的Bogoliubov-de Gennes (BdG)哈密顿量。

Result: 该对称性约束机制产生了三种稳健的节线拓扑相：一个具有Majorana平带（Majorana flat bands, MFBs）的节点相（nodal-point phase）和两个具有手征Majorana边缘态（chiral Majorana edge states）的不同节线环相（nodal-loop phases）。即使在反幺正对称性自发破缺后，节线结构仍然存在，表明拓扑起源于对称性约束的配对而非直接的对称性保护。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种在本征交错磁体中实现节线拓扑超导的新机制，并通过理论分析预言了可通过隧穿信号（tunneling signatures）区分这些节线相并实验探测对称性破缺的实验方案。

Abstract: Topological superconductivity hosts protected quasiparticles and is central to topological quantum computation, yet its realization in intrinsic materials remains challenging and often relies on engineered platforms. Here we uncover a symmetry-constrained mechanism for nodal topological superconductivity in altermagnets. Focusing on fourfold rotational collinear altermagnets, we show that the native crystalline antiunitary symmetry $\mathcal{T}C_{4z}$ generically forbids pure spin-singlet pairing and selects pairing structures that admit Bogoliubov-de Gennes (BdG) Hamiltonians with emergent chiral symmetries. These symmetries further give rise to robust nodal topological phases over broad parameter regimes, including a nodal-point phase hosting Majorana flat bands (MFBs) and two distinct nodal-loop phases with chiral Majorana edge states. Notably, the nodal structure persists even after spontaneous breaking of the antiunitary symmetry, indicating that the topology originates from symmetry-constrained pairing rather than direct symmetry protection. Finally, we propose tunneling signatures that can distinguish these nodal phases and probe symmetry breaking experimentally.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.soft'></div>

# cond-mat.soft [[Back]](#toc)

### [7] [Fluctuation-Dissipation Framework for Size-Dependent Surface Tension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13244)
*Sergii Burian,Yevhenii Shportun,Liudmyla Klochko,Leonid Bulavin,Dmytro Gavryushenko,Mykola Isaiev*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文发展了一个热力学-统计力学框架，将Tolman长度（液-气界面张力的一阶曲率修正）与单组分液体在液-气共存线附近的体相响应性质联系起来。对于弱可压缩液体，曲率效应通过蒸气过饱和进入考虑。在平面极限下，Tolman长度可表达为液体等温压缩系数及其压力导数的组合，或等价于等温等压系综中体积涨落的二、三阶矩。对水的估算结果为约-0.7 Å。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纳米尺度下，液-气表面张力（surface tension）的尺寸依赖性控制着相变、润湿和输运过程，但其一阶曲率修正——Tolman长度（Tolman length）——长期以来难以确定。本文旨在建立该修正与体相性质之间的严格联系。

Method: 基于热力学（thermodynamics）与统计力学（statistical mechanics）框架，针对弯曲界面同时考虑过余压力（excess pressures）和相对密度偏差（relative density deviations）两种局域毛细-化学平衡表述方式。在弱可压缩液体情形下，采用非对称的基于密度的公式，其中有限曲率效应通过毛细平衡下的蒸气过饱和（vapor supersaturation）引入。平面极限下的Tolman长度被重新表达为等温等压系综（isothermal-isobaric ensemble）中均匀液体的涨落-响应可观测量，即体积分布的二阶和三阶中心矩。

Result: 对水的SPC/E和TIP4P/2005模型进行均匀（N,P,T）分子动力学模拟（不显式模拟液-气界面），得到300 K下Tolman长度约为-0.7 Å。基于IAPWS-IF97工业物性公式的独立评估给出Tolman长度为-0.713 ± 0.004 Å，并预测沿共存线存在弱非单调的温度依赖性。

Conclusion: 该框架适用于其他单组分液体，前提是具备精确的热状态方程（equation of state）或充分收敛的体相体积统计量。这一方法将Tolman长度的确定从界面模拟转向了体相涨落分析，简化了计算路径。

Abstract: The size-dependent liquid-vapor surface tension controls phase change, wetting, and transport at nanoscales, yet its first curvature correction, the Tolman length, remains difficult to determine. We develop a thermodynamic and statistical-mechanical framework that relates this correction to bulk response properties of a one-component liquid near liquid-vapor coexistence. For curved interfaces, the analysis considers two local formulations of the same capillary-chemical balance, in excess pressures and in relative density deviations. For weakly compressible liquids in the regime emphasized here, the adopted asymmetric density-based formulation is the practically relevant one, with finite-curvature effects entering through vapor supersaturation under capillary equilibrium. At coexistence, the planar-limit value of the same Tolman length reduces to a combination of the liquid isothermal compressibility and its pressure derivative and can be recast as a bulk fluctuation-response observable of the homogeneous liquid in the isothermal-isobaric ensemble. In this representation, the planar-limit coefficient is determined by second and third central moments of the volume distribution, equivalently by the pressure response of the relative fluctuation width. For water, homogeneous (N,P,T) simulations of SPC/E and TIP4P/2005 sample the bulk liquid, not an explicit liquid-vapor interface, and yield estimates near -0.7 Angstrom at 300 K. An independent evaluation based on the IAPWS-IF97 industrial formulation gives -0.713 +/- 0.004 Angstrom at the same coexistence state and predicts a weakly nonmonotonic temperature dependence along coexistence. Beyond water, the framework applies to other one-component liquids in regimes where an accurate thermal equation of state or sufficiently converged bulk volume statistics are available.

</details>


<div id='physics.optics'></div>

# physics.optics [[Back]](#toc)

### [8] [Ghost State of Light](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13584)
*R. M. de Boer,C. Toebes,Jan Klars,S. R. K. Rodriguez*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文在单模光学腔（single-mode optical cavity）中观测到一种长寿命的非定态光状态，即鞍结分岔的“幽灵”（ghost of a saddle-node bifurcation）。通过引入具有记忆效应的非线性响应机制，实验实现了寿命超过腔光子寿命十个数量级的幽灵态，并展示了其与预热化（prethermalization）相似的弛豫动力学平台及标度行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 鞍结分岔的幽灵态在相空间中（phase space）表现为一个瓶颈（bottleneck），已知其存在但极难观测，关键在于缺乏一种能够将弛豫路径从真实吸引子（true attractor）引导至瓶颈区域的机制。本文旨在识别并实现这种机制，从而在实验上获得这种长寿命非定态。

Method: 实验基于单模光学腔系统，利用一种具有记忆（memory）的非线性响应机制，将系统的弛豫路径偏离真实吸引子，导向鞍结分岔幽灵所在的相空间瓶颈区域。通过测量腔透射率（cavity transmission）的弛豫动力学，观察幽灵态的出现及其寿命。

Result: 实验成功观测到幽灵态，其寿命超过腔光子寿命（cavity photon lifetime）十个数量级以上，且即使在强涨落（strong fluctuations）环境下仍能保持稳定。幽灵态在透射率弛豫动力学中表现为一个平台（plateau），类似于预热化现象。研究进一步展示了幽灵寿命对记忆时间和到分岔点的距离的依赖关系，并在固定驱动条件下观察到了幽灵寿命分布的标度（scaling）特征。

Conclusion: 本文确立了实现参数性长寿命非定态（parametrically long-lived non-stationary states）的最小条件，为理解非平衡态物理和分岔动力学中的长寿命瞬态行为提供了新的实验平台和理论依据。

Abstract: We report the observation of a long-lived non-stationary state of light in a single-mode optical cavity. The observed state is a ghost of a saddle-node bifurcation which creates a bottleneck in phase space. While such ghosts are known to exist, accessing them is challenging because it requires a mechanism that steers the relaxation pathway away from the true attractor and into the bottleneck where the ghost emerges. Here we identify such a mechanism, namely a nonlinear response with memory. Our experimental system leverages this mechanism, enabling us to observe ghost states with lifetimes exceeding the cavity photon lifetime by more than ten orders of magnitude, even in the presence of strong fluctuations. The ghost manifests as a plateau in the relaxation dynamics of the cavity transmission, reminiscent of prethermalization. We show how the ghost lifetime depends on the memory time and the distance to the bifurcation, and we observe signatures of scaling in the distribution of ghost lifetimes at fixed driving conditions. Our work establishes minimal conditions for realizing parametrically long-lived non-stationary states.

</details>

### [9] [Diagrammatic technique for Vogel's universality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12911)
*D. Khudoteplov,A. Sleptsov*

Main category: math.QA

TL;DR: 本文复兴了Vogel基于图论代数的Λ-代数（Λ-algebra）图解法，展示了该方法能够实现真正普遍（universal）的计算，并通过大量例子进行了验证和讨论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Vogel在1999年预印本中提出了普遍李代数（universal Lie algebra）存在的假说，该假说至今悬而未决；尽管许多李理论（Lie theory）中的量已通过单李（超）代数（simple Lie (super)algebras）的表示论得到普遍描述，但Vogel基于图论代数（diagrammatic algebra）的原始框架在过去二十年间几乎被忽视，亟需重新审视与复兴。

Method: 复兴并采用Vogel提出的Λ-代数（Λ-algebra）图解法（diagrammatic technique），以此作为计算工具进行普遍计算（universal computations），并通过大量示例进行检验和讨论。

Result: 该图解法能够实现真正普遍的计算，并且通过多个例子验证了其有效性和广泛适用性。

Conclusion: Vogel基于Λ-代数的图解法值得重新关注，它提供了一种超越传统表示论（representation theory）的、真正普遍的计算框架。

Abstract: In his 1999 preprint "Universal Lie Algebra", P. Vogel put forward a hypothesis on the existence of a universal Lie algebra. Although this hypothesis remains open, it is known that many quantities in Lie theory admit universal descriptions. Remarkably, almost all such universal formulas have been obtained through the representation theory of simple Lie (super)algebras, whereas Vogel's original framework was based on a more abstract diagrammatic algebra. Nevertheless, the diagrammatic approach has received little attention over the past two decades, since the last contributions by P.Vogel and J.Kneissler.
  In this work, we revive the diagrammatic technique grounded in Vogel's $Λ$-algebra and show that it enables truly universal computations. We examine numerous examples and discuss them.

</details>

### [10] [A solvable model of 3d quantum gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12590)
*Anatoly Dymarsky*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个由 $n$ 份有理 Virasoro TQFT（拓扑量子场论）复制品、并对所有 3d 拓扑求和所定义的 3d 量子引力模型。该理论全息对偶于具有中心荷 $c=n/2$ 和手征代数 $Vir_{1/2}^n$ 的所有 2d CFT（共形场论）的系综。通过求和所有拓扑，模型在大中心荷极限下凝聚为阿贝尔相，展现出半经典 3d 量子引力的诸多特征，包括治愈态密度负性、霍金-佩奇相变、指数抑制的虫洞振幅，并提供了全息编码的玩具模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解 3d 量子引力中全息对偶（holographic duality）的严格实现，特别是当边界系综平均（ensemble average）取代单一对偶 CFT 时的情形。同时，探究求和所有 3d 拓扑结构能否修复半经典引力中出现的负态密度（negative density of states）等病态行为。

Method: 采用 $n$ 份中心荷为 $1/2$ 的有理 Virasoro TQFT 复制品构成 3d 体时空理论，并对所有可能的 3d 拓扑结构求和。计算体时空配分函数（partition function），并将其与边界上具有中心荷 $c=n/2$ 且手征代数包含 $Vir_{1/2}^n$ 的所有 2d CFT 的系综进行匹配。在小 $n$ 情形下验证该全息对偶，并在大中心荷极限下分析体理论向阿贝尔相（Abelian phase）的凝聚行为。

Result: 在大中心荷极限下，对全部 3d 拓扑的求和有效治愈了环面配分函数计算的态密度负性问题。模型展现出霍金-佩奇相变（Hawking-Page transition）和指数抑制的虫洞振幅（exponentially suppressed wormhole amplitude），并作为一个全息编码（holographic code）的玩具示例。小 $n$ 情形下全息对偶关系得到确认。

Conclusion: 该模型为半经典 3d 量子引力提供了一个可精确求解的玩具框架。求和所有拓扑结构是恢复物理上合理的态密度和实现全息编码的关键。这些结果有助于理解体-边界对应中系综平均的起源，并为探索半经典量子引力中的概念性问题提供了启示。

Abstract: We consider a model of 3d quantum gravity defined by $n$ copies of a rational Virasoro TQFT with central charge $1/2$, summed over all 3d topologies. This theory is holographically dual to an ensemble of all 2d CFTs with central charge $c=n/2$ and chiral algebra that includes $Vir_{1/2}^n$. We perform the sum over topologies and evaluate the partition function of the bulk theory. We then confirm the holographic duality by matching it to the boundary ensemble for small $n$. We proceed to consider the limit of a large central charge, in which the bulk theory simplifies and condenses to an Abelian phase. In this regime, the model manifests many features expected in semiclassical 3d quantum gravity. In particular, inclusion of all 3d topologies in the bulk sum cures the negativity of the density of states evaluated by the torus partition function. The model also exhibits a Hawking-Page transition, an exponentially suppressed wormhole amplitude, and provides a toy example of the holographic code. We discuss these aspects in detail and conclude with lessons for semiclassical quantum gravity.

</details>


### [11] [String probes, simple currents, and the no global symmetries conjecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12594)
*Guglielmo Lockhart,Luca Novelli,Yann Proto*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过“忠实弦探针”（faithful string probes）的世界面描述，论证了量子引力理论中中心一形式对称性（center one-form symmetries）必须被破缺或规范化的普遍预期，并展示了该框架如何重现并推广六维和八维中已知的场论与几何障碍，同时揭示了与BPS粒子和更高自旋手征流（higher-spin chiral currents）相关的弦论推广。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解一致量子引力理论（consistent quantum gravity theories）中中心一形式对称性的命运——即它们必须被破缺或规范化（gauged），从而决定规范群（gauge group）的全局形式——并从弦论世界面的角度为这一预期提供新视角。

Method: 引入“忠实弦探针”（faithful string probes）作为区分性的扩展客体，其上规范对称性实现为全纯流代数（holomorphic current algebra）。论证规范化中心一形式对称性的世界面对应物是存在手征单纯流（chiral simple currents）以扩展该流代数，并通过一致性条件重现并推广已知障碍。

Result: 该世界面一致性条件成功重现并推广了六维和八维中场论与几何中关于规范化中心一形式对称性的已知障碍。在杂化弦紧致化（heterotic string compactifications）的多组例子中验证了这一图像，并应用于推断一类无已知F-理论实现（F-theoretic realization）的六维模型的规范群拓扑。此外，澄清了Kim和Vafa关于圆约化所需BPS粒子存在的观察，并发现多个维度模型中存在超出流代数的复合更高自旋手征流。

Conclusion: 忠实弦探针框架为量子引力中中心一形式对称性的规范化提供了统一的世界面理解；复合更高自旋手征流的存在暗示了体时空（bulk）中中心一形式对称性可能存在弦论性的推广。

Abstract: Center one-form symmetries in consistent quantum gravity theories are expected to be either broken or gauged, thereby determining the global form of the gauge group. We shed light on this expectation from the perspective of distinguished extended objects, which we denote by faithful string probes, for which the gauge symmetry is realized as a holomorphic current algebra. We argue that the worldsheet counterpart of gauged center one-form symmetries is the existence of chiral simple currents extending the current algebra. Accordingly, we show that the consistency condition for such extensions reproduce and generalize known field theoretic and geometric obstructions to the gauging of center one-form symmetries in six and eight dimensions. We verify this picture in a number of examples arising from heterotic string compactifications, and apply it to infer the gauge group topology of a recently identified class of six-dimensional models with no known F-theoretic realization. In 6d supergavity, our results also clarify an observation of Kim and Vafa on the existence of BPS particles required for consistency upon circle reduction: these particles arise from worldsheet simple currents whose existence is dictated by the presence of a gauged center one-form symmetry. Intriguingly, in several models across different dimensions we find composite higher-spin chiral currents beyond the current algebra, hinting at a stringy generalization of center one-form symmetries in the bulk.

</details>


### [12] [Butterflies in $\textrm{T}\overline{\textrm{T}}$ deformed anomalous CFT$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12616)
*Debarshi Basu,Mingshuai Xu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有引力反常的 T\overline{T} 形变二维共形场论中的量子混沌及其在拓扑质量引力中的全息对偶描述，发现混沌界仍然饱和，而蝴蝶速度对形变参数和反常呈现非平凡依赖，并识别出一个 Hagedorn 区域，在该区域混沌响应变为复数值，标志着形变理论物理分支的失效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索 T\overline{T} 形变与宇称破坏（parity-violating）动力学之间的相互作用如何影响量子混沌，特别是在存在引力反常（gravitational anomaly）的二维共形场论（CFT）及其全息对偶（holographic dual）——拓扑质量引力（topologically massive gravity）——中的表现。

Method: 采用极点跳跃（pole-skipping）和激波（shock-wave）分析方法，提取李雅普诺夫指数（Lyapunov exponent）和蝴蝶速度（butterfly velocity）。

Result: 混沌界（chaos bound）仍然饱和；蝴蝶速度对形变参数和反常呈现非平凡依赖；发现一个 Hagedorn 区域，在该区域内混沌响应变为复数值，表明形变理论的物理分支失效。

Conclusion: T\overline{T} 形变和引力反常虽然改变了蝴蝶速度，但并未破坏混沌界的饱和；Hagedorn 区域的存在揭示了该形变理论在一定参数范围内的物理不可行性。

Abstract: We study quantum chaos in $\textrm{T}\overline{\textrm{T}}$-deformed two-dimensional conformal field theories with gravitational anomaly and their holographic dual description in topologically massive gravity. Using pole-skipping and shock-wave analysis, we extract the Lyapunov exponent and butterfly velocity and analyze the interplay between irrelevant deformation and parity-violating dynamics. We find that the chaos bound remains saturated, while the butterfly velocity exhibits nontrivial dependence on the deformation parameter and anomaly. We also identify a Hagedorn regime in which the chaotic response becomes complex valued, signaling a breakdown of the physical branch of the deformed theory.

### [13] [Criticality Quenching and Microstructure of Quintessence-AdS Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12632)
*Apurba Tiwari,Randeep Kaur,Javed Khan Bhutto,Thafasalijyas Vayalpurayil,Mohammed Sayeeduddin Habeeb*

TL;DR: 该论文利用Ruppeiner曲率标量研究了巨正则系综中带有精质场（quintessence）的RN-AdS黑洞的热力学几何，揭示了微观相互作用随电势变化从吸引主导向排斥主导转变的特性，并发现相变过程中相互作用强度保持恒定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究精质场（quintessence）对RN-AdS黑洞微观相互作用的影响，特别是其在扩展相空间（extended phase space）中对相变行为和相互作用性质的调制作用。

Method: 采用Ruppeiner曲率标量（Ruppeiner curvature scalar）作为热力学几何分析工具，在巨正则系综（grand canonical ensemble）中计算RN-AdS黑洞的曲率，通过曲率发散标识相变，通过曲率正负判断相互作用类型（负为吸引，正为排斥）。

Result: 低电势时吸引相互作用占主导，高电势时排斥相互作用占主导，这一行为与不带精质场的普通带电黑洞不同。此外，相变过程中相互作用强度保持近似恒定。

Conclusion: 精质场的存在显著改变了RN-AdS黑洞的微观相互作用特性，使其在电势调控下呈现出吸引与排斥之间的转换，且相变过程中相互作用强度的稳定性为理解精质场影响下的黑洞微观属性提供了新的见解。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the thermodynamic geometry of Reissner-Nordstrom Anti-de Sitter (RN-AdS) black holes with quintessence in the grand canonical ensemble. The analysis employs the Ruppeiner curvature scalar to elucidate the microscopic interactions and critical phenomena in the extended phase space. Divergence of the scalar curvature signal phase transitions, while its sign characterizes the nature of the underlying interactions; negative for attractive and positive for repulsive type interactions. The analysis reveals that attractive interactions dominate at low electric potentials, whereas repulsive interactions prevail at higher potentials unlike the usual charged black holes. Finally, the interaction strength is fairly constant during the phase transition, providing a greater understanding of the quintessence influenced microscopic attributes of RN-AdS black holes.

### [14] [Collision Dynamics of False-Vacuum Oscillons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12633)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用Fodor等人的展开方法构造假真空附近的小振幅振荡子（small-amplitude oscillon）解；通过数值模拟研究两类标量场论（正常与反转型四阶自相互作用）中二振荡子碰撞的动力学行为。

Result: 振荡子间的力随间距呈指数衰减，强度受相对相位调制；碰撞呈现反射、穿越及激发振荡子形成；存在类似扭结-反扭结碰撞的共振窗（resonance window）；正常理论中，能量足够时场可越过斯法勒隆（sphaleron）势垒演化为扭结-反扭结对，触发真真空相变。

Conclusion: 振荡子碰撞在适当条件下可引发从假真空到真真空的相变；两种类型理论的振荡子碰撞动力学均表现出共振结构，与已知的拓扑孤子碰撞行为相似。

Abstract: We study the collision dynamics of localized oscillons in two classes of $(1+1)$-dimensional scalar field theories with metastable false vacua, a normal class with a positive quartic self-interaction term and an inverted class with a negative quartic term. We construct small-amplitude oscillon solutions around the false vacuum using the Fodor {\emph{et al.}} expansion, and show that the force between oscillons decays exponentially at large separation, with a strength modulated by their relative phase. Numerical simulations of two-oscillon collisions exhibit reflection, crossing, and formation of excited oscillons. Resonance windows occur, similar to those found in kink-antikink collisions. In the normal theory, if the oscillons have sufficient energy, the field can pass over a sphaleron barrier and evolve into a kink-antikink pair, initiating a phase transition to the true vacuum. We also simulate the collision of oscillons evolved from a slightly perturbed sphaleron.

### [16] [Neural Networks, Dispersion Relations and the Thermal Bootstrap](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13183)
*Vasilis Niarchos,Constantinos Papageorgakis*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文综述了一种不依赖正定性的共形自举（conformal bootstrap）框架，通过色散关系（dispersion relations）和神经网络（neural networks）处理共形关联函数中高维算子乘积展开（OPE）的无穷塔贡献，并应用于$S^1\times \mathbb R^{d-1}$上的标量热两点函数，讨论了非凸优化方案的稳定性及其与CFT关联函数光滑性问题的潜在联系，以广义自由场和4d全息CFT为例进行了数值验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的共形自举方法通常依赖正定性（positivity）条件，这限制了其应用范围。本文旨在发展一种不依赖正定性的替代框架，以处理共形关联函数中无穷多高维OPE（operator product expansion）贡献带来的计算挑战。

Method: 该方法结合色散关系与神经网络来高效处理共形关联函数中高维算子的无穷塔贡献，并采用非凸优化（non-convex optimisation）方案进行数值求解。

Result: 讨论了非凸优化方案的稳定性性质，揭示了其与CFT（conformal field theory）关联函数光滑性问题的潜在关联；以广义自由场（Generalized Free Fields）和4d全息CFT（holographic CFTs）为例，展示了该方法的数值应用效果。

Conclusion: 该不依赖正定性的共形自举框架为处理高维OPE贡献提供了新途径，色散关系与神经网络的结合在数值实现上具有可行性，且与CFT关联函数光滑性问题的讨论相互呼应。

Abstract: We review a framework for the conformal bootstrap that does not rely on positivity and treats the infinite tower of high-dimension OPE contributions to conformal correlators through dispersion relations and neural networks. We apply it to scalar thermal two-point functions on $S^1\times \mathbb R^{d-1}$. We discuss the stability properties of the relevant non-convex optimisation scheme and potential relations to recent discussions of smoothness properties in CFT correlators. We illustrate the numerical application of the method to Generalized Free Fields and 4d holographic CFTs. This is a proceedings contribution to the ``Athens Workshop in Theoretical Physics: 10th Anniversary", held at the National and Kapodistrian University of Athens on December 17-19 2025.

</details>


### [17] [Quantum spacetime and quantum fluctuations in the IKKT model at weak coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13294)
*Harold C. Steinacker*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文系统厘清了IKKT型矩阵模型中涌现结构的概念性问题，指出即使在作用量中没有可调参数，非平凡矩阵真空仍能产生有意义的耦合常数以及两种不确定性能标——非对易性能标与量子涨落能标，并据此区分半经典与深量子两个物理区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在澄清IKKT型矩阵模型（IKKT-type matrix models）中涌现结构（emergent structure）的概念性方面，特别是无参数作用量下物理标度如何自然产生。

Method: 针对两种原型矩阵背景——Moyal-Weyl量子平面（Moyal-Weyl quantum plane）和协变量子时空（covariant quantum spacetime）——估算非对易性尺度与量子涨落尺度，并依据二者的相对重要性划分两个物理区域。

Result: 识别出两种不确定性能标：（a）矩阵背景的非对易性尺度（scale of noncommutativity）；（b）路径积分下矩阵的量子涨落尺度（scale of quantum fluctuations）。在弱耦合区域中，量子涨落可忽略；两个区域分别为半经典区域（semi-classical regime）和深量子区域（deep quantum regime）。

Conclusion: 弱耦合区量子涨落可忽略的结论，为此前关于合适真空中涌现3+1维半经典几何与（量子）引力的工作提供了理论正当性。

Abstract: This paper aims to clarify conceptual aspects of emergent structure in IKKT-type matrix models. Even without any adjustable parameters in the action, non-trivial matrix vacua do acquire a meaningful coupling constant, as well as two distinct uncertainty scales: a) the scale of noncommutativity of the matrix background, and b) the scale of quantum fluctuations of the matrices under the path integral. These scales are estimated for two prototypes of matrix backgrounds, known as Moyal-Weyl quantum plane and covariant quantum spacetime. Their relative importance separates two regimes: 1) the semi-classical regime interpreted in terms of semi-classical noncommutative geometry, and 2) the deep quantum regime usually interpreted in terms of holography. The quantum fluctuations are shown to be negligible in the weak coupling regime. This justifies previous work on the emergent 3+1-dimensional semi-classical geometry and (quantum) gravity in suitable vacua.

### [18] [What does it mean to have a quantum gravitational theory of de Sitter Space?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13490)
*Tom Banks*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文论证，如果德西特空间（de Sitter space）确实由一个有限维量子系统表示，那么半经典考虑结合量子测量理论（quantum measurement theory）的基本原理，会导致任何理论模型都存在歧义性。如果我们的宇宙渐近到该德西特态，并且作为有限系统的模型可以被嵌入一系列模型中，最终收敛到渐近平坦空间中唯一超弦模型（superstring model）的非微扰完备化，则可能获得非常精确的宇宙数学模型。然而，局域探测器（local detectors）在宇宙中可能进行的最全面的实验，也无法测量该系统中超过极小一部分的量子比特（q-bits）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究德西特空间的有限量子系统表示所导致的理论歧义性问题，并探索在超弦理论框架下构建精确宇宙模型的可能性，同时指出局域观测的固有局限性。

Method: 采用半经典分析（semi-classical considerations）与量子测量理论的基本原理相结合的方式，对德西特空间的有限维量子系统表示进行理论论证，并讨论将有限系统模型嵌入收敛于渐近平坦空间中唯一超弦模型的序列。

Result: 德西特空间的有限维量子系统表示导致任何理论模型都存在固有歧义性；即使存在收敛到唯一超弦模型的模型序列，局域探测器最多也只能测量系统中极小部分的量子比特。

Conclusion: 在德西特宇宙的有限量子系统框架下，理论模型的歧义性是不可避免的，且局域实验的观测能力存在根本性的限制。

Abstract: We argue that if de Sitter space is indeed represented by a finite dimensional quantum system, then semi-classical considerations, combined with the fundamental principles of quantum measurement theory, imply that any theoretical model of it is ambiguous. If our own universe asymptotes to such a de Sitter state, and if a model of it as a finite system can be embedded in a sequence of models that converges to a non-perturbative completion of a unique superstring model in asymptotically flat space, then one might be able to find a very precise mathematical model of our universe. However, even the most comprehensive experiments possible to local detectors in the universe cannot measure more than a tiny fraction of the total number of q-bits in the system.

</details>


### [19] [Semiclassical algebraic reconstruction for type III algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13576)
*Haocheng Zhong*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过引入交叉积代数（crossed product algebras）和半经典近似（semiclassical approximations），解决了代数重建定理（algebraic reconstruction theorem）中未解决的类型III（type III）情形，并建立了包含代数Ryu-Takayanagi（RT）公式的完整代数描述框架，为全息对偶（holographic duality）中的体-边界对应（bulk-boundary correspondence）提供了内在的代数基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 代数重建定理中关于类型III情形的未解问题构成了本文的核心研究动机。作者旨在通过交叉积代数与半经典方法，给出代数重建定理的完整描述，从而为全息对偶中的体-边界对应提供严密的代数框架。

Method: 首先推导了交叉积代数中相对熵（relative entropy）可分解为原始代数贡献与观测者波函数（observer wavefunctions）贡献之和。进而针对“体（bulk）”和“边界（boundary）”两种类型III因子（type III factors），构造了“全息（holographic）”交叉积代数，并在此基础上将代数重建定理扩展至包含半经典近似的代数Ryu-Takayanagi（RT）公式。

Result: 成功将代数重建定理推广至类型III情形，获得了包含代数RT公式的半经典完整描述，为全息对偶中的体-边界对应提供了内在的代数表述框架。

Conclusion: 基于交叉积代数的半经典方法，能够为类型III情形下的代数重建定理提供完整的代数描述，进而建立起全息对偶中体-边界对应的代数版本的内在框架。

Abstract: In this work, we address the unresolved type III cases of the algebraic reconstruction theorem by integrating crossed product algebras and semiclassical approximations. We first derive that the relative entropy in crossed product algebras factorizes into contributions from the original algebra and observer wavefunctions. By constructing ``holographic'' crossed product algebras for ``bulk'' and ``boundary'' type III factors, we extend the algebraic reconstruction theorem to include the algebraic Ryu-Takayanagi (RT) formula semiclassically, which provides a complete algebraic description of the reconstruction theorem, as an intrinsic framework for the algebraic version of bulk-boundary correspondences in holographic duality.

</details>


### [20] [Before the Bang: Wormholes at the Dawn of the Universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13777)
*Panos Betzios,Paul Ghiringhelli,Ioannis D. Gialamas,Olga Papadoulaki*

TL;DR: 本文讨论了欧几里得虫洞（Euclidean wormholes）作为宇宙初始量子态候选贡献的最新进展，通过与哈特尔-霍金无边界提议（Hartle-Hawking no-boundary proposal）的对比，展示了虫洞方案在扩大半经典初始条件景观、符合全息原理（Holographic principle）以及解决无边界提议中存在问题方面的优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索宇宙初始量子态的合理候选方案，并改进哈特尔-霍金无边界提议中存在的缺陷。

Method: 通过比较欧几里得虫洞与哈特尔-霍金无边界提议，分析虫洞方案在保留欧几里得鞍点（Euclidean-saddles）对宇宙学波函数（cosmological wavefunctions）编码作用的同时，如何扩展物理相关的正则鞍点（regular saddles）类别。

Result: 虫洞方案能够扩大半经典初始条件景观（semiclassical initial-condition landscape），丰富物理内涵，符合全息原理的预期，从而在紫外完备的量子引力理论（UV complete theories of quantum gravity）中与早期宇宙模型构建日益相关。

Conclusion: 欧几里得虫洞为宇宙初始量子态提供了物理上更丰富的候选贡献，能够解决无边界提议中的若干问题，并在全息量子引力框架下具有重要的早期宇宙模型构建意义。

Abstract: This essay discusses recent progress on Euclidean wormholes as candidate contributions to the Universe's initial quantum state. The comparison with the Hartle-Hawking no-boundary proposal highlights both a conceptual affinity and genuine advance: wormholes retain the relevance of Euclidean-saddles as encoders of properties of cosmological wavefunctions, while they broaden the class of regular saddles that are physically relevant for inflating universes and are capable of resolving issues that plague the no-boundary proposal. The principal achievement of the wormhole program is to enlarge the semiclassical initial-condition land-scape in a way that is physically rich, conforms with Holographic expectations and as such becomes increasingly relevant for early-universe model building, within UV complete theories of quantum gravity.

</details>


### [21] [Universal Confining Strings: From Compact QED to the Hadron Spectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13791)
*M. C. Diamantini,F. Quevedo,C. A. Trugenberger,L. Zapata*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明，在（3+1）维中，带拓扑θ项的紧致QED（compact QED）在处于dyon凝聚相时，可由一个带有红外Brazovskii-Lifshitz强耦合不动点的弦理论描述。该“自由弦”具有有限厚度，包含有质量的world-sheet共振态，其禁闭势能推广了Arvis势，且对重夸克偶素质量比和Regge轨迹截距的计算与实验或理论预期吻合，支持了Polyakov关于红外禁闭规范理论普适性的猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究夸克禁闭（quark confinement）在弦或通量管（flux tube）描述下的微观机制，验证Polyakov关于红外（IR）禁闭规范理论普适性的长期猜想。

Method: 基于带拓扑θ项的紧致QED（compact QED with a topological θ-term）在dyon凝聚相（dyon condensation phase）中的有效理论，推导出一个有质量的两形式场（two-form field）$B_{μν}$，并由此构造出一个具有IR Brazovskii-Lifshitz不动点的弦理论，计算其禁闭势能及Regge轨迹截距。

Result: 该弦理论在（3+1）维中实现了一个量子自洽的“自由弦”，具有有限厚度而非依赖于额外维度；禁闭势能给出推广的Arvis势 $V(L) = aL \sqrt{1 - c/L^2}$，其中参数$a(L), c(L)$是跑动的（running）；最重夸克偶素（quarkonium）的质量差比值与实验的吻合度达到2.5%；弦的厚度倾向于使Regge轨迹截距（intercept）增大，偏离Nambu-Goto值$α_0 = 1/12$。

Conclusion: 红外Brazovskii-Lifshitz弦理论能够很好地描述禁闭现象，并与实验数据定量吻合，从而有力支持了Polyakov关于禁闭规范理论在红外普适性的猜想。

Abstract: We investigate the description of quark confinement in terms of confining strings or flux tubes. We show that compact QED with a topological $θ$-term, in the dyon condensation phase, is described by a massive two-form field $B_{μν}$ that gives rise to a string theory with an IR Brazovskii-Lifshitz fixed point at strong coupling. This corresponds to a quantum consistent "free string" in (3+1) dimensions, representing the dual of asymptotic freedom in the UV. Contrary to critical strings, which correspond to trivial Gaussian fixed points, this string is stabilized by a finite thickness, determined by the mass of the $B_{μν}$ field, instead of living in a higher-dimensional space. It correspondingly contains a massive world-sheet resonance, in addition to the Nambu-Goto phonons, that improves fitting with data. We compute the confining potential and show that it reproduces a generalized Arvis potential $V(L) = aL \sqrt{1 - c/L^2}$ with running parameters $a(L), c(L)$. We compute the mass difference ratios for the heaviest quarkonium and find 2.5 percent agreement with experiment already at the infrared fixed point. We also compute the intercept of Regge trajectories and find that the thickness of Brazovskii-Lifshitz strings tends to increase it from the Nambu-Goto value $α_0 = 1/12$. Overall, our findings strongly support Polyakov's longstanding conjecture on universality of confining gauge theories in the IR.

</details>


### [22] [An algebra of proper observables at null infinity: Dirac brackets, Memory and Goldstone probes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13804)
*Rodrigo Andrade e Silva,Simone Speziale*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文对零无穷远（null infinity）辐射引力模态相空间上的狄拉克括号（Dirac brackets）进行了严格评估，自然纳入了记忆效应（memory effects）。研究识别了恰当可观测量（proper observables）的代数，揭示了超平移荷（supertranslation charges）对剪切（shear）的正确变换作用，论证了传统“戈德斯通模（Goldstone mode）”并非恰当可观测量但可由无穷族“戈德斯通探针（Goldstone probes）”测量，并给出了含非局域修正的分布性狄拉克括号公式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文献对零无穷远相空间中引力记忆效应的可观测量定义尚不严格，传统“戈德斯通模”的可观测性存在歧义，且基于不同记忆态构造可分希尔伯特空间（separable Hilbert space）的尝试屡屡失败，亟需对相空间上的狄拉克括号结构和恰当可观测量进行严格分析。

Method: 研究基于Ashtekar-Streubel相空间（Ashtekar-Streubel phase space），采用时间边界条件：news消失且剪切为纯电性（purely electric）。通过考虑相空间的无穷维性，识别与光滑辛流（smooth symplectic flows）相关联的恰当可观测量代数；随后推导剪切与news的分布性狄拉克括号，并分析超平移荷的生成作用和戈德斯通探针的构造限制。

Result: 结果表明：超平移荷正确生成剪切上的变换；传统“戈德斯通模”不是恰当可观测量，但存在无穷族“戈德斯通探针”可测量该模式；仅由剪切或仅由news均无法构造戈德斯通探针；局部剪切与news之间的分布性狄拉克括号含非局域修正。

Conclusion: 这些发现为无法基于不同记忆态构造可分希尔伯特空间提供了解释，并为零无穷远上引力记忆效应的严格相空间量子化（canonical quantization）奠定了形式基础。

Abstract: We develop a rigorous evaluation of Dirac brackets for classical observables on the phase space of radiative gravitational modes at null infinity that naturally incorporates memory effects. Considering the Ashtekar-Streubel phase space, with boundary conditions in time given by vanishing {\it news} and purely electric {\it shear}, and taking into account the infinite dimensionality of the phase space, we identify the algebra of proper observables (understood as functions on phase space that can be associated with smooth symplectic flows). We show that the action of supertranslation charges generate the correct transformations on the shear. We also show that the conventional definition of the ``Goldstone mode'' adopted in the literature cannot be associated with a proper observable, but nevertheless there exists an infinite family of proper observables, which we call {\it Goldstone probes}, that are capable of measuring the Goldstone mode. We notice that there are no Goldstone probes constructed only out of the shear {\it or} the news, providing a possible explanation for why attempts to construct a (separable) Hilbert space with different memory states have failed so far. Finally, we derive formulas for distributional Dirac brackets between local shear and news, and show that they contain non-local corrections.

</details>


### [23] ["Metric-affine-like" generalization of YM (mal-YM): detailed classical consideration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13809)
*Władysław Wachowski*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文对之前提出的“度规-仿射类”杨-米尔斯理论（mal-YM）进行了经典层面的详细分析，该理论通过放宽纤维上联络与埃尔米特形式的相容性条件，引入新场并实现自发对称性破缺 \(GL(n,\mathbb{C}) \to U(n)\)，在质量趋于无穷大时恢复标准杨-米尔斯理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机是推广标准杨-米尔斯理论（Yang-Mills theory）：不再要求纤维中的联络与埃尔米特形式（Hermitian form）相容，从而引入更丰富的场结构，探讨一种“度规-仿射类”（metric-affine-like）的推广模型（mal-YM）。

Method: 通过引入新的非平凡相互作用场 \(\boldsymbol{B}_a\)、\(\boldsymbol{h}\)、\(\boldsymbol{G}_{ab}\)、\(\boldsymbol{N}_a\)，构建了一个非阿贝尔推广的Stückelberg理论；利用自发对称性破缺机制（\(GL(n,\mathbb{C}) \to U(n)\)）使这些新场获得质量，并在质量极限 \(M\to\infty\) 下恢复标准YM理论；在经典层面详细分析了场变换、规范对称性（gauge symmetry）、作用量、运动方程、Noether恒等式（Noether identities）及规范固定（gauge fixing）等问题。

Result: 成功构建了mal-YM模型的经典理论框架，揭示了新场与标准YM势 \(\boldsymbol{A}_a\) 及场强张量 \(\boldsymbol{F}_{ab}\) 之间的相互作用结构，明确了自发对称性破缺的数学形式与物理后果。

Conclusion: 该模型为YM理论提供了一种具有几何动机的推广，新场在自发破缺后成为有质量场，且在大质量极限下可回归标准YM理论，为探索非阿贝尔规范理论的新扩展方向提供了经典层面的理论基础。

Abstract: We consider the ``metric-affine-like'' generalization of the Yang-Mills theory (mal-YM) which we first proposed earlier. In this model, the connection is no longer assumed to be compatible with the Hermitian form in the fibers. As a consequence, along with the usual YM potential $\boldsymbol{A}_a$ and the field strength tensor $\boldsymbol{F}_{ab}$, it contains non-trivially interacting fields $\boldsymbol{B}_a$, $\boldsymbol{h}$, and $\boldsymbol{G}_{ab}$, $\boldsymbol{N}_a$, forming a non-Abelian generalization of Stückelberg theory. Due to the spontaneous symmetry breaking $GL(n,\mathbb{C}) \to U(n)$, these new fields can be made massive and the limit $M\to\infty$ restores the standard YM theory. We perform a detailed analysis of this theory on the classical level. We discuss in detail geometric motivation for the model, field transformations, gauge symmetry and its spontaneous breaking, action, equations of motion, Noether identities, gauge fixing, and other issues.

</details>

### [24] [Space-Charge Effects in Silicon Reconfigurable Nonlinear-Processing Units](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13477)
*Jonas Kareem,Lorenzo Cassola,Reinier J. C. Cool,Janiek I. van Slooten,Peter A. Bobbert,Wilfred G. van der Wiel*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文通过温度与长度依赖的电流-电压测量和漂移-扩散模拟，揭示了硅基可重构非线性处理单元（RNPU）中室温非线性的物理起源：空间电荷主导的输运机制，其中界面陷阱态抑制平衡载流子密度，而功能非线性源于注入载流子与固定电离掺杂剂之间的电压依赖性竞争。实验结果与模拟的一致性表明，注入载流子与固定电荷的空间分布决定了内部电场分布和器件响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 硅基可重构非线性处理单元（RNPU）虽已具备可扩展性和技术相关性，但其室温非线性的物理起源仍未得到充分理解，这阻碍了器件的可重复设计与CMOS兼容实现。

Method: 对物理器件进行温度和长度依赖的电流-电压（I-V）测量，并辅以漂移-扩散（drift-diffusion）模拟分析电荷输运行为。

Result: 输运由空间电荷（space charge）主导；界面陷阱态强烈抑制平衡载流子密度；功能非线性源于注入载流子与固定电离掺杂剂之间的电压依赖性竞争；非平衡输运呈现从欧姆区（Ohmic regime）到强非线性区，最终到速度饱和空间电荷限制电流（velocity-saturation space-charge-limited current）区的转变；相反极性背景掺杂可控制非线性强度，使其超越经典Mott-Gurney定律的二次依赖关系。

Conclusion: 建立了硅基RNPU无需无序或跳跃输运（hopping transport）的物理框架，为可重复、可扩展且与CMOS兼容的非线性计算硬件实现提供了设计指南。

Abstract: Reconfigurable nonlinear-processing units (RNPUs) are multi-terminal electronic devices that act as computational primitives, exploiting intrinsic nonlinear charge transport combined with electrostatic tunability. Silicon-based realizations provide a scalable and technologically relevant platform, yet the physical origin of their room-temperature nonlinearity has remained insufficiently understood. Here, we investigate charge transport using temperature- and length-dependent current-voltage measurements on physical devices, complemented by drift-diffusion simulations, and show that transport is governed by space charge. Interface trap states strongly suppress the equilibrium carrier density, while the functional nonlinearity arises from the voltage-dependent competition between injected mobile carriers and fixed ionized background dopants. The resulting non-equilibrium transport exhibits a transition from an Ohmic regime to a strongly nonlinear regime, and ultimately to a velocity-saturation space-charge-limited current regime, as evidenced by the observed voltage and length scaling. We further show that background doping of opposite polarity to the injected carriers controls the onset and strength of the nonlinearity, leading to behavior exceeding the quadratic dependence of the classical Mott-Gurney law. Agreement between experiment and simulation supports that the spatial distribution of injected carriers and fixed charge governs the internal electric-field profile and device response. These results establish a physical framework for silicon-based RNPUs without requiring disorder or hopping transport, and provide design guidelines for reproducible, scalable, and CMOS-compatible implementations of nonlinear computing hardware.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.dis-nn'></div>

# cond-mat.dis-nn [[Back]](#toc)

### [25] [The critical slowing down in diffusion models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12597)
*Luca Maria Del Bono,Giulio Biroli,Patrick Charbonneau,Marylou Gabrié*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本论文在统计场论$O(n)$模型的大$n$极限下，解析分析了扩散模型（diffusion models）的采样行为。研究表明，单层网络的得分模型（score model）训练存在临界慢化（critical slowing down）现象，而引入双层架构与物理局域性（physical locality）可将训练时间从系统尺寸的二次依赖降为对数依赖，且无需增加网络参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于机器学习的生成模型在实践中取得了重大进展，但其行为机制尚不清晰，缺乏对成功条件与失败原因的理论控制。本文旨在为扩散模型提供理论洞见，理解其在统计物理采样中的行为与瓶颈。

Method: 将扩散模型应用于统计场论$O(n)$模型的高斯极限（$n \to \infty$），在该解析可处理的设定中，训练与精确解匹配的单层网络得分模型，并进一步引入双层网络架构和局部得分近似（local score approximation）进行分析。

Result: 单层网络训练表现出临界慢化现象，该慢化同样影响生成过程。采用双层架构后，训练时间的规模依赖性从二次降至对数；通过局部得分近似，这一加速可在不增加神经网络参数的情况下实现。

Conclusion: 扩散模型通过适当的架构设计能够克服临界慢化，本文建立了一个可控的理论框架，用于理解和改进统计物理学及其他领域中的学习型采样方法。

Abstract: Computational sampling has been central to the sciences since the mid-20th century. While machine-learning-based approaches have recently enabled major advances, their behavior remains poorly understood, with limited theoretical control over when and why they succeed. Here we provide such insight for diffusion models-a class of generative schemes highly effective in practice-by analyzing their application to the $O(n)$ model of statistical field theory in the Gaussian limit $n \to \infty$. In this analytically tractable setting, we show that training a score model with a one-layer network architecture matching the exact solution exhibits a form of critical slowing down in parameter learning. This slowing down also impacts the generation process, indicating that the well-known difficulties of sampling near criticality persist even for learned generative models. To overcome this bottleneck, we demonstrate the power of combining architectural depth with physical locality. We find that using a two-layer architecture drastically reduces the critical slowing down, with the training time scaling logarithmically rather than quadratically with system size. By introducing a local score approximation we show that this acceleration in training time can be achieved without increasing the number of neural network parameters. Taken together, these results demonstrate that diffusion models can overcome the critical slowing down through appropriate architectural design, and establish a controlled framework for understanding and improving learned sampling methods in statistical physics and beyond.

</details>


### [26] [Do Hopfield Networks Dream of Stored Patterns? A Statistical-Mechanical Theory of Dreaming in Multidirectional Associative Memories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13721)
*Adriano Barra,Fabrizio Durante,Andrea Ladiana,Michela Marra Solazzo*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出梦境L方向联想记忆模型（DLAM），一种多层Hebbian架构，将离线梦境（off-line dreaming）与监督异联想耦合（supervised heteroassociative coupling）统一于单个能量函数中。通过Guerra插值方案推导出副本对称自由能及其自洽方程，揭示了信号、层内梦境噪声与层间噪声的分解机制。梦境通过差异化衰减经验相关矩阵的高本征值干扰模式来提升检索性能，并与层间耦合产生协同效应，打开了任一单独机制无法触及的检索区域。在模式分离任务中，网络可将混合输入拆分为各层独立恢复的模态特异性模式。相图揭示了数据-计算权衡：离线整合可替代额外训练数据。该工作将标准Hopfield模型拓展为能够处理复杂任务的能量基模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将离线梦境机制与监督异联想耦合统一于单个能量函数框架内，在能量基模型（energy-based models, EBMs）的范式下，探索二者在多层次联想记忆架构中的相互作用及其对检索性能与模式分离能力的提升。

Method: 提出Dreaming L-directional Associative Memory (DLAM)多层Hebbian架构，利用Guerra插值方案推导副本对称自由能（replica-symmetric free energy），建立序参量的自洽方程（self-consistency equations），并通过蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）验证L=3时的理论预测。

Result: 梦境通过差异化衰减经验相关矩阵的高本征值干扰模式来抑制跨模式串扰（inter-pattern crosstalk）并保留信号；梦境与层间耦合具有协同效应，能打开任一机制单独无法达到的检索区域；在(ρ,t)相平面中，相图揭示了数据-计算权衡（data-computation trade-off），即离线整合可替代额外训练数据。

Conclusion: 在标准Hopfield模型中引入异联想性与梦境机制，使得能量基模型能够完成超越经典模式识别的复杂任务，有助于建立现代神经信息处理理论。

Abstract: We introduce the Dreaming $L$-directional Associative Memory (DLAM), a multi-layer Hebbian architecture in which off-line dreaming and supervised heteroassociative coupling coexist within a single energy function, placing our approach within the framework of energy-based models (EBMs). The replica-symmetric free energy, derived via the Guerra interpolation scheme, yields self-consistency equations governing the order parameters across the control-parameter space. The effective local field decomposes into signal, intra-layer dreaming noise, and inter-layer noise. Dreaming improves retrieval by differentially attenuating high-eigenvalue interference modes of the empirical correlation matrix, suppressing inter-pattern crosstalk while preserving the signal. Dreaming and inter-layer coupling prove synergistic, opening retrieval regions unreachable by either mechanism alone, as confirmed by Monte Carlo simulations for $L=3$. Their interplay is most pronounced on pattern disentanglement: given a mixture state as input, the network splits the constituent patterns one-per-layer, recovering each modality-specific pattern from a common cue that simultaneously blends noisy evidence from all sensory channels. Phase diagrams are planar projections of the hyperspace $(α,β,ρ,t)$-where $α$ is the storage load, $β$ the fast-noise inverse temperature, $ρ$ the dataset entropy, and $t$ the sleeping time. In the $(ρ,t)$-plane, the diagrams reveal a data-computation trade-off: off-line consolidation substitutes for additional training data, extending to heteroassociative architectures a phenomenon previously established for autoassociative networks. Enriching the standard Hopfield model with heteroassociativity and dreaming gives rise to EBMs capable of complex tasks beyond classical pattern recognition, contributing to a modern theory of neural information processing.

</details>

### [27] [Exclusive dimuon production and coherent charmonium photoproduction at forward rapidity in ultra-peripheral Pb$-$Pb collisions at $\mathbf{\sqrt{s_{\rm NN}}=5.36}$ TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13569)
*ALICE Collaboration*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: 本文利用ALICE探测器在LHC采集的Pb-Pb超外围碰撞数据（√sNN=5.36 TeV，积分亮度1170 μb⁻¹），测量了前向快度区（-4 < y < -2.5）相干J/ψ和ψ(2S)光生过程以及双μ子产生的快度与质量微分截面，揭示了核遮蔽效应（nuclear shadowing）的重要作用以及光子通量（photon flux）建模对撞击参数近核半径区域的敏感性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在超外围重离子碰撞中，通过测量相干矢量介子光生过程和双轻子产生，可以研究原子核内的胶子分布及核遮蔽效应等非微扰量子色动力学（QCD）现象。本文旨在利用高统计量数据，在LHC能量下对J/ψ和ψ(2S)光生以及双μ子产生进行精确的微分测量，以检验现有理论模型。

Method: 基于ALICE探测器在2023年记录的Pb-Pb超外围碰撞数据（质心系能量√sNN=5.36 TeV，积分亮度1170±50 μb⁻¹），在前向快度区间-4 < y < -2.5进行测量。对J/ψ和ψ(2S)采用快度微分分析，对双μ子产生则进行快度与质量双重微分分析。

Result: J/ψ和ψ(2S)测量结果显示了核遮蔽效应的显著作用：在快度y≈-3处（对应Bjorken-x典型值约10⁻²），测得的夸克偶素（quarkonium）截面与冲激近似（impulse approximation）预测之比的平方根，J/ψ约为0.76，ψ(2S)约为0.71。双μ子产生的结果则突出了在撞击参数（impact parameter）接近核半径时，对光子通量精确建模的敏感性。

Conclusion: 相干J/ψ和ψ(2S)光生截面相对于冲激近似的显著压低，定量揭示了在前向快度区存在较强的核遮蔽效应。双μ子微分测量表明，要准确描述实验数据，光生过程的理论模型需要精细处理核周边区域的光子通量分布。

Abstract: This Paper presents rapidity-differential measurements of coherent J/$ψ$ and $ψ({\rm 2S})$ photoproduction, as well as rapidity- and mass-differential measurements of exclusive dimuon production, in the forward rapidity region $-4 < y < -2.5$ in ultra-peripheral Pb$-$Pb collisions at $\sqrt{s_{\rm NN}}=5.36$ TeV using data recorded by the ALICE detector at the LHC in 2023, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of $\mathcal{L} = 1170 \pm 50~μ{\rm b}^{-1}$. The J/$ψ$ and $ψ({\rm 2S})$ results reveal the significant role of nuclear shadowing effects. The square root of the ratio of the measured quarkonium cross section to the impulse approximation prediction is about 0.76 for J/$ψ$ and 0.71 for $ψ({\rm 2S})$, at $y \approx -3$, corresponding to typical Bjorken-$x$ values of $10^{-2}$. The exclusive dimuon results highlight the sensitivity of such measurements to precise modeling of the photon flux, particularly at impact parameters near the nuclear radius.

### [28] [In-situ tunable superconducting diode: towards field-free operation with infinite nonreciprocity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13254)
*Razmik A. Hovhannisyan,Taras Golod,Amirreza Lotfian,Vladimir M. Krasnov*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究基于四端子铌平面约瑟夫森结（four-terminal niobium planar Josephson junction）的超导二极管，其无需外加磁场即可实现宽范围原位可调谐性和极性可重构性，展示了作为高斯神经元（Gauss neuron）和无限非互易性（infinite nonreciprocity）无阈值交流整流等新功能，有望用于未来数字与神经形态计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高效、可扩展且无需磁场的超导二极管（superconducting diode）对于未来超导电子学至关重要，但现有方案缺乏宽范围原位可调谐性（in-situ tunability），难以实现优化和类晶体管操作。

Method: 采用四端子铌平面约瑟夫森结（four-terminal niobium planar Josephson junction）结构，通过多端子构型消除对外加磁场的依赖，实现可重构极性（reconfigurable polarity）和宽范围原位调谐。

Result: 实验演示了该二极管可作为高斯神经元（Gauss neuron）运行，基于回滞超导（reentrant superconductivity）机制；通过调谐结参数，获得了在实验分辨率内有效的无限非互易性（infinite nonreciprocity），从而实现无阈值交流整流（threshold-free ac-current rectification）。

Conclusion: 这种技术简单、可重构且广泛可调谐的超导二极管可能对未来的数字计算与神经形态计算（neuromorphic computing）起到关键作用。

Abstract: Efficient, scalable, and magnetic-field-free superconducting diodes are essential for future superconducting electronics; yet, despite significant efforts, such practical devices remain unrealized. The main challenge lies in achieving broad-range in-situ tunability, both for optimization and for achieving transistor-like operation. Here, we study diodes based on four-terminal niobium planar Josephson junctions. We show that the multiterminal structure eliminates the need for an external magnetic field and enables essentially unrestricted in-situ tunability, along with reconfigurability of the diode polarity, leading to new functionality. For example, we demonstrate that such diodes can operate as Gauss neurons via reentrant superconductivity. By deliberately tuning the junction parameters, we obtain effectively infinite nonreciprocity (within experimental resolution) leading to threshold-free ac-current rectification. Such technologically simple, reconfigurable, and broadly tunable diodes could be instrumental for future digital and neuromorphic computing.

### [29] [A hyperbolic cell cycle law for early embryonic developmental timing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13234)
*Adrián Aguirre-Tamaral,Johanna Royer,Magdalena Schindler-Johnson,Jun-Ru Lee,Daniel R. Amor,Nicoletta I. Petridou,Bernat Corominas-Murtra*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 该研究揭示，后生动物早期胚胎细胞分裂速度普遍减缓的现象，源于细胞分裂在生物化学时间尺度而非时钟时间尺度上进行。有限母体资源消耗与类米氏动力学耦合，导致细胞周期长度呈双曲增长并趋近数学奇点（发育停滞）。跨门类实验数据均塌缩至同一曲线，定量预测了包括原肠胚形成时机在内的关键发育特征。资源可用性与消耗速率的实验调控验证了模型，并表明生化时间尺度的改变是早期发育异时性的来源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 后生动物（metazoans）的早期胚胎尽管在发育速度和分子机制上差异巨大，但其细胞分裂速度却表现出惊人的保守性减缓现象，这一跨物种共同行为的潜在物理或生化机制尚不明确。

Method: 该研究提出，早期发育遵循生物化学时间尺度（biochemical timescale）而非时钟时间尺度（chronological timescale），通过将有限母体资源（maternal resource）消耗与类米氏动力学（Michaelis-Menten-like kinetics）耦合，推导出细胞周期长度（Cell Cycle Length, CCL）呈双曲增长并趋近数学奇点的模型。跨刺胞动物、线虫、节肢动物、软体动物、棘皮动物、被囊动物、两栖动物和鱼类等门类的胚胎数据进行模型拟合与验证，并结合实验调控资源可用性与消耗速率进行检验。

Result: 多种后生动物的实验数据均塌缩至同一理论曲线，模型不仅定量捕捉了细胞周期长度（CCL）的普适动力学行为，还准确预测了细胞数量随时间演化、细胞周期长度对细胞尺寸的依赖性，以及原肠胚形成（gastrulation）时机恰位于预测的奇点处。实验调控资源可用性与消耗速率进一步验证了模型，并表明资源消耗的生化时间尺度改变是早期发育异时性（heterochrony）的来源。

Conclusion: 资源消耗速率是驱动跨物种早期胚胎发生（embryogenesis）中发育时序（developmental timing）的基本机制。该工作为后生动物早期发育中细胞分裂速度的保守性减缓提供了统一的物理解释。

Abstract: Across metazoans, early embryos exhibit a strikingly conserved slowing down of their cell duplication speed, despite widely varying developmental paces and underlying molecular mechanisms. Here we show that this common behavior arises because early development unfolds along a biochemical rather than a chronological timescale, resulting from the coupling of finite maternal resource consumption to the Michaelis-Menten-like kinetics governing the rates of the biochemical reactions involved in cell duplication. This leads to a hyperbolic growth of the Cell Cycle Length (CCL), approaching a mathematical singularity, which would correspond to developmental arrest. Data from a wide range of organisms -- cnidarians, nematodes, arthropods, molluscs, echinoderms, tunicates, amphibians, and fish -- collapse on a single curve, quantitatively capturing not only a universal CCL dynamical behaviour, but also key hallmarks of early metazoan development, including cell-number temporal evolution, the dependency of CCL on cell size, and, remarkably, gastrulation timing at the predicted singularity. Crucially, experimental modulation of resource availability and consumption rates validate the model and further demonstrate that a source of heterochrony in early development is an altered biochemical timescale of resource depletion. Overall, this work reveals resource consumption rates as a fundamental mechanism driving developmental timing in early embryogenesis across species.

</details>

### [30] [Radioactive Molecules as Laboratories of Fundamental Physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12767)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 放射性分子能够结合核性质带来的增强效应与分子结构提供的高灵敏度和控制能力，从而在超越标准模型的新物理搜索中提供与高能粒子对撞机能标互补的探测途径。

Method: 综述当前放射性分子的产生与控制技术进展，以及新兴的实验工具和理论方法（theoretical techniques）如何推动该交叉学科的快速发展。

Result: 该领域正处于快速推进阶段，在放射性分子的制备、操控以及相关实验与理论工具开发方面均取得了显著进展。

Conclusion: 放射性分子研究作为核物理、原子与分子物理及粒子物理交叉的前沿领域，在新物理探索中展现出巨大潜力，未来发展前景广阔。

Abstract: Radioactive molecules provide a powerful new platform in the search for new physics at energy scales complementary to high-energy particle colliders. By combining enhancements from nuclear properties with the sensitivity and control offered by molecular structure, experiments with radioactive molecules offer great reach in the search for new physics beyond the Standard Model. Rapid progress in this field is being driven by advances in the production and control of radioactive molecules, alongside the development of new experimental tools and theoretical techniques. In this Perspective, we discuss the current status and future prospects of this rapidly developing, interdisciplinary field at the intersection of nuclear physics, atomic and molecular physics, and particle physics.

### [31] [Jets from Scratch: A 3D Dynamo Origin of Long Gamma-Ray Burst Jets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12931)
*Ho-Sang Chan,Ore Gottlieb,Jonatan Jacquemin-Ide,Matteo Cantiello,Mathieu Renzo*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文通过首次三维广义相对论磁流体动力学（general-relativistic magnetohydrodynamic, GRMHD）坍缩星（collapsar）模拟，证明吸积盘中的发电机机制（dynamo）可以从初始环向磁场（toroidal magnetic field）产生大尺度极向磁场（poloidal magnetic field），进而驱动相对论性喷流（relativistic jet），其功率与长伽马射线暴（LGRB）相当。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 坍缩星驱动相对论性喷流所需的大尺度极向磁场的起源尚不确定；极向场可能由前超新星核（PNS）坍缩继承，但效率不明，因此需要一种原位（in situ）机制从恒星较差转动（differential rotation）产生的优势环向磁场中生成极向场。

Method: 采用首次三维广义相对论磁流体动力学（GRMHD）模拟，初始环向磁场分布紧密遵循坍缩前恒星模型；模拟追踪吸积盘中环向场在动力学上变得重要后如何触发发电机（dynamo），并产生相干极向磁环。

Result: 极向磁环在约100引力半径（gravitational radii）处出现，沿偏离盘面（disk midplane）的路径向内输运，最终贯穿黑洞（BH）并发射高度可变、摆动的相对论性喷流，功率持续高于10^50 erg/s，与长伽马射线暴（LGRB）相当；还发现随机发电机（stochastic dynamo）驱动的磁通反转（magnetic-flux inversions）导致条纹喷流（striped jets）形成。

Conclusion: 吸积盘发电机机制为多种前身星模型下的坍缩星喷流产生提供了稳健路径，表明该机制在广泛的前身星范围内均有效。

Abstract: The origin of the large-scale poloidal magnetic field required to power relativistic jets in collapsars remains uncertain. While such a field may be inherited during PNS collapse, the efficiency of this process is unclear, motivating an in situ mechanism to generate poloidal fields out of the predominantly toroidal fields produced by stellar differential rotation. We present the first 3D general-relativistic magnetohydrodynamic collapsar simulations initialized with toroidal magnetic field profiles that closely follows those of pre-collapse stellar models. As the toroidal field in the disk becomes dynamically important, it seeds the dynamo, producing coherent poloidal magnetic loops that appear at $\sim \mathcal{O}(100)$ gravitational radii and are then advected inward along paths that may deviate from the disk midplane. The resulting poloidal fields thread the black hole (BH) and launch highly variable, wobbling relativistic jets on timescales of order seconds, with the onset depending on the initial magnetic field and the plasma circularization radius. Although the jets are highly variable and misaligned with the BH spin axis, they sustain $\gtrsim 10^{50}$ erg s$^{-1}$, comparable to that inferred for long gamma-ray bursts (LGRB). We identify magnetic-flux inversions driven by the stochastic dynamo, leading to the formation of striped jets that could be imprinted in LGRB light curves. These results demonstrate that the accretion0disk dynamo provides a robust pathway for jet production in collapsars across a broad range of progenitors.

</details>

### [32] [Equilibrium Biphasicity and Non-Binary Pathwise Confinement in Stochastic Ising Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12708)
*Jean-Gabriel Attali*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 针对低温二维伊辛模型，论文揭示了Glauber动力学路径吸收结构比Gibbs相分类更为丰富：存在一个在纯相下测度为零但路径受限的集合R，其轨迹被限制在中心扇区C₀，但Cesàro平均收敛于两个纯相的等权重混合，并未产生第三Gibbs相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典统计力学认为低温二维伊辛模型（two-dimensional Ising model）的极值平衡态仅由两个纯Gibbs相（pure Gibbs phases）构成。然而，Glauber动力学（Glauber dynamics）的路径吸收结构（pathwise absorbing structure）是否完全等价于Gibbs相分类，尚不明确。论文旨在探索二者之间的差异。

Method: 论文通过构造一族稠密的初始构型（initial configurations）来展示路径吸收结构的丰富性。具体定义了集合R为所有不在两个纯相中的构型，并进一步定义中心扇区C₀，其中磁化强度（magnetization）M_n(σ)趋近于0。通过分析这些构型轨迹的受限性质，并与Cesàro平均的收敛行为相结合，进行对比分析。

Result: 集合R在两个纯相下均为零测集，但包含一个稠密的路径受限子集。具体地，存在一族稠密的初始构型，其轨迹被限制在中心扇区C₀⊂R内。尽管如此，这些轨迹的Cesàro平均收敛于两个纯相的等权重混合1/2(μ⁺+μ⁻)。

Conclusion: 低温二维伊辛模型的Glauber动力学路径吸收几何结构比Gibbs相分类更为丰富，但并未产生第三个Gibbs相。这一发现表明，平衡态分类与动力学吸收结构之间存在本质性差异。

Abstract: For the low-temperature two-dimensional Ising model, the two pure Gibbs phases exhaust the extremal equilibrium states, but not the pathwise absorbing structure of the Glauber dynamics. Let \[ P^\pm=\{σ:M_n(σ)\to \pm m_β\},\qquad R=Ω\setminus(P^+\cup P^-). \] We show that \(R\) is null under both pure phases but contains a dense pathwise confined subset. More precisely, we construct a dense family of initial configurations whose trajectories are confined to the centered sector \[ C_0=\{σ:M_n(σ)\to0\}\subset R. \] Nevertheless, the corresponding Cesaro averages converge to \(\frac12(μ^++μ^-)\). Thus the pathwise absorbing geometry is richer than the Gibbs-phase classification, without creating a third Gibbs phase.

### [33] [Chewing gums, snakes and candle cakes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12572)
*Benedetta Facciotti,Marta Mazzocco,Nikita Nikolaev*

Main category: math.GT

TL;DR: 本文通过具体且可计算性强的实例，系统阐述了带标记边界黎曼曲面的高阶Teichmüller空间中的一系列概念，重点介绍了从经典Teichmüller空间到边界带尖点Teichmüller空间的口香糖移动（chewing-gum move）极限过程，并从Fock-Goncharov视角重新审视了这些构造。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于CIME学校讲座内容，旨在通过显式且易于计算的例子，直观阐释围绕带标记边界的黎曼曲面的高阶Teichmüller空间（higher Teichmüller spaces）的一系列概念与定理。

Method: 首先回顾了带边界双曲黎曼曲面的经典Teichmüller空间及其在胖图（fat-graph）上的Thurston剪切坐标（shear coordinates）组合描述；然后通过口香糖移动（chewing-gum move）构造带边界尖点Teichmüller空间（bordered cusped Teichmüller space）作为两个边界分量碰撞的合流极限，产生蜡烛蛋糕（candle cake）结构；最后从Fock-Goncharov视角，利用PSL_n(R)中传输矩阵的蛇形演算（snake calculus）重新审视这些构造，并指出口香糖移动是合并（amalgamation）的逆操作。

Result: 建立了一个从经典Teichmüller空间到带边界尖点Teichmüller空间的显式极限构造过程，并在高阶群PSL_n(R)的框架下实现了相应的传输矩阵描述与几何操作的代数对应。

Conclusion: 本文以具体、直观的方式展示了相关定理与构造，侧重于概念阐释而非形式化证明，为理解和进一步研究高阶Teichmüller空间提供了清晰的计算导向路径。

Abstract: The aim of these lecture notes, based on lectures given by the second author at the CIME school in Cetraro, is to illustrate a range of ideas surrounding higher Teichmuller spaces of Riemann surfaces with marked boundaries through explicit and computationally tractable examples. After reviewing the classical Teichmuller space of hyperbolic Riemann surfaces with boundary and its combinatorial description in terms of Thurston shear coordinates on a fat-graph, we explain how the bordered cusped Teichmuller space arises as a confluent limit when two boundary components in the Riemann surface collide via the so-called chewing-gum move giving rise to a candle cake. We then revisit these constructions from the Fock-Goncharov perspective, explaining snake calculus for transport matrices in PSL_n(R) and explain how the chewing gum move is the inverse of amalgamation. Rather than focusing on formal proofs, our goal is to illustrate the underlying theorems and constructions in a concrete and intuitive way.

### [34] [Scaling Symmetry in Symplectic Thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12641)
*M. C. Baldiotti,R. Fresneda*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过将约束哈密顿动力学（constrained Hamiltonian dynamics）与辛几何（symplectic geometry）和切触几何（contact geometry）相统一，研究了热力学中的标度对称性（scaling symmetry）。通过接触化（contactization）和辛化（symplectization）的数学过程，证明固定一个扩展的全局标度变量可恢复基于标度不变量的标准热力学描述。该几何形式体系通过理想气体与范德瓦尔斯气体（van der Waals gas）拉格朗日子流形（Lagrangian submanifold）之间的微分同胚得到阐明。将该框架应用于史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）发现，打破内能与熵之间的标度对称性是容纳非等温动力学的基本物理要求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索热力学中标度对称性的几何基础，旨在统一约束哈密顿动力学与辛/切触几何，从而在更抽象的数学框架下理解热力学的基本结构。

Method: 采用接触化与辛化等数学过程，在几何框架内固定扩展的全局标度变量，以恢复标准热力学描述。通过建立理想气体与范德瓦尔斯气体拉格朗日子流形之间的微分同胚来阐明该形式体系，并将其应用于史瓦西黑洞系统。

Result: 证明了固定全局标度变量可有效恢复基于标度不变量的标准热力学。在黑洞情形下，打破内能与熵之间的标度对称性是描述非等温动力学的必要条件。

Conclusion: 标度对称性的破缺在非等温热力学系统中具有基础性地位，几何形式体系为理解热力学对称性提供了统一视角。

Abstract: This paper investigates scaling symmetry in thermodynamics by unifying constrained Hamiltonian dynamics with symplectic and contact geometries. Through the mathematical processes of contactization and symplectization, we demonstrate that fixing an extended global scale variable effectively recovers the standard thermodynamic description in terms of scale-invariant quantities. The geometric formalism is illustrated by establishing the diffeomorphism between the Lagrangian submanifolds of ideal and van der Waals gases. Finally, applying this framework to a Schwarzschild black hole reveals that breaking the scale symmetry between internal energy and entropy is a fundamental physical requirement to accommodate non-isothermal dynamics.

Result: 证明了在某些有限谱三元组中，Lipschitz半范数（Lipschitz seminorm）与算子范数（operator norm）相等；此外，显式构造了一类谱三元组，其中Connes谱距离恰好等于量子迹距离。

Abstract: In this paper, we study the properties of Connes spectral distances between quantum states under unitary transformations. We mainly focus on spectral triples with matrix algebras acting on finite dimensional Hilbert spaces via some linear representations. We derive some elementary properties of the Connes spectral distances and optimal elements. We prove that there are some finite spectral triples in which the Lipschitz seminorms are equal to the operator norms. We also explicitly construct some spectral triples in which the Connes spectral distances between quantum states are exactly the quantum trace distances. These results and concrete examples are significant for studies of geometric structures of finite spectral triples and mathematical relations of qubits and other quantum states in the framework of noncommutative geometry.

### [36] [A Guide to Applications of $k$-Contact Geometry in Dissipative Field Equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13313)
*J. de Lucas,J. Lange,M. Krych*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了 $k$-接触 Hamilton–De Donder–Weyl 形式主义作为耗散场方程几何框架的实际适用范围，给出了多种非线性非保守偏微分方程（PDE）的显式哈密顿描述，并建立了正则性条件、双曲性/椭圆性判据及耗散定律等关键工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的几何场论框架主要适用于保守系统，缺乏描述耗散（dissipative）场方程的统一几何结构。本文旨在拓展 $k$-接触 Hamilton–De Donder–Weyl 形式主义（$k$-contact Hamilton–De Donder–Weyl formalism）的实际应用范围，为耗散型非线性场方程提供严谨的几何描述。

Method: 采用 $k$-接触流形（$k$-contact manifolds）作为核心几何框架，定义并分析了 $\bigoplus^k {\rm T}^*Q\times\mathbb{R}^k$ 上的正则 $k$-接触结构以及精确 $k$-辛相空间（exact $k$-symplectic phase spaces）的 $k$-接触化（$k$-contactification）。特别地，针对余切丛上的精确二辛结构定义了并分析了特殊的二接触化（two-contactification）。此外，发展了 $k$-接触化上的 Hamilton–De Donder–Weyl 方程分裂结果、正则性条件、超双曲性/双曲性/椭圆性判据（ultrahyperbolicity/hyperbolicity/ellipticity criteria），以及由无穷小动力学对称性（infinitesimal dynamical symmetries）诱导的耗散定律。

Result: 得到了多种含多项式耗散项的非线性非保守偏微分方程（nonlinear nonconservative PDEs）的显式哈密顿描述，包括阻尼 Klein–Gordon、Allen–Cahn、广义 Burgers、带线性吸收的孔隙介质方程（porous medium equations with linear absorption）、复 Ginzburg–Landau、阻尼非线性 Schrödinger、Fisher–KPP、阻尼 $\phi^4$、阻尼 sine–Gordon 以及 FitzHugh–Nagumo 方程等。

Conclusion: 该 $k$-接触几何框架能够为一大类耗散型非线性场方程提供统一的哈密顿描述，具有广泛的实际应用前景。文中还强调了该框架在更多实际问题中的进一步应用潜力。

Abstract: We study the practical scope of the $k$-contact Hamilton--De Donder--Weyl formalism as a geometric framework for dissipative field equations. In particular, our work focuses on canonical $k$-contact manifolds on $\bigoplus^k {\rm T}^*Q\times\mathbb{R}^k$ and $k$-contactifications of exact $k$-symplectic phase spaces. A special two-contactification of exact two-symplectic structures on cotangent bundles is defined and analysed. We also develop several tools for applications, including splitting results for the Hamilton--De Donder--Weyl equations on $k$-contactifications, regularity conditions for such spaces, criteria for the ultrahyperbolicity, hyperbolicity, or ellipticity of PDEs associated with Hamiltonian $k$-contact systems, dissipation laws associated with infinitesimal dynamical symmetries, relevance and applications of quadratic dissipative terms in the Hamiltonian, etc. Our methods yield explicit Hamiltonian descriptions for several nonlinear nonconservative PDEs with polynomial dissipative terms, including damped Klein--Gordon, Allen--Cahn, generalized Burgers, porous medium equations with linear absorption, complex Ginzburg--Landau, damped nonlinear Schrödinger, Fisher--KPP, damped $φ^4$, damped sine--Gordon, and FitzHugh--Nagumo equations, and many others. Our work also stresses the many further practical applications of this framework.

### [37] [On the asymptotic behavior at the kinetic time of a weakly interacting Fermi gas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13499)
*Peter S. Madsen,Phan Thành Nam,Herbert Spohn,Minh-Binh Tran*

Method: 通过分析弱相互作用费米气体在 $t\sim λ^{-2}$ 动力学时间尺度下的多体量子动力学，证明当初始状态接近平衡时，两点时间关联函数（two-point time correlation function）的领头阶行为完全由平衡态下玻尔兹曼-诺德海姆碰撞算符的碰撞频率（collisional frequency）确定。

Result: 成功证明，在初态接近平衡的条件下，多体量子动力学的两点时间关联函数的领头阶行为完全由平衡态玻尔兹曼-诺德海姆碰撞算符的碰撞频率决定，证实了Lukkarinen-Spohn的预测。

Conclusion: 该结果为量子玻尔兹曼方程提供了来自多体量子力学的严格验证，表明在弱相互作用极限下，平衡态附近的量子动力学可由经典碰撞过程有效描述。

Abstract: This paper is devoted to the dynamics of a weakly interacting Fermi gas at the kinetic time regime $t\sim λ^{-2}$ where $λ\ll 1$ is the strength of the interaction potential. We prove that if the initial state is close to equilibrium, then the two-point time correlation function of the many-body quantum dynamics can be computed effectively. In fact, we show that its leading order behavior is determined completely by the collisional frequency of the Boltzmann-Nordheim collision operator at equilibrium. This settles a prediction by Lukkarinen-Spohn, and thus gives a justification of the quantum Boltzmann equation from many-body quantum mechanics.

### [38] [Gibbons-Tsarev type systems and Eventual identities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13505)
*Alessandro Arsie,Paolo Lorenzoni,Sara Perletti,Karoline van Gemst*

TL;DR: 本文证明与正则非半单F-流形相关的dKP方程的非可对角化约化不存在，通过推导广义Gibbons-Tsarev系统并利用正则F-流形的最终恒等（eventual identity）结构构造了一类解，进而将此类向量场用于构造Pavlov流体动力学链的可积约化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究与正则非半单F-流形（regular non-semisimple F-manifolds）相关的dKP方程（dispersionless Kadomtsev–Petviashvili equation）是否存在非可对角化（non-diagonalisable）约化，以填补该理论框架下的空白。

Method: 在非半单/非可对角化设定下推导并研究广义Gibbons–Tsarev系统（generalised Gibbons–Tsarev system, gGT system），利用正则F-流形结构的最终恒等（eventual identity）定义解类，并以此构造Pavlov流体动力学链（Pavlov's hydrodynamic chain）的可积约化。

Result: 证明了与正则非半单F-流形相关的dKP方程的非可对角化约化不存在；发现了gGT系统的一类解由底层正则F-流形结构的最终恒等定义；构造了Pavlov流体动力学链的可积约化，其解由乘法算子的Jordan块结构任意选择决定。

Conclusion: 正则非半单F-流形框架下dKP方程的非可对角化约化被严格排除，但通过最终恒等结构仍可获得gGT系统的解，并成功构造Pavlov链的可积约化，这为F-流形理论中的可积系统提供了新的构造途径。

Abstract: We show that non-diagonalisable reductions of the dKP equation associated with regular non-semisimple $F$-manifolds cannot exist. The proof is based on the derivation and study of a generalised Gibbons--Tsarev system (gGT system) in the non-semisimple/non-diagonalisable setting. Remarkably, a class of solutions of the gGT system is defined by eventual identities of the underlying regular $F$-manifold structure. Furthermore, we use these vector fields to construct integrable reductions of Pavlov's hydrodynamic chain. In this case, the corresponding solutions are defined for any choice of Jordan block structure of the operator of multiplication by an eventual identity.
