### [39] [Surface Growth Driven by an Optimality Criterion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13602)
*Rohan Abeyaratne,Roberto Paroni,Marco Picchi Scardaoni*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一个基于最优性原则（optimality principle）的变分框架（variational framework），用于模拟增生性表面生长（ accretive surface growth）。不同于预设动力学定律，该框架在时间离散设定下，通过求解约束最小化问题获得每个时间步的构型。生长被建模为受全局质量约束的不可逆表面沉积过程，驱动力由目标泛函（此处为结构平均柔度，structural mean compliance）编码。以线弹性悬臂梁的层层沉积生长为例进行说明，并讨论了生长诱导残余应力导致的非唯一性与局域化现象，以及通过正则化项和形式极限过程导出时间连续极限（constrained gradient flow）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有生长模型通常需要预设动力学定律来刻画演化过程。本文旨在提出一个更一般的变分框架，通过最优性原则而非先验动力学关系来确定表面生长构型，以捕捉生长过程中的残余应力效应、非唯一性和局域化等复杂现象。

Method: 采用时间离散设定，将每个时间步的构型定义为在全局质量约束下最小化某个目标泛函（如结构平均柔度）的解。生长被视为不可逆表面沉积过程。针对柔度泛函可能失去凸性导致解不唯一的问题，引入正则化项惩罚与前一步构型的偏差。最后通过形式极限过程，从时间离散公式导出时间连续极限——约束梯度流（constrained gradient flow）。

Result: 以线弹性悬臂梁的层层沉积（可能包含预应变和预曲率）为例进行说明。结果表明，生长诱导的残余应力会改变柔度泛函的凸性，从而导致解的非唯一性和局域化现象。引入正则化项可缓解这一问题。

Conclusion: 所提出的变分框架为模拟增生性表面生长提供了一种不依赖预设动力学定律的新途径。通过约束最小化问题统一描述了质量约束与驱动机制，并能自然地处理残余应力导致的非唯一性。时间连续极限的导出使得该框架与梯度流（gradient flow）动力学建立了联系。

Abstract: We propose a variational framework for accretive surface growth driven by an optimality principle. Rather than prescribing a kinetic law, the configuration at each time step is obtained, within a time-discrete setting, as the solution of a constrained minimization problem. Growth is modeled as an irreversible surface deposition process subject to a global mass constraint, while the driving mechanism is encoded in an objective functional, here taken to be the structural mean compliance.
  The approach is illustrated on a linearly elastic cantilever beam whose cross-sectional height evolves through layered accretion, possibly involving prestrain and precurvature. Growth-induced residual stresses can alter the convexity of the compliance functional, leading to nonuniqueness and localization phenomena. We explore the possibility of adding a regularization term penalizing deviations from the previous-step configuration. Finally, through a formal limiting procedure, we derive from the time-discrete formulation a time-continuous limit in the form of a constrained gradient flow.

</details>


### [40] [Volumetric Growth in Linear Elasticity Driven by an Optimality Criterion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13609)
*Rohan Abeyaratne,Roberto Paroni,Marco Picchi Scardaoni*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文在线性弹性力学框架下，将体积增长（volumetric growth）构建为一个由约束优化驱动的过程，其中生长张量（growth tensor）通过隐式优化而非唯象演化律确定，并通过有限元离散（finite element discretization）转化为仅关于生长变量的有限维约束最小化问题，数值算例验证了该框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有体积增长模型通常依赖唯象演化律（phenomenological evolution laws）来显式规定生长张量，缺乏从优化视角出发的统一理论框架。本文旨在建立一种将生长视为约束优化过程的力学框架，以更自然地捕捉生长与平衡、质量守恒及不可逆性之间的耦合关系。

Method: 以线性弹性力学（linearized elasticity）为力学框架，将体积增长表述为优化驱动过程。生长张量通过约束优化隐式确定：每一步增量中，位移和生长场需满足平衡方程、质量守恒约束以及增量生长的不可逆性条件（irreversibility condition），同时目标泛函（objective functional）编码生长驱动机制。采用有限元离散将问题转化为仅关于生长变量的有限维约束最小化问题，使演化具有投影梯度流（projected gradient flow）的几何诠释。

Result: 通过有限元离散，成功将原连续优化问题归约为一个仅涉及生长变量的有限维约束最小化问题。该方法使生长演化可被解释为投影梯度流。数值算例展示了所提出框架的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文表明，在线性弹性框架下，体积增长可通过约束优化而非唯象演化律进行建模，该优化视角为理解生长与力学平衡的耦合提供了新的理论路径。

Abstract: Using linearized elasticity as a convenient mechanical framework, we show that volumetric growth can be formulated as an optimization-driven process in which the growth tensor is determined implicitly by constrained optimization rather than prescribed through phenomenological evolution laws. At each incremental step, the displacement and growth fields satisfy equilibrium, mass-balance constraints, and an irreversibility condition enforcing accretive growth, while an objective functional encodes the driving mechanism of the process.
  Finite element discretization leads to a finite-dimensional constrained minimization problem in the growth variables alone and makes explicit the interpretation of the evolution as a projected gradient flow. Numerical examples illustrate the proposed framework.

</details>


### [41] [Stochastic modeling of Fourier modes in two-dimensional turbulence via filtered white noise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13671)
*Paolo Cifani,Franco Flandoli,Andrea Zanoni*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过随机傅里叶分解（random Fourier decomposition）对二维湍流（two-dimensional turbulent flows）进行建模，识别出显著统计结构（如典型时间关联长度），并提出了一个傅里叶分量的随机模型（stochastic model），最后通过直接数值模拟（DNS）对比了该模型在被动标量输运（passive tracer transport）中的有效扩散效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了在热输运（heat transport）等应用中利用简化的湍流模型，需要一种能够有效捕捉湍流统计特性的建模方法。本文旨在通过随机傅里叶分解构建一个既简洁又能反映真实湍流统计结构的模型。

Method: 首先，对中间尺度（intermediate scales）强迫下的二维湍流进行傅里叶时间序列（Fourier time series）分析，识别统计结构；然后，基于发现的典型时间关联长度（typical time correlation length），提出一个描述傅里叶分量的随机模型；最后，通过直接数值模拟（direct numerical simulation, DNS）计算对流动力学（convective dynamics）下被动标量的输运，并与随机模型产生的有效扩散（effective diffusion）进行比较。

Result: 研究发现二维湍流傅里叶分量中存在显著的统计结构，尤其是一个典型的时间关联长度。据此构建的随机模型能够产生与直接数值模拟可比较的有效扩散效果。

Conclusion: 基于随机傅里叶分解的建模方法能够有效再现二维湍流的关键统计特性，并在被动标量输运中提供合理的有效扩散预测，为简化湍流模型在热输运等领域的应用提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Modeling turbulent flows by a random Fourier decomposition is a classical procedure in order to use simplified models of turbulence in heat transport and other applications. We carefully investigate the Fourier time series of two-dimensional turbulent flows forced at intermediate scales and identify significant statistical structures. In particular, we find the existence of a typical time correlation length, and propose a stochastic model for the Fourier components. Finally, we compute the transport of a passive tracer under purely convective dynamics by means of direct numerical simulation of the turbulent flow and compare it with the effective diffusion produced by the stochastic model.

### [42] [Irregular SLE(4) martingales and isomonodromic deformations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13802)
*Harini Desiraju,Aleksandra Korzhenkova,Eveliina Peltola*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文在黎曼球面上研究了非 Fuchs 型单值保持形变，推导了等单值形变参数的 Loewner 演化，并利用此结果构造了具有双极点的 Schramm-Loewner 演化（SLE(4)）过程的鞅可观测量，最终通过中心荷 c=1 的共形场论（CFT）中的合流 BPZ 方程唯一刻画了这些 SLE(4) 可观测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将非 Fuchs 型单值保持形变（non-Fuchsian monodromy preserving deformations）与 Loewner 演化及 SLE 过程建立联系，从而拓展等单值形变理论在统计力学和共形场论中的应用。

Method: 首先在黎曼球面上引入非 Fuchs 型单值保持形变，其等单值形变参数（isomonodromic deformation parameters）包含奇点位置和 Birkhoff 谱不变量（Birkhoff spectral invariants）。然后推导这些参数的 Loewner 演化，并利用共形协变性（conformal covariance）构造 SLE(4) 过程的鞅可观测量（martingale observables）。最后通过中心荷 c=1 的共形场论中的合流 BPZ 方程（confluent BPZ equations）唯一刻画这些可观测量。

Result: 得到了等单值形变参数的 Loewner 演化方程；构造了含双极点（double poles）的 SLE(4) 过程的鞅可观测量，其表达式包含 Loewner 演化的前 Schwarz 导数和 Schwarz 导数（pre-Schwarzian and Schwarzian）；证明了这些 SLE(4) 可观测量可由 c=1 CFT 的合流 BPZ 方程唯一表征。

Conclusion: 非 Fuchs 型单值保持形变与 SLE(4)/CFT 之间存在深层联系，Loewner 演化成为连接等单值形变理论与随机共形几何的桥梁。

Abstract: We consider non-Fuchsian monodromy preserving deformations on a Riemann sphere. The associated isomonodromic deformation parameters on this surface comprise the positions of the singularities, together with the Birkhoff (spectral) invariants owing to the presence of irregular singularities. Our first main result is the derivation of the Loewner evolution of these isomonodromic deformation parameters. Using this result, we construct martingale observables for Schramm-Loewner evolution (SLE(4)) processes in the presence of double poles. Geometrically, the expressions contain the pre-Schwarzian and Schwarzian of the Loewner evolution, arising from conformal covariance of the observable. Furthermore, we characterize these SLE(4) observables uniquely in terms of confluent BPZ equations of a CFT with central charge c=1.

</details>

### [43] [Determining the Spin-Analyzing Powers via Invariants of the Spin Correlation Matrices and Probing the Bell Non-Locality at the Lepton Colliders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13250)
*Dianwei Wang,Xiqing Hao,Liwei Liu,Lina Wu,Tianjun Li*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 论文证明了自旋关联矩阵（spin correlation matrix）的迹 Tr[C] 在洛伦兹对称性和基旋转下保持不变，并利用该不变量（invariant）实现双费米子（two-fermion）自旋分析能力的提取、自旋关联矩阵重构，以及基于 CHSH-Horodecki 判据的贝尔非局域性（Bell non-locality）探测。以 BESIII 实验中的 Λ\barΛ 产生与衰变为例，展示了该不变量在标准模型（Standard Model, SM）精度检验和新物理（new physics）探测中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在 e⁺e⁻ 对撞机中研究双费米子 F_aF_b 经由单媒介子交换的产生与衰变过程，旨在寻找能够规避不可行定理（no-go theorem）的贝尔非局域性探测方法，并构建一个可在标准模型精度测量和新物理探测中使用的新的物理可观测量（physical observable）。

Method: 基于洛伦兹对称性（Lorentz symmetry）定义自旋，或考虑自旋密度矩阵（spin density matrix）中的隐含对称性，证明自旋关联矩阵 C 的迹 Tr[C] 是基旋转下的不变量（invariant quantity）。利用该不变量确定双费米子的自旋分析能力（spin-analyzing power）乘积，并重构自旋关联矩阵；再通过 CHSH-Horodecki 判据探测贝尔非局域性。

Result: 对于标量玻色子（scalar）和规范玻色子（gauge boson）等单媒介子交换，可通过 Tr[C] 确定自旋分析能力乘积并重构自旋关联矩阵；利用 CHSH-Horodecki 判据可有效探测贝尔非局域性，规避不可行定理。以 BESIII 实验的 Λ\barΛ 产生与衰变为例进行了具体研究。对于标量交换情形，进一步讨论了自旋关联矩阵的广义不变量及其现象学后果。

Conclusion: Tr[C] 是一个不依赖于基选择的普适不变量，可作为一种新的物理可观测量，用于标准模型精度检验和超越标准模型的新物理探测。在标量交换情形下，自旋关联矩阵的广义不变量还具有额外的现象学含义。

Abstract: We consider the two-fermion $F_a F_b$ productions and decays via one mediator exchange at the $e^+e^-$ collider. With the assumption that the spin is defined via the Lorentz symmetry, or considering the implicit symmetry in the spin density matrix, we prove that the trace ${\rm Tr} [C]$ of the spin correlation matrix $C$ is an invariant quantity, and is invariant under basis rotations. Thus, for the exchanges of one mediator such as scalar and gauge boson, we can determine the product of the spin-analyzing powers for $F_a F_b$ via ${\rm Tr} [C]$, and reconstruct the spin correlation matrix. With the CHSH-Horodecki criterion, we can probe the Bell non-locality, and evade the no-go theorem. To be concrete, we study the Bell non-locality for the $Λ\bar Λ$ productions and decays at the BESIII experiment. In addition, the invariant ${\rm Tr} [C]$ is a new physics observable to probe the new physics beyond the Standard Model (SM) and study the SM precision measurements. Moreover, for the scalar exchanges, we discuss the general invariants of the spin correlation matrices and the related phenomenological consequences.

</details>


### [44] [Calorimetric approach to paleo-detection of dark matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13659)
*Samuel Hedges,Patrick Huber*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文首次基于量热读出（calorimetric readout）对古探测器（paleo-detector）暗物质灵敏度进行分析，利用核反冲产生的稳定晶格空位数作为每事件可观测量（per-event observable），与径迹长度互补。通过橄榄石（olivine）中的全级联SRIM模拟，计算了100 g·Gyr暴露量的灵敏度，发现空位读出与现有径迹分析灵敏度相当；两者联合可提供|\emph{dE}/\emph{dx}|的事件级代理，从而区分反冲核种类，将中子本底抑制一个数量级以上。联合分析的灵敏度在弱相互作用大质量粒子（WIMP）质量几十GeV时可达自旋无关的暗物质-核子散射截面约10^{-48} cm^2，与未来直接探测实验相当。研究还提出结合选择平面照明显微镜与扫描电子显微镜的两阶段读出方案，使百克级分析成为可能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有古探测器暗物质分析主要依赖径迹长度作为可观测量，但忽略了核反冲产生的晶格空位信息。同时，中子本底是暗物质探测中的主要背景，需要有效的区分手段。本文旨在探索量热读出模式，利用空位数作为补充可观测量以提升暗物质探测灵敏度并抑制中子本底。

Method: 采用橄榄石矿物中的全级联SRIM模拟，计算核反冲产生的稳定晶格空位数，将其作为每事件可观测量；将空位读数与径迹长度联合分析，构建|\emph{dE}/\emph{dx}|的事件级代理，利用暗物质-原子核散射截面与核质量数平方（A²）成正比、而中子-原子核散射截面近似平坦的质量依赖性差异来区分信号与中子本底。

Result: 空位读出单独可达到与最先进径迹分析相当的灵敏度水平；两种可观测量联合分析可在中等暗物质质量下将中子本底抑制一个数量级以上；联合分析在WIMP质量几十GeV时达到自旋无关的暗物质-核子散射截面约10^{-48} cm²，与未来直接探测实验的灵敏度相当。

Conclusion: 量热读出模式为古探测器暗物质探测提供了一种有效的补充手段，空位与径迹的联合分析显著提升了中子本底抑制能力，使古探测器灵敏度达到与未来直接探测实验相当的水平。结合选择平面照明显微镜（SPIM）与扫描电子显微镜（SEM）的两阶段读出方案为实现百克级暴露量分析提供了可行路径。

Abstract: We present the first paleo-detector dark matter sensitivity analysis based on a calorimetric readout, in which the number of stable lattice vacancies produced by each nuclear recoil is used as a per-event observable complementary to the track length. Using full-cascade SRIM simulations in olivine, we compute the expected sensitivity for a 100 gGyr exposure. We find that a vacancy-only readout reaches a sensitivity envelope very similar to that of state-of-the-art track-only analyses. The combination of the two observables provides an event-by-event proxy for |dE/dx| and hence for the recoiling nuclear species. Since the neutron-nucleus cross section is approximately flat in nuclear mass while the dark-matter--nucleus cross section scales as $A^2$, this discrimination suppresses the dominant neutron background by more than an order of magnitude at moderate dark matter masses. The combined-analysis sensitivity reaches spin-independent dark-matter--nucleon cross sections of order $10^{-48}\,\mathrm{cm}^2$ at WIMP masses of a few tens of GeV, comparable to future direct detection experiments. A two-stage readout combining selective-plane illumination microscopy with scanning electron microscopy is identified as a path to making a 100 g-scale analysis plausible.

</details>

*D. Aristizabal Sierra,A. Betancur,K. Pohl,J. Velez*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本论文利用π⁰衰变中产生的光子与暗光子（dark photon）的能谱形状差异，提出一种新的暗光子搜索方法；通过GEANT4模拟钨箔靶与质子束系统，证明该方法能够探测此前未探索的参数空间，且结果具有高度模型无关性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究假设使用70 μm厚的钨箔（tungsten foil），间距为200 μm，并采用1 GeV的质子束（proton beam）；基于GEANT4模拟框架开发了包含光子产生与探测过程以及背景噪声（background）的蒙特卡洛模型进行数值估算。

Conclusion: 所提出的搜索方案具有高度的模型无关性（model independent），为暗光子实验提供了新的可行路径。

Abstract: Spectral shape differences between photons produced in $π^0\toγ+γ$ and $π^0\toγ+A_D$ may provide a new avenue for dark photon searches. Assuming 70 $μ$m thick tungsten foils separated by 200 $μ$m and a 1 GeV proton beam, we developed a GEANT4 model to estimate photon production and detection including background. Our results demonstrate that multiple campaign runs with a 10-50 $μ$A beam could probe previously unexplored regions of parameter space in models where the dark photon has predominantly invisible decays. ### [46] [Mass of the dark antibaryon using $B_d\rightarrow Λψ_{DS}$ channel in light cone QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13701)
*M. A. Abri,N. Hajirasouliha,K. Azizi*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用光锥求和规则（Light Cone Sum Rules, LCSR）分析B_d→Λ ψ_{DS}衰变过程；在算子乘积展开（operator product expansion, OPE）中引入Λ重子分布振幅（distribution amplitudes）直至twist-6的非微扰贡献。

Result: 计算出分支比（branching fraction）作为暗区反重子ψ_{DS}质量的函数；通过与BaBar和Belle合作组的实验上限比较，确定了与B介子生成机制相一致的ψ_{DS}质量范围。

Abstract: According to the $B$-mesogenesis framework, the baryon asymmetry of the Universe and dark matter can be simultaneously generated through CP-violating $B$-meson oscillations. In this mechanism, $B$-mesons decay into a Standard Model baryon and a dark-sector antibaryon, denoted by $ψ_{DS}$. Within this scenario, we investigate the allowed mass window for $ψ_{DS}$ using Light Cone Sum Rules (LCSR) for $B_d\rightarrowΛ\, ψ_{DS}$ decay. To include non-perturbative effects, we employ contributions up to twist-6 of the $Λ$ distribution amplitudes in the operator product expansion (OPE). We derive the branching fraction as a function of dark antibaryon mass and, by comparing with the experimental limits by the BaBar and Belle collaborations, determine the mass ranges of $ψ_{DS}$ consistent with the $B$-mesogenesis mechanism.

### [47] [Jet Momentum Broadening in Viscous QCD Matter: A Moment Expansion Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12791)
*Isabella Danhoni,Nicki Mullins,Jorge Noronha*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文将针对射流展宽（jet broadening）的非平衡修正公式化地引入QCD有效动力学理论（QCD effective kinetic theory），通过介质分布函数的矩展开（moment expansion）方法，并在14矩近似（14-moment approximation）下显式计算了近平衡态贡献，证明该修正由介质的剪切应力张量（shear-stress tensor）控制，从而建立了从QCD有效动力学理论到事件逐事件黏性流体力学模拟（event-by-event viscous hydrodynamic simulations）的直接映射，用于将局域剪切应力场转换为重离子碰撞中各向异性射流展宽修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非平衡条件下射流动量展宽的解析描述尚不完善，传统方法多局限于平衡态假设。本文旨在通过矩展开方法将非平衡效应系统地纳入QCD有效动力学理论框架，并建立其与黏性流体力学模拟之间的定量联系。

Method: 采用介质分布函数的矩展开方法——该技术原本用于从动理学理论导出相对论性黏性流体力学（relativistic viscous hydrodynamics）——将非平衡射流动量展宽纳入QCD有效动力学理论。在14矩近似下显式计算了近平衡态下空间射流展宽张量（spatial jet broadening tensor）$\hat q^{ij}$的领先阶贡献。

Result: 显式计算表明，近平衡态下$\hat q^{ij}$的领先阶贡献由介质的剪切应力张量直接控制。由此建立了从QCD有效动力学理论到事件逐事件黏性流体力学模拟的直接映射。

Conclusion: 该映射允许将流体力学模拟中局域的剪切应力场直接转换为重离子碰撞中射流展宽的各向异性修正，为非平衡环境下射流-流体耦合研究提供了可计算的动理学理论基础。

Abstract: We formulate out-of-equilibrium jet momentum broadening in QCD effective kinetic theory through a moment expansion of the medium distribution function, a method traditionally used to derive relativistic viscous hydrodynamics from kinetic theory. We explicitly compute the leading near-equilibrium contribution to the spatial jet broadening tensor $\hat q^{ij}$ within the 14-moment approximation, and show that it is controlled by the medium shear-stress tensor. This provides a direct map from QCD effective kinetic theory to event-by-event viscous hydrodynamic simulations, converting local shear-stress fields into anisotropic corrections to jet broadening in heavy-ion collisions.

</details>


### [48] [Secondary Gravitational Wave Signatures from 5D Rotating Primordial Black Holes in the Dark Dimension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12948)
*Waqas Ahmed,George K. Leontaris*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在Swampland纲领启发的暗维度（Dark Dimension）框架下，研究了五维旋转原初黑洞作为暗物质候选者的可行性。分析表明，微米尺度额外维度和记忆负担效应（memory burden effect）显著延长了黑洞寿命，从而打开了10¹⁰ g至10²¹ g的暗物质窗口。该窗口内黑洞形成产生的曲率扰动能通过二阶标量诱导机制产生随机引力波背景，信号峰值位于nHz至Hz频段，处于LISA和DECIGO/BBO的灵敏度范围内，Fisher预测显示未来观测台能以百分比精度约束黑洞参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在Swampland纲领启发的暗维度（Dark Dimension）框架下，探索五维旋转原初黑洞作为暗物质候选者的可行性，并检验该情景中产生的可观测引力波信号。

Method: 计算五维旋转原初黑洞的蒸发动力学；引入记忆负担效应（memory burden effect）对蒸发速率的量子引力抑制（因子S⁻ᵖ）；采用对数正态原初功率谱（log-normal primordial power spectrum，σ=1, f_PBH=1）通过二阶标量诱导机制（second-order scalar-induced effects）计算引力波能量密度Ω_GW h²；利用Fisher预测（Fisher forecasts）评估未来观测台对模型参数的约束能力。

Result: 五维旋转黑洞在p=2时的寿命显著延长，建立暗物质质量窗口为10¹⁰ g ≲ M ≲ 10²¹ g。引力波背景信号峰值覆盖nHz至Hz频段，落在LISA和DECIGO/BBO的灵敏度范围内，且与当前宇宙微波背景（CMB）谱畸变约束一致。Fisher预测表明未来观测台能以百分比精度约束黑洞质量、暗物质占比、谱宽和记忆负担指数。

Conclusion: 探测预期的引力波背景将为微米尺度额外维度、原初黑洞暗物质和记忆负担效应提供同时证据，从而对量子引力和额外维度物理构成决定性检验。

Abstract: We investigate five-dimensional rotating primordial black holes (PBHs) as dark matter candidates within the Dark Dimension (DD) scenario motivated by the Swampland Program. In this framework, a micron-scale extra dimension suppresses Hawking evaporation, allowing PBHs with initial masses \(M \gtrsim 10^{10}\,\mathrm{g}\) to survive to the present epoch. Moreover, the memory burden effect, a quantum-gravitational suppression of the evaporation rate by \(S^{-p}\), significantly prolongs PBH lifetimes and enlarges the allowed parameter space. We compute the evaporation dynamics for rotating 5D PBHs, derive the enhanced lifetime for \(p=2\), and establish the dark matter window \(10^{10}\,\mathrm{g} \lesssim M \lesssim 10^{21}\,\mathrm{g}\). The curvature perturbations responsible for PBH formation also generate a stochastic gravitational wave background through second-order scalar-induced effects. Assuming a log-normal primordial power spectrum with \(σ=1\) and \(f_{\mathrm{PBH}}=1\), we calculate the present-day energy density \(Ω_{\mathrm{GW}}h^2\) across the Dark Dimension window. The predicted signals peak at frequencies from nHz to Hz, within the sensitivity ranges of LISA and DECIGO/BBO, while remaining consistent with current CMB spectral distortion bounds. Fisher forecasts show that future observatories can constrain the PBH mass, dark matter fraction, spectral width, and memory burden exponent with percent-level precision. A detection of the predicted gravitational wave background would provide simultaneous evidence for a micron-sized extra dimension, PBH dark matter, and the memory burden effect, offering a decisive test of quantum gravity and extra-dimensional physics.

</details>

### [49] [Competing Effect of Biquadratic and Heisenberg Coupling on Magnetic Tunnel Junction Molecular Spintronics Devices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12885)
*Andoniaina Mariah Randriambololona,Hayden Brown,Eva Mutunga,Andrew Grizzle,Christopher DAngelo,Pawan Tyagi*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟，系统研究了磁隧道结分子自旋电子学器件（MTJMSD）中海森堡交换耦合（HC）与双二次交换耦合（BQC）的竞争关系，发现HC主导器件磁化动力学并提供稳定性，而BQC仅起次要作用，但其存在可解释实验中观察到的非常规磁相位取向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 海森堡交换耦合（Heisenberg exchange coupling, HC）和双二次交换耦合（biquadratic exchange coupling, BQC）在磁隧道结（magnetic tunnel junctions, MTJ）及纳米自旋电子学结构中均已知存在，但两者在MTJ基分子自旋电子学器件（MTJMSD）中的竞争作用尚不明确。

Method: 采用基于三维海森堡模型（three-dimensional Heisenberg model）的蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟，在三种条件下系统改变BQC强度：无分子HC、强平行HC和强反平行HC，并分析MTJMSD的磁学与物理性质。

Result: 当存在强HC时，增加BQC强度对整体磁化强度影响极小，表明HC主导器件磁化；时间演化研究表明，仅含BQC的器件无法达到磁稳定性，而同时包含HC和BQC的器件因HC的稳定作用实现稳定磁态。

Conclusion: BQC在磁化动力学中起次要作用，无法超越HC的更强稳定效应；BQC的存在为实验中超出简单平行与反平行态的磁相位取向提供了合理解释。

Abstract: Heisenberg exchange coupling (HC) and biquadratic exchange coupling (BQC) are known to occur in magnetic tunnel junctions (MTJ) and nanoscale spintronics structures. MTJ-based molecular spintronics devices (MTJMSD) provide a platform to study these interactions and the correlated magnetic behavior they generate. Molecular spin channels formed along the exposed MTJ edge have been shown to produce strong exchange interactions that include HC and BQC, which can drive perpendicular alignment of spin vectors in adjacent ferromagnetic electrodes. Despite their importance, the competing roles of HC and BQC in MTJMSDs remain unclear. Monte Carlo simulations using a three-dimensional Heisenberg model were performed to systematically vary BQC strength under three conditions: no molecular HC, strong parallel HC, and strong antiparallel HC. The resulting magnetic and physical properties of the MTJMSDs were analyzed. Increasing BQC strength produced minimal changes in overall magnetization when strong HC was present, indicating that HC dominates device magnetization. Temporal evolution studies showed that devices with only BQC failed to reach magnetic stability, while devices with both HC and BQC achieved stable magnetic states due to the stabilizing influence of HC. These results show that BQC plays a secondary role in magnetization dynamics and cannot overcome the stronger stabilizing effect of HC. The presence of BQC offers a plausible explanation for experimentally observed magnetic phase orientations beyond simple parallel and antiparallel states in MTJMSDs.

### [50] [Matrix-noise Jacobians in stochastic-calculus inference and optimal paths](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12972)
*Surachate Limkumnerd*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个适用于θ-离散化扩散过程的有限步路径似然框架，发现矩阵型乘性噪声（multiplicative noise）在短时展开中会产生一个标量雅可比项J_σ，该量在标量各向同性和严格对角情形下为零，但在状态依赖的噪声方向混合不同分量时非零，并能在随机模型拟合和优化路径中产生可测量的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 乘性噪声（multiplicative noise）在白噪声极限下的解释方式会影响随机动力学的行为，而多维系统中矩阵值噪声振幅（matrix-valued noise amplitudes）存在标量例子中缺失的局部雅可比贡献，现有研究对此关注不足。

Method: 提出一个有限步路径似然框架（finite-step path-likelihood framework）来处理θ-离散化扩散过程，通过短时展开（short-time expansion）提取出标量雅可比项J_σ = ∂_j σ_{ik} ∂_i σ_{jk} - (∂_i σ_{ik})(∂_l σ_{lk})，并设计了两个配对比较模型（Model A和Model B）来控制漂移、扩散矩阵、插值点和高斯增量项，以测试该量的实际影响。

Result: J_σ在一维、标量各向同性（scalar-isotropic）和严格对角情形下为零，但当状态依赖的噪声方向混合不同分量时非零。在Model A中，移除非对角行列式贡献导致随机拟合法（stochastic prescription）的偏移，且当J_σ=0时该偏移消失。在Model B中，移除对应的状态依赖作用项改变了稳定的优化过渡路径（optimized transition path）。

Conclusion: 矩阵噪声部分的短时路径测度能够在标量例子中常见的抵消效应之外存活，并对拟合的随机拟合法和Onsager-Machlup路径产生可测量的变化，表明矩阵噪声效应在多维随机动力系统中不可忽视。

Abstract: Multiplicative noise makes stochastic dynamics depend on how the white-noise limit is interpreted. In multidimensional systems with matrix-valued noise amplitudes $σ(x)$, this dependence includes a local Jacobian contribution that is absent from the scalar examples most often used to build intuition. We formulate a finite-step path-likelihood framework for $θ$-discretized diffusions and show that its short-time expansion isolates the scalar $J_σ=\partial_jσ_{ik}\partial_iσ_{jk}-(\partial_iσ_{ik})(\partial_lσ_{lk})$. For a specified noise-amplitude representation $σ$, this quantity vanishes in one-dimensional, scalar-isotropic, and strictly diagonal cases, but can survive when state-dependent noise directions mix different components. We then test its consequences using paired comparisons that hold the drift, diffusion matrix, interpolation point, and Gaussian increment term fixed. In Model A, removing only the off-diagonal determinant contribution produces a shift in the fitted stochastic prescription that vanishes when $J_σ=0$. In Model B, removing the corresponding state-dependent action term changes a stable optimized transition path. These results show that a genuinely matrix-noise part of the short-time path measure can survive the scalar cancellations familiar from simpler settings and produce measurable changes in fitted stochastic prescriptions and Onsager--Machlup paths.

</details>


### [51] [Quantifying information flow along a stochastic trajectory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13509)

Method: 提出一种可扩展的深度学习方法（scalable deep-learning method），用于从一般时间序列数据中估计SIF。

Result: 该方法在精确可解的双粒子模型、Kuramoto振子（Kuramoto oscillators）以及相互作用的运动细胞的经验轨迹上均得到应用验证。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，SIF可作为数据驱动的协作结构（cooperative structures）指标，具有实证应用价值。

Abstract: Stochastic information flow (SIF) quantifies information flow at the trajectory level, overcoming the limitations of conventional symmetric, ensemble-averaged measures. Its applications to an exactly solvable two-particle model, Kuramoto oscillators, and empirical trajectories of interacting motile cells demonstrate the utility of SIF as a data-driven indicator of cooperative structures.

### [52] [Emergence of information interference in stochastic systems with non-diagonal noise and switching environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13556)
*Andrea Marchetti,Daniel Maria Busiello,Giorgio Nicoletti*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本研究聚焦于具有非对角噪声矩阵和随机切换环境的线性化随机系统，揭示了噪声各向异性和环境切换如何导致“信息干扰”（information interference）现象，即总互信息（mutual information）无法分解为确定性相互作用、噪声各向异性和环境切换各自贡献之和。研究识别出静态和动态两类信息干扰来源，并在流体力学耦合、温度切换及燃料驱动化学反应网络等物理系统中验证了该框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自然界中的随机力（stochastic forces）通常是非各向异性的（non-isotropic），噪声之间具有固有相关性，这与内部相互作用和环境变化共同塑造了真实系统中自由度之间的统计依赖关系。然而，现有理论缺乏对噪声各向异性（noise anisotropy）与环境随机切换共同作用下互信息结构的系统性理解。

Method: 研究针对线性化随机系统（linearized stochastic systems），同时引入非对角噪声矩阵（non-diagonal noise matrices）和随机切换环境（stochastically switching environments），从信息论角度分析总互信息的可分解性，识别信息干扰的静态项（static term）和动态项（dynamic term）。

Result: 在切换温度（switching temperatures）场景下，互信息可精确分解为内部贡献和环境贡献；在流体力学相互作用（hydrodynamic interactions）导致噪声各向异性时，共享流体会根据非互易性（non-reciprocity）程度掩盖或增强来自非保守力（non-conservative force）的信息；在燃料驱动化学反应网络（fuel-driven chemical reaction network）中，信息干扰受非平衡驱动（non-equilibrium driving）控制。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了关于各向异性噪声和环境变异性如何塑造随机系统中统计依赖关系的通用信息论视角，揭示了信息干扰的存在及其物理来源，并为理解复杂系统中的信息结构提供了新框架。

Abstract: Stochastic forces in natural systems are rarely isotropic. From hydrodynamically coupled colloids to chemical reaction networks, noise contributions are inherently correlated. Together with internal interactions and changing environments, they shape the dependencies between the degrees of freedom of real-world systems, as quantified by their mutual information. In this work, we focus on linearized stochastic systems with both non-diagonal noise matrices and stochastically switching environments. We study how their presence leads to the emergence of information interference, so that the total mutual information cannot be decomposed as the sum of the contributions from deterministic interactions, noise anisotropy, and environmental switching alone. We identify two distinct sources of information interference: a static term, arising from the simultaneous presence of deterministic coupling and noise anisotropy; and a dynamic term, emerging from the interplay between internal processes and environmental switches. We then apply this framework to different physical systems. In the presence of switching temperatures, the mutual information disentangles exactly into internal and environmental contributions. When the noise anisotropy arises instead from hydrodynamic interactions, we find that the presence of a shared fluid can either mask or enhance the information stemming from a non-conservative force depending on its degree of non-reciprocity. Finally, in a fuel-driven chemical reaction network, we show that information interference is controlled by the non-equilibrium driving. These results establish a general information-theoretic perspective on how anisotropic noise and environmental variability shape statistical dependencies in stochastic systems.

</details>


### [53] [Phase Ordering in a few O(n) Symmetric Models: Slow Growth, Mpemba Effect and Experimental Relevance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13564)
*Wasim Akram,Nalina Vadakkayil,Sohini Chatterjee,Subir K. Das*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟研究三维非守恒XY模型（nonconserved XY model）中的相序动力学，发现淬火（quench）到零温时特征长度尺度以约t^{0.15}的指数增长，远小于预期值1/2；同时观察到类似Mpemba效应（Mpemba effect）的反常弛豫行为，并在二维和三维Ising模型（Ising model）中进行了验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解三维非守恒XY模型从顺磁相（paramagnetic phase）淬火到铁磁区（ferromagnetic region）内不同最终温度时的相序动力学（phase ordering dynamics），特别是通过涡旋-反涡旋对（vortex and anti-vortex pair）湮灭形成的线缺陷（line defect）所主导的生长行为，并探究起始温度对弛豫速率的影响是否呈现类似Mpemba效应的反常现象。

Method: 采用蒙特卡洛模拟方法，对三维非守恒XY模型进行从顺磁相到铁磁区内不同最终温度T_f的淬火实验；同时对二维和三维Ising模型也进行类似模拟，并对比不同起始温度T_s下的弛豫行为差异。

Result: 当T_f=0时，特征长度尺度ℓ(t)随时间t的增长近似为t^{0.15}，远小于预期值1/2；该指数与三维Ising模型零温中间时间序化（intermediate time ordering）的指数类似。较高的起始温度T_s使系统更快达到最终平衡，此行为类似Mpemba效应。二维Ising模型中该效应仅在起始磁化（magnetization）接近零时出现；而三维中对于两种模型，即使初始构型从完整磁化分布中选取，该效应仍存在。

Conclusion: 三维非守恒XY模型在零温淬火下的生长指数显著偏离预期值，且系统表现出类似Mpemba效应的起始温度依赖性弛豫行为。该效应在三维模型中的鲁棒性更强，具有实验相关性（experimental relevance）。

Abstract: We study phase ordering dynamics in the three-dimensional nonconserved XY model, via Monte Carlo simulations, for quenches from paramagnetic phase to certain final temperatures $T_f$ within the ferromagnetic region of the phase diagram. The growth in the system occurs via annihilation of vortex and anti-vortex pairs, cores of which, in the three dimensional system geometry, join from different planes, on which the spins lie, to form line defects. In the long-time limit, the associated characteristic length scale, $\ell(t)$, appears to grow with time $(t)$ approximately as $t^{0.15}$, for $T_f=0$. The exponent is much smaller, like in the zero temperature intermediate time ordering in the three dimensional Ising model, than $1/2$, the expected value, that is realized for quenches to $T_f$ value that is sufficiently larger than zero. We carry out quenches from different starting temperatures, $T_s$, that lie above the critical temperature $T_c$. It is observed that the systems with higher $T_s$ approach the final equilibrium faster. This resembles the puzzling Mpemba effect. We present similar results also from the simulations of the two- and three- dimensional Ising model. In the case of the 2D Ising model, we show that the Mpemba effect is observed only if the starting magnetization is restricted to a value close to zero. In $d=3$, on the other hand, for both the models, the effect appears even if the initial configurations at a given $T_s$ are chosen from the full distribution of magnetization. Thus, our results are of much experimental relevance.

</details>

### [54] [Observation of an aperiodic polariton monotile](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13206)
*Sergey Alyatkin,Yaroslav V. Kartashov,Kirill Sitnik,Philipp Grigoryev,Pavlos G. Lagoudakis*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本研究通过光学方法在无机微腔中构建了由单一“爱因斯坦”单瓦片（monotile）组成的非周期准晶（quasicrystal），实验观测到激子-极化激元凝聚体（exciton-polariton condensate）的非平凡相对相位，并利用动量空间能量分辨断层扫描（energy-resolved tomography）揭示了六重对称布拉格峰（Bragg peak）和狄拉克（Dirac）类光谱特征，其同步化模式区别于周期三角晶格（triangular lattice）和彭罗斯准晶（Penrose quasicrystal）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长期以来，人们认为准周期结构（quasiperiodic structure）至少需要两种不同的瓦片（tile）才能构成，但2024年发现仅需一种单瓦片（monotile）即可构建准晶。然而，这种新型单瓦片准晶的物理实现及其中的传播相干激发（propagating coherent excitation）研究仍属空白，亟需实验探索。

Method: 研究采用光学方法在无机微腔（inorganic microcavity）中构建了由“爱因斯坦”单瓦片组成的非周期准晶，并通过非共振激发（nonresonant excitation）在每块单瓦片顶点处激发出激子-极化激元凝聚体。利用动量空间中的能量分辨断层扫描进行布拉格峰分析，并结合干涉相位重建（interferometric phase reconstruction）测量同步化模式。

Result: 实验观察到六重对称、类似石墨烯（graphene-like）结构的布拉格峰和狄拉克类光谱指纹（Dirac-like spectral fingerprints）；干涉相位重建显示一种非平凡同步化模式，该模式既不同于周期三角晶格，也不同于彭罗斯准晶。

Conclusion: 单瓦片可以转化为可编程的驱动-耗散人造材料（driven-dissipative artificial material），其中长程相干性（long-range coherence）与强制性几何非周期性（geometric aperiodicity）共存，产生区别于周期晶格和传统准晶瓦片的同步化与光谱响应。

Abstract: A plethora of unconventional localization phenomena and fractal features of linear spectrum observed in quasiperiodic structures have been accompanied by a long-standing quest for the geometrical elements and structures that permit tilings of the plane, but only in a non-periodic manner. Until 2024, it was believed that such quasiperiodic structures, or quasicrystals, could only be composed of at least two different tiles. Surprisingly, a newly discovered class of quasicrystals requires only one elementary monotile. However, its physical realization and study of propagating coherent excitations in this novel setting remained elusive. Here we optically sculpt aperiodic quasicrystals composed of "einstein" monotiles in an inorganic microcavity and observe nontrivial relative phases of the exciton-polariton condensates nonresonantly excited at the vertices of each monotile. Utilizing energy-resolved tomography in momentum-space, we reveal the formation of distinct Bragg peaks with six-fold symmetry and Dirac-like spectral fingerprints, intrinsic to the underlying graphene-like structure, while interferometric phase reconstruction shows a nontrivial synchronization pattern distinct from both periodic triangular lattices and Penrose quasicrystals. Our work demonstrates that monotiles can be converted into a programmable driven-dissipative artificial material, where long-range coherence coexists with enforced geometric aperiodicity, producing synchronization and spectral responses distinct from both periodic and conventional quasicrystalline tilings.

</details>


### [55] [Nagaoka supermetal in the particle-doped triangular Hubbard model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13837)
*Rui Cao,Xiangyue Zhang,Hui Tan,Jian-Shu Xu,Yuan-Yao He,Jianmin Yuan,Yongqiang Li*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文研究三角晶格哈伯德模型（triangular-lattice Hubbard model）在粒子掺杂下的金属态，发现一种由相互作用驱动的内禀量子态——长冈超金属（Nagaoka supermetal），其特征包括直流电阻率的亚线性温度依赖、电荷压缩率与零频频谱权重的奇异行为。通过推导有效低能模型，揭示高阶范霍夫奇点（higher-order Van Hove singularity）源于重构的色散关系，态密度的幂律发散（power-law divergence）捕捉了该超金属区（supermetallic regime）的异常性质，为非费米液体（non-Fermi liquid）态提供了新视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 掺杂莫特绝缘体（doped Mott insulators）中关联效应与几何阻挫（geometric frustration）的相互作用为奇异量子相提供了沃土，但粒子掺杂后出现的金属态本质仍不清楚，亟需阐明其内在机制。

Method: 采用三角晶格哈伯德模型进行粒子掺杂研究；通过数值计算提取直流电阻率、电荷压缩率及零频频谱权重等物理量；并构建有效低能模型（effective low-energy model）分析色散重构与高阶范霍夫奇点。

Result: 发现一种称为长冈超金属的相互作用驱动内禀量子态，其直流电阻率呈亚线性温度依赖，电荷压缩率和零频频谱权重出现奇异行为。有效模型显示，色散重构产生高阶范霍夫奇点，导致态密度出现幂律发散，从而解释了超金属区的异常性质。

Conclusion: 该研究为几何阻挫系统中的非费米液体态提供了新视角，且结论可直接在当前超冷原子（ultracold atom）实验中检验。

Abstract: While the interplay of correlations and geometric frustration in doped Mott insulators provides a fertile ground for exotic quantum phases, the nature of the metallic state emerging upon particle doping remains poorly understood. In this work, we investigate the triangular-lattice Hubbard model with particle doping and provide compelling evidence for an intrinsic, interaction-driven quantum state, which we term the Nagaoka supermetal. This state is characterized by a sublinear temperature dependence in the DC resistivity, along with singular behaviors in the charge compressibility and zero-frequency spectral weight. To understand the origin of these singular properties, we derive an effective low-energy model and demonstrate that a higher-order Van Hove singularity emerges from the reconstructed dispersion. This singularity gives rise to a power-law divergence in the density of states, capturing the anomalous properties observed in the supermetallic regime. Our findings offer a new perspective on non-Fermi liquid states in geometrically frustrated systems and are directly accessible in current ultracold atom experiments.

</details>

### [56] [First evidence of neutrino absorption on argon using $^{8}$B solar neutrinos in DEAP-3600](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12769)
*P. Adhikari,P. -A. Amaudruz,D. J. Auty,M. Batygov,B. Beltran,M. A. Bigentini,C. E. Bina,W. Bonivento,M. G. Boulay,J. Brachman,B. Broerman,J. F. Bueno,M. Cadeddu,B. Cai,M. Càrdenas-Montes,N. Cargioli,S. Cavuoti,S. Choudhary,B. T. Cleveland,R. Crampton,S. Daugherty,P. Di Stefano,G. Dolganov,L. Doria,F. A. Duncan,M. Dunford,E. Ellingwood,A. Erlandson,S. S. Farahani,N. Fatemighomi,L. Ferro,G. Fiorillo,R. J. Ford,A. Garai,P. García Abia,S. Garg,P. Giampa,D. Goeldi,P. Gorel,K. Graham,A. L. Hallin,M. Hamstra,S. Haskins,T. Hoyte,J. Hu,J. Hucker,D. Huff,T. Hugues,A. Ilyasov,B. Jigmeddorj,C. J. Jillings,G. Kaur,A. Kemp,M. Khoshraftar Yazdi,G. Killaire,M. Kuźniak,F. La Zia,M. Lai,S. Langrock,B. Lehnert,M. Lissia,L. Luzzi,I. Machulin,A. Maru,J. Mason,A. B. McDonald,T. McElroy,J. B. McLaughlin,C. Mielnichuk,L. Mirasola,S. Mohanty,A. Moharana,J. Monroe,A. Murray,M. Needs,C. Ng,G. Nieradka,G. Oliviéro,M. Olszewski,S. Pal,D. Papi,B. Park,R. Pavarani,M. Perry,V. Pesudo,T. R. Pollmann,F. Rad,C. Rethmeier,F. Retière,L. Roszkowski,R. Santorelli,F. G. Schuckman,M. Sestu,S. Seth,V. Shalamova,P. Skensved,T. Smirnova,K. Sobotkiewich,T. Sonley,J. Sosiak,J. Soukup,R. Stainforth,M. Stringer,J. Tang,P. Taylor,C. Tierney,S. Tullio,R. Turcotte-Tardif,E. Vázquez-Jáuregui,G. Vera Díaz,S. Viel,B. Vyas,J. Walding,M. Ward,S. Westerdale,R. Wormington*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: DEAP-3600探测器利用（7.29±0.05）吨·年的曝光量，首次实验观测到来自太阳$^{8}$B中微子在$^{40}$Ar上发生的电子中微子带电流相互作用（CC $ν_e$），在兴趣区（ROI）内观测到6个中微子候选事件，背景预期0.48事件，统计显著度达4.0σ，测得的能量平均截面为$(4.0^{+2.0}_{-1.6}~\mathrm{(stat)}~^{+0.8}_{-0.7}~\mathrm{(sys)})\times 10^{-41}\,\mathrm{cm}^2$，比Bhattacharya等人（2009）的理论预言高出约2.4倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验验证$^{8}$B太阳中微子在$^{40}$Ar上的电子中微子带电流相互作用（neutrino absorption, CC $ν_e$），检验现有理论截面预言（Bhattacharya, Goodman & García 2009）的准确性。

Method: 利用DEAP-3600探测器的（7.29±0.05）吨·年曝光量数据，选取10.5-13.0 MeV重建能量区间作为兴趣区（region of interest, ROI），对应入射中微子能量12.0-14.5 MeV；对高能段探测器响应非线性进行校正后，在ROI中筛选与$^{8}$B太阳中微子能谱一致的候选事件。

Result: 在ROI内观测到5个单峰（single-peak）和1个双峰（double-peak）中微子候选事件，背景预期为$0.48~^{+0.16}_{-0.15}$事件，对应背景假设的显著度为4.0σ；测得ROI内CC $ν_e$信号的能量平均截面为$(4.0~^{+2.0}_{-1.6}~\mathrm{(stat)}~^{+0.8}_{-0.7}~\mathrm{(sys)})\times 10^{-41}\,\mathrm{cm}^2$，比理论预言高约2.4倍。

Conclusion: 实验首次提供了$^{8}$B太阳中微子在$^{40}$Ar上发生CC $ν_e$相互作用的实验证据，测得截面显著高于现有理论预言，暗示当前理论计算可能需要修正。

Abstract: We report experimental evidence for electron neutrino charged-current interactions (neutrino absorption, CC $ν_e$) from $^{8}$B solar neutrinos on $^{40}$Ar using an exposure of ($7.29 \pm 0.05$) tonne$\cdot$years in the DEAP-3600 detector. A region of interest (ROI) of 10.5-13.0 MeV reconstructed energy calibrated on single-peak events, corresponding to incident neutrino energy in 12.0-14.5 MeV, is used for this measurement. We observe 5 single-peak and 1 double-peak neutrino-like events consistent with the $^{8}$B solar neutrino energy spectrum in the ROI after correcting for nonlinearities in the detector response at high energies. With an expected background of $0.48~^{+0.16}_{-0.15}$ events, the data correspond to a significance of $4.0\,σ$ with respect to the background-only hypothesis. We report an energy-averaged cross section of $(4.0~^{+2.0}_{-1.6}~\mathrm{(stat)}~^{+0.8}_{-0.7}~\mathrm{(sys)})\times 10^{-41}\,\mathrm{cm}^2$ in the ROI for the CC $ν_{e}$ signal, a factor $(2.4~^{+1.3}_{-1.0})$ higher than predicted by Bhattacharya, Goodman and García (2009).

</details>


### [57] [Search for pair production of additional neutral scalars within the Inert Doublet Model in a final state with two electrons or two muons in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV and 13.6 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13614)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文利用CMS探测器收集的质子-质子对撞数据，在惰性双希格斯模型（Inert Doublet Model, IDM）框架下首次专门搜索新标量粒子的对产生。分析基于13 TeV（138 fb⁻¹）和13.6 TeV（35 fb⁻¹）的数据，目标末态为两轻子（电子或缪子）加缺失横动量。未观测到显著信号超出，并在m_H vs. m_A平面上设置了95%置信水平的排除限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 惰性双希格斯模型（Inert Doublet Model, IDM）预言了四个额外标量玻色子（H, A, H⁺, H⁻），其中最轻的中性标量H因额外的离散对称性而稳定，可作为暗物质（dark matter）候选者。此前尚未有针对该模型预测的新标量对产生进行专门的实验搜索。

Method: 使用CMS探测器在质心能量√s = 13 TeV（积分亮度138 fb⁻¹）和13.6 TeV（积分亮度35 fb⁻¹）下收集的质子-质子对撞数据。信号过程为夸克-反夸克湮灭产生离壳Z玻色子（offshell Z boson），后者衰变为一对新标量粒子。目标末态为正好两个电荷相反、味相同的轻子（电子或缪子），伴随稳定中性标量导致的缺失横动量（missing transverse momentum），且强子活动极少。采用参数化神经网络（parameterised neural network）将信号与标准模型本底分离。

Result: 未观测到显著的事件超出。在95%置信水平（confidence level）下，对两个新中性标量H和A的产生截面设置了排除限，结果以m_H vs. m_A平面的形式给出。观测（预期）排除区域在m_H − m_A = 78（76）GeV时达到m_H = 108（106）GeV；在m_H = 70 GeV时覆盖m_H − m_A = 40–90（35–90）GeV的范围。

Conclusion: 该搜索基于惰性双希格斯模型（Inert Doublet Model）对暗物质候选者进行了排除限制，给出了迄今为止首个针对该模型新标量对产生的实验约束。结果缩小了模型中中性标量H和A的质量参数空间，为后续理论模型构建和更高统计量的实验搜索提供了参考边界。

Abstract: A first dedicated search for pair production of new scalars predicted by the Inert Doublet Model is performed using proton-proton collisions. Data were collected with the CMS detector at the CERN LHC at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV and 13.6 TeV, corresponding to integrated luminosities of 138 fb$^{-1}$ and 35 fb$^{-1}$, respectively. Within this model, four additional scalar bosons (H, A, H$^+$, and H$^-$) are predicted. Through an additional discrete symmetry, the lightest new scalar, H, is stable, rendering it a viable dark matter candidate. These candidates can originate from quark-antiquark annihilation producing an offshell Z boson that decays to a pair of the new scalars. The target final state consists of exactly two opposite-charge same-flavour leptons (electrons or muons), with missing transverse momentum due to the stable neutral scalars, and very little hadronic activity. A parameterised neural network is used to separate the signal from the standard model background. No significant excess of events is observed. Exclusion limits at 95% confidence level are set on the production cross section of the two new neutral scalars, H and A, expressed in terms of their masses, $m_\mathrm{H}$ and $m_\mathrm{A}$, in the $m_\mathrm{H}$ vs. $m_\mathrm{A}$ plane. The observed (expected) exclusion region reaches $m_\mathrm{H}$ = 108 (106) GeV for $m_\mathrm{H}-m_\mathrm{A}$ = 78 (76) GeV and at $m_\mathrm{H}$ = 70 GeV, covers the range of $m_\mathrm{H}-m_\mathrm{A}$ = 40$-$90 (35$-$90) GeV.

</details>


### [58] [Search for single vector-like quark production in opposite-sign dilepton final states in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13649)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文报道了CMS实验在13 TeV质子-质子对撞数据中寻找单产生矢量样顶夸克T（衰变为顶夸克和希格斯玻色子）的研究，未观察到超出背景预期的显著信号，并在95%置信水平上给出了T的产生截面与衰变分支比的乘积上限（2.0 pb @ 600 GeV 至 0.1 pb @ 1000 GeV），是T→tH衰变道在异号双轻子末态中的首次搜索。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准模型（Standard Model）之外的矢量样顶夸克（vector-like top quark T）是许多新物理模型（如复合希格斯模型、额外维度模型）的普遍预言，而T→tH衰变道在异号双轻子（opposite-sign dilepton）末态中此前尚未被实验搜寻过。因此，该研究旨在填补这一搜索空白，检验是否存在超出标准模型的信号。

Method: 利用CMS探测器于2016-2018年在CERN LHC收集的13 TeV质子-质子（proton-proton）对撞数据，积分亮度（integrated luminosity）达138 fb⁻¹。选取包含两个异号轻子（电子或μ子）、喷注（jets）和缺失横动量（missing transverse momentum）的末态事件，对单产生的T→tH过程进行搜索。

Result: 未发现数据与背景预期之间存在超出统计涨落的显著过剩。在95%置信水平（confidence level）上，对T的产生截面（production cross section）与其衰变分支比（decay branching fraction）的乘积设定了上限：当T质量从600 GeV变化到1000 GeV时，上限值从2.0 pb下降至0.1 pb。

Conclusion: 该搜索是T→tH衰变道在异号双轻子末态中的首次实验报道，未观测到新物理信号，并对T的产生与衰变参数给出了当前最严格的约束之一。该结果对矢量样夸克模型中的参数空间提供了重要限制。

Abstract: A search is presented for single production of a vector-like top quark T, decaying into the standard model top quark and Higgs boson, in a final state including two opposite-sign leptons (electrons or muons), jets, and missing transverse momentum. The data were recorded by the CMS experiment in proton-proton collisions at a center-of-mass energy of 13 TeV at the CERN LHC in the years 2016$-$2018, and corresponding to an integrated luminosity of up to 138 fb$^{-1}$. No excess in data over the background expectations is observed. Upper limits at 95% confidence level on the product of the T production cross section and its decay branching fraction to tH are set, ranging from 2.0 pb at a T mass of 600 GeV to 0.1 pb at 1000 GeV. This is the first search in the T $\to$ tH channel in opposite-sign dilepton final states.

</details>


### [59] [Search for charginos and neutralinos with $B-L$ $R$-parity violating decays in $\sqrt{s}=13$ TeV and $13.6$ TeV $pp$ collisions with the ATLAS detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13819)
*ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文利用ATLAS实验收集的140 fb⁻¹ (√s=13 TeV) 和56 fb⁻¹ (√s=13.6 TeV) 的质子-质子对撞数据，搜索通过R宇称破坏（R-parity violation）耦合衰变到轻子与W、Z或希格斯玻色子的chargino电弱对产生和chargino-neutralino伴随产生。数据与标准模型（Standard Model）预测一致，在95%置信水平下设置了模型无关截面上限，并在具有额外自发破缺B−L规范对称性的最小超对称标准模型（Minimal Supersymmetric Standard Model, MSSM）框架下，排除了质量在150 GeV至1100 GeV范围内、通过希格斯玻色子衰变且各轻子味分支比相等的chargino和neutralino。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超对称（Supersymmetry）是超越标准模型（Beyond the Standard Model, BSM）的重要理论扩展，但迄今缺乏实验证据。R宇称破坏（R-parity violation, RPV）超对称模型允许chargino和neutralino通过新的耦合衰变到轻子和电弱规范玻色子，包含希格斯玻色子（Higgs boson）通道的末态提供了尚未被充分探索的信号拓扑。

Method: 利用ATLAS探测器在2015–2023年收集的质子-质子对撞数据，积分亮度分别为140 fb⁻¹（√s=13 TeV）和56 fb⁻¹（√s=13.6 TeV）。选取含有三个或以上b标记喷注（b-tagged jet）以及一个或两个电子或缪子的事件，针对chargino和neutralino通过希格斯玻色子衰变的通道进行搜索。

Result: 观测数据与标准模型（Standard Model）预测一致。在95%置信水平（confidence level, CL）下给出了模型无关的BSM过程产生截面上限。在具有额外自发破缺B−L规范对称性的最小超对称标准模型（MSSM）中，假设通过希格斯玻色子衰变且各轻子味（lepton flavor）分支比相等，质量在150 GeV至1100 GeV范围内的chargino和neutralino被排除。此外还给出了味特定（flavor-specific）衰变场景下的额外排除限。

Conclusion: 该搜索未发现超越标准模型的新物理信号，对R宇称破坏超对称模型中chargino和neutralino的产生和衰变施加了迄今最严格的限制之一，尤其针对涉及希格斯玻色子的衰变通道，覆盖了150 GeV到1.1 TeV的质量范围。

Abstract: A search is performed for the electroweak pair production of charginos and associated production of a chargino and neutralino, each of which decays through an $R$-parity-violating coupling into a lepton and a $W$, $Z$, or Higgs boson. This search targets the Higgs boson decay channel of the charginos and neutralinos, using events with three or more $b$-tagged jets and one or two electrons or muons. The analyzed data corresponds to an integrated luminosity of 140 fb$^{-1}$ and 56 fb$^{-1}$ of proton-proton collision data produced by the Large Hadron Collider at center-of-mass energies of $\sqrt{s}=13$ TeV and $\sqrt{s}=13.6$ TeV respectively, collected by the ATLAS experiment between 2015 and 2023. The data are found to be consistent with predictions from the Standard Model. The results are interpreted as limits at 95% confidence level on model-independent cross sections for processes beyond the Standard Model. Limits are also set on the production of charginos and neutralinos for a Minimal Supersymmetric Standard Model with an additional $B-L$ gauge symmetry that is spontaneously broken. Charginos and neutralinos with masses between 150 GeV and 1100 GeV are excluded at 95% confidence level for a scenario in which they decay via Higgs bosons, assuming equal decay branching fractions to each lepton flavor. Additional limits are derived for flavor-specific decay scenarios.

</details>

### [60] [Bridging perturbation and variational approaches in brittle fracture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12631)
*Serafim Egorov,Antoine Sanner,Jean Sulem,Lars Pastewka,Mathias Lebihain*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对三维脆性固体中混合型（I+II+III）裂纹共面扩展的变分降阶模型，结合变分断裂力学与摄动理论，利用快速傅里叶变换和矩阵自由牛顿共轭梯度算法求解非凸约束最小化问题，通过大规模模拟揭示了无序介质中裂纹扩展的有限尺寸效应、模式混合度的影响以及从光滑到间歇性扩展的转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法难以高效且准确地模拟三维异质脆性固体中混合型加载下尖锐裂纹的共面传播，尤其是在考虑无序介质、有限尺寸效应和模式混合度的复杂相互作用时，缺乏兼具物理精度与计算效率的降阶模型。

Method: 将Francfort和Marigo（1998）的变分断裂公式与Rice（1985）的摄动理论相结合，通过最小化总能量（弹性势能与耗散能之和）求解平衡裂纹前沿构型；弹性势能及其导数通过快速傅里叶变换（Fast Fourier Transform, FFT）高效计算；非凸箱式约束最小化问题采用带信任区与基于物理预处理的矩阵自由牛顿共轭梯度（Newton conjugate gradient）算法求解，并强制执行不可逆性条件。

Result: 通过与新解析解对比验证了模型正确性；基于116,000次大规模模拟发现：（1）模型复现了从光滑到间歇性裂纹扩展的转变；（2）模式混合度对间歇性 onset 影响有限，但在混合II+III加载下诱导出准椭圆形裂纹前沿；（3）观测到依赖于系统尺度的从无序诱导弱化到增韧的交叉行为，该行为受脱钉（depinning）不稳定性的出现所控制。

Conclusion: 所提出的变分降阶模型能够有效处理三维异质脆性固体中混合型裂纹的共面传播问题，揭示了无序、有限尺寸与模式混合度对裂纹扩展行为的复杂耦合作用，为理解脆性断裂中的尺寸效应与间歇性动力学提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We present a variational reduced-order model for three-dimensional coplanar propagation of sharp cracks in heterogeneous perfectly brittle solids under mixed-mode I+II+III loading. The approach connects the variational fracture formulation of Francfort and Marigo (1998) and the perturbation theory of Rice (1985) by computing equilibrium crack-front configurations through minimization of the total energy defined as the sum of (i) the elastic potential energy, evaluated asymptotically from front deformations, and (ii) the dissipated energy, set by the fracture energy field.
  The potential energy and its derivatives are evaluated efficiently using the Fast Fourier Transform. The resulting nonconvex box-constrained minimization problem is solved with a matrix-free Newton conjugate gradient algorithm with a trust region and physics-based preconditioning, enforcing irreversibility while resolving energy barriers and long-range elastic interactions. We validate our implementation against newly derived analytical solutions. We then perform 116,000 large-scale simulations of tensile and shear crack propagation in disordered media to quantify the impact of finite-size effects, disorder intensity, and mode mixity. The simulations reproduce the transition from smooth to intermittent crack growth, and show that mode mixity has limited influence on the onset of intermittency but induces quasi-elliptic fronts in mixed II+III loading. They reveal a size-dependent crossover from disorder-induced weakening to toughening controlled by the emergence of depinning instabilities.

</details>


### [61] [On-demand steering of hyperbolic chiral polaritons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12686)
*Andrea S. Dai,Fuyang Tay,Ding Xu,Inki Lee,Noah Bussell,Daria Balatsky,Francesco L. Ruta,Emma Lian,Colin Nuckolls,Xavier Roy,James G. Analytis,Andrew J. Millis,D. N. Basov,Milan Delor*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文在天然双曲范德瓦尔斯金属MoOCl₂中实验实现了可见光至近红外波段的双曲自旋霍尔效应（hyperbolic spin Hall effect），利用新型远场泵浦-探测显微镜（pump-probe microscope）结合高动量参考场干涉，实现了对双曲等离极化激元（HPPs）的高灵敏度激发与成像，并展示了手性等离激元的传播方向可通过光 helicity 反转实现完全切换。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 亚波长架构中光偏振与传播控制是纳米光子学的基础，而利用强光学自旋-轨道相互作用（spin-orbit interaction）实现偏振选择性光操控——即光子自旋霍尔效应（photonic spin Hall effect）——是前沿方向。双曲等离极化激元（HPPs）因强局域化、介电各向异性带来的大光学自旋-轨道耦合以及射线式传播特性而备受关注，但天然材料中的双曲自旋霍尔效应（hyperbolic spin Hall effect）此前尚未被实验证实。

Method: 本研究开发了一种新型远场泵浦-探测显微镜（pump-probe microscope），通过将待测信号与高动量参考场（high-momentum reference field）进行干涉，以极高灵敏度激发并成像双曲等离极化激元（HPPs）。该方法在保持对光偏振精确控制的同时，克服了偏振选择性探测双曲材料（hyperbolic materials）的关键障碍。

Result: 在天然双曲范德瓦尔斯金属MoOCl₂中，实验证实了可见光至近红外波段的双曲自旋霍尔效应（hyperbolic spin Hall effect）。双曲等离极化激元（HPPs）和表面等离极化激元（surface plasmons）均展现出手性场（chiral fields），且其传播方向可随光 helicity 反转而完全切换。

Conclusion: 研究结果展示了手性等离激元（chiral plasmons）的按需操控，确立了天然双曲材料（natural hyperbolic materials）作为可重构纳米光子学（reconfigurable nanophotonics）和手性光-物质耦合（chiral light-matter coupling）理想组件的地位。

Abstract: Control of light polarization and propagation in sub-wavelength architectures is foundational to nanophotonic technologies. A frontier direction is to leverage strong optical spin-orbit interactions to realize polarization-selective light steering, known as the photonic spin Hall effect. In this context, hyperbolic plasmon polaritons (HPPs) are of particular interest as they offer large optical spin-orbit coupling from strong confinement and dielectric anisotropy, as well as ray-like propagation. Despite theoretical predictions, however, the hyperbolic spin Hall effect in natural materials has remained elusive. Here, we demonstrate the hyperbolic spin Hall effect in the visible and near-infrared range in the natural hyperbolic van der Waals metal MoOCl2. Enabling this discovery is a novel far-field pump-probe microscope that facilitates the launching and imaging of HPPs with exceptional sensitivity through interference with a high-momentum reference field. This approach preserves excellent control over light polarization, overcoming a key barrier to polarization-selective interrogation of hyperbolic materials. We show that both hyperbolic and surface plasmons in MoOCl2 display chiral fields, and that their propagation direction can be completely switched upon light helicity reversal. Our results demonstrate on-demand steering of chiral plasmons, firmly establishing natural hyperbolic materials as ideal components for reconfigurable nanophotonics and chiral light-matter coupling.

### [62] [Ultrafast electron dynamics of electron-irradiated graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12854)

Result: 在约400 eV入射能量下，经典点电荷与量子波包描述在背散射电子产额上存在显著差异；当入射能量高于600 eV时，量子力学效应减弱。研究明确识别出量子效应在特定能量区间发挥重要作用的范围。

Conclusion: 研究为根据动能区间选择合适的入射电子描述提供了明确指导，并确定了可用于分离纯量子背散射效应的目标实验窗口。该结果有助于在纳米制造（nanofabrication）和高分辨电子束技术（high-resolution electron-beam technologies）中理性设计二维材料。

Abstract: Electron irradiation is essential for materials characterization and modification, though the fundamental interactions between incident electrons and host materials remain under investigation. Here, we employ first-principles simulations to study electron dynamics under external electron irradiation. We quantify differences in key observables, including kinetic energy loss, secondary electron emission, and backscattered electrons, between classical and quantum mechanical descriptions of the incident electron. Around 400 eV incident energy, we identify significant differences in backscattered electron yields between classical point-charge and quantum wave-packet descriptions, whereas the quantum-mechanical effects diminish at incident energies above 600 eV. These differences highlight the critical importance of quantum effects in electron irradiation phenomena that occur in a specific energy range of the incident electron. Our results provide clear guidance for selecting appropriate incident, electron descriptions based on kinetic-energy regimes, identify a targeted experimental window for isolating quantum-only backscattering, and enable the rational design of 2D materials for nanofabrication and high-resolution electron-beam technologies.

Abstract: This work reports the fabrication and optical characterization of ultraviolet-emitting plastic scintillators based on polystyrene [-(CH2-CH(C6H5))n-] and polyvinyltoluene [-(CH2-CH(C6H4CH3))n-] doped with different concentrations of naphthalene (Naph). Overall, these results demonstrate the effectiveness of Naph as a UV emission enhancer and highlight Naph-doped PVT as a promising candidate for compact and radiation-resistant scintillation detectors.

### [65] [Apparent Ferroelectric Polarization Hysteresis and a Simple Method to Observe Piezoelectric Strain Loops with a Microphone](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13089)
*Mamoru Fukunaga*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文指出，即使使用双波法（DWM），与非铁电电容串联的额外元件也可能导致虚假的铁电D-E滞后回线。通过简单电路模型研究了假回线的特征，并在一些使用DWM的论文中发现了实际材料的可疑回线。基于逆压电效应，S-E回线比D-E回线更可靠地证明铁电性，但测量成本高。作者开发了一种利用廉价驻极体麦克风观察块体样品S-E回线的简易方法，并通过对商业陶瓷电容器的测量揭示了其看似铁电的D-E回线实际上是虚假的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: D-E滞后回线（D-E hysteresis loop）常被用于判断铁电性（ferroelectricity），但非铁电材料因电路寄生效应也可能产生虚假回线。双波法（double-wave method, DWM）虽能排除部分伪迹，但不足以完全消除串联非铁电电容带来的干扰。需要更可靠的表征手段和低成本验证方法。

Method: 采用简单电路模型研究虚假D-E回线的特征；基于逆压电效应（inverse piezoelectric effect）提出S-E回线（strain-electric field loop）作为更可靠的铁电性判据；设计了利用廉价驻极体麦克风（electret microphone）对块体样品进行S-E回线测量的简易装置，仅需对D-E回线测量电路做少量扩展。

Result: 使用该简易方法测量了商业陶瓷电容器（commercial ceramic capacitor）的S-E回线，结果显示其看似铁电的D-E回线实际上是虚假的（apparent）。

Conclusion: 单纯依赖D-E回线（即使采用双波法）判断铁电性存在误判风险；S-E回线是更可靠的判据；所提出的低成本S-E回线测量方法可有效甄别虚假铁电性，有助于避免铁电材料研究中的误判。

Abstract: Extra components in series to non-ferroelectric capacitance can cause apparent ferroelectric D-E hysteresis loops even with the double-wave method (DWM). Characteristics of fake loops are studied withsimple circuit models, and suspicious loops of actual materials are found in some papers using the DWM. Inverse piezoelectric strain also reverses along with the polarization by the electric field, and S-E loops are considered more reliable to prove ferroelectricity than the D-E loops. But measurement of S-E loops usually requires expensive instruments in contrast to D-E loops with a simple circuit. A very simple method is developed to observe S-E loops of bulk samples with an inexpensive small electret microphone and a little expansion to the circuit for D-E loops. S-E loops of a commercial ceramic capacitor by this method reveal that its D-E loops apparent.

### [66] [Ultrafast Critical Slowing of Spin Dynamics and Emergent Nonequilibrium Fano Interference in Fe3GeTe2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13121)
*Anupama Chauhan,Sidhanta Sahu,Satyabrata Bera,Tuhin Debnath,Mintu Mondal,Anamitra Mukherjee,Siddhartha Lal,N. Kamaraju*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文利用双色泵浦-探测反射率技术，研究了金属范德瓦尔斯铁磁体 Fe₃GeTe₂ 中电子、自旋与晶格自由度的耦合动力学，发现非平衡 A1g 声子 Fano 不对称性、临界慢化指数 ~0.3 以及磁-声耦合增强等行为，揭示了磁序如何调控自旋临界动力学、电子连续激发与晶格响应之间的相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Fe₃GeTe₂ 是一种具有巡游磁性（itinerant magnetism）和高可调居里温度（Curie temperature）的典型金属范德瓦尔斯铁磁体，但电子激发如何在其磁相变过程中与自旋和晶格自由度耦合仍基本未得到探索。

Method: 采用双色泵浦-探测反射率测量（two-color pump-probe reflectivity），分析时间分辨的反射率信号，用以研究电子、自旋和晶格自由度的耦合动力学。

Result: 时间分辨反射率呈现三指数弛豫（tri-exponential relaxation）：中间分量在居里温度附近出现反常，归因于层间自旋-晶格相互作用增强；最慢分量表现出显著的临界慢化（critical slowing down），指数约为 0.3，揭示了与层内自旋关联相关的非普适弛豫动力学。同时，观察到非平衡 A1g 声子 Fano 不对称性（Fano asymmetry）在铁磁相被抑制而在顺磁区反常增强，由热激活的非简并非谐衰减通道驱动。在 T_c 附近，声学应变脉冲幅度显著增强，进一步证实了稳健的磁-声耦合（magnetoelastic coupling）。

Conclusion: 结果表明，磁序在金属范德瓦尔斯铁磁体中主导了自旋临界动力学、电子连续激发与晶格响应之间的相互作用机制。

Abstract: Fe$_3$GeTe$_2$ is a prototypical metallic van der Waals ferromagnet with itinerant magnetism and a highly tunable Curie temperature, yet how electronic excitations couple to spin and lattice degrees of freedom across its magnetic transition remains largely unexplored. Here, we use two-color pump-probe reflectivity to investigate the coupled electronic, spin, and lattice dynamics. The time-resolved reflectivity exhibits a tri-exponential relaxation, in which the intermediate component shows an anomaly near the Curie temperature due to enhanced interlayer spin-lattice interactions, while the slowest component displays pronounced critical slowing down with an exponent of ~ 0.3, revealing non-universal relaxation dynamics associated with intralayer spin correlations. Furthermore, we observe an emergent nonequilibrium A1g phonon Fano asymmetry that is suppressed in the ferromagnetic phase but anomalously enhanced in the paramagnetic regime, driven by thermally activated anharmonic decay pathways that bridge the kinematic gap to a hot electronic continuum. The pronounced enhancement of the acoustic strain pulse amplitude near T$_c$ further evidences robust magnetoelastic coupling. Overall, our results reveal how magnetic order governs the interplay among critical spin dynamics, electronic continuum excitations, and lattice response in metallic van der Waals ferromagnets

### [67] [Helium Bubbles in Liquid Lead Lithium Solutions: Pressure Inhomogeneities at Interfaces and Non Ideal Mixture Effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13164)
*Edgar Alvarez-Galera,Jordi Marti,Lluis Batet*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氦在液态金属中的溶解度极低，易导致过饱和并诱发生成氦气泡。该研究旨在深入理解液态Pb-Li合金中氦气泡的形成机制，这对未来核聚变反应堆中增殖包层的设计尤为关键。

Method: 采用经典分子动力学模拟，研究一系列Pb-Li体系（包括纯Pb和纯Li的极限情况）中氦的偏析行为；通过直接力学计算评估局部压力变化，从而表征界面性质。

Result: 在多个热力学条件（温度从各组分金属熔点附近直至1021 K）下确定了界面张力与气泡半径；还探讨了曲率和合金成分对界面行为的影响。

Conclusion: 界面张力、曲率和合金成分共同调控氦气泡的稳定性与相互作用；研究结果为预测液态Pb-Li合金中氦气泡行为并优化核聚变反应堆设计提供了重要依据。

Abstract: The extremely low solubility of helium in liquid metals may lead to rapid supersaturation, promoting spontaneous formation of helium bubbles by nucleation. Once nucleated, the stability of these bubbles is governed by the properties of the helium liquid metal interface. In particular, interfacial tension between the immiscible phases controls bubble interactions and induces local pressure inhomogeneities. This work is motivated by the need of a better understanding of helium bubble formation in liquid Pb Li alloys, which are of particular relevance for the design of breeding blankets in the future nuclear fusion reactors. We employ classical molecular dynamics simulations to investigate helium segregation in a range of lead lithium systems, including the limiting cases of pure lead and pure lithium. Changes in local pressure are evaluated from direct mechanical calculations, enabling the characterization of interfacial properties. Interfacial tension and radius of the bubble are subsequently determined across multiple thermodynamic conditions, spanning temperatures starting near the melting points of the constituent metals up to 1021 K. The impact of curvature and composition of the alloy on the interfacial behaviour are also investigated.

### [68] [Structural, electronic, and optical properties of hexagonal GeSn from density functional theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13166)
*Yetkin Pulcu,János Koltai,Andor Kormányos,Guido Burkard*

Conclusion: 六方GeSn绕过了立方相所需的组成阈值限制，提供了一个高度可调的直接带隙体系，适用于红外光电子学（infrared optoelectronics）应用。

Abstract: Unlike cubic GeSn, which requires a high Sn concentration to undergo an indirect-to-direct bandgap transition, lonsdaleite (2H) germanium is an intrinsic direct-gap semiconductor. We employ first-principles density functional theory to investigate the structural, electronic, and optical properties of 2H-Ge$_{1-x}$Sn$_{x}$ random alloys in the dilute Sn regime ($x \le 0.10$). We show that 2H-Ge$_{1-x}$Sn$_{x}$ maintains a direct bandgap at the $Γ$ point across the studied composition range, exhibiting a strong bandgap bowing that shifts the fundamental absorption edge into the mid-infrared. Evaluation of the optical transition matrix elements reveals a giant polarization anisotropy dictated by spin-orbit coupling. The fundamental transition is strongly dipole-allowed for light polarized perpendicular to the crystal $c$-axis, an optical selection rule that is robustly preserved despite the random alloy disorder breaking the symmetry. These results demonstrate that hexagonal GeSn bypasses the compositional threshold limitations of the cubic phase, providing a highly tunable direct-gap system for infrared optoelectronics.

### [69] [Magnesium-graphene interphase boundaries created by high-pressure torsion enhance hydrogen storage kinetics:Mechanisms and significance of activation energy and frequency factor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13184)
*Runchen Zhou,Payam Edalati,Anthony Alhayek,Shivam Dangwal,Marc Novelli,Md. Amirul Islam,Baran Bidyut Saha,Thierry Grosdidier,Kaveh Edalati*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用高压扭转（high-pressure torsion, HPT）技术对纯镁及镁-石墨烯复合材料进行剧烈塑性变形（severe plastic deformation），以引入大量晶界（grain boundaries）和相界（interphase boundaries）。通过动力学建模（kinetic modeling）和Kissinger分析方法定量评估速率控制机制及活化能（activation energy）与频率因子（frequency factor）的变化。

Conclusion: 通过剧烈塑性变形（severe plastic deformation）进行相界工程（interphase boundary engineering）可显著增强储氢材料的动力学性能与空气稳定性，其本质在于增加界面作为氢扩散和金属/氢化物非均匀形核（heterogeneous nucleation）的位点，从而提高频率因子而非改变活化能。

Abstract: A strategy to overcome sluggish hydrogenation/dehydrogenation of magnesium is demonstrated by creating magnesium-graphene interphase boundaries via high-pressure torsion (HPT). HPT reduces the grain size of pure magnesium from 1 mm to 850 nm, with 70% of grain boundaries having high misorientation angles. Graphene addition leads to even finer grain sizes of 10-500 nm with a bimodal morphology. The magnesium-graphene composites exhibit superior kinetics at 623 K while maintaining high air resistance. Kinetic modeling reveals that the rate-controlling mechanism transits from interfacial reaction in coarse-grained magnesium to atomic diffusion in magnesium-graphene nanocomposites. Kissinger analysis shows that the activation energy for hydrogen desorption remains unchanged at 145 +/- 2 kJ/mol, regardless of the presence of grain or interphase boundaries. However, the frequency factor (number of successful attempts to overcome the activation energy) increases with the generation of interfaces, which serve as sites for hydrogen diffusion and heterogeneous metal/hydride nucleation. These findings highlight the impact of interphase boundary engineering via severe plastic deformation for enhancing the kinetics and air resistance of hydrogen storage materials.

### [70] [Conditional probability density functional theory for solids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13226)

Method: 采用条件概率密度泛函理论（CP-DFT），将其应用于具有周期性边界条件的扩展材料体系，对弱关联材料（Na, Si）和强关联Kagome材料CsV₃Sb₅进行计算分析。

Conclusion: CP-DFT能够扩展到周期性扩展体系，并在弱关联体系中验证有效；对于强关联系统，CP-DFT可揭示标准DFT无法描述的关联效应，是一种有前景的强关联系统研究方法。

Abstract: A recently developed approach, conditional probability density functional theory (CP-DFT), yields direct access to the exchange-correlation hole of a system, an important correlation function that is not available from any standard DFT calculation. We present the first results for extended materials with periodic boundary conditions. We demonstrate that CP-DFT works on weakly correlated materials (Na, Si). When applied to the prototypical Kagome material $CsV_3Sb_5$, we find $d$-orbital correlations that are not captured by standard DFT. Such distribution leads to a positive finding probability between two separated electrons and an enhanced charge density wave signal, suggesting a useful approach for strongly correlated systems.

Result: 缺陷湮灭（defect annihilation）经历三个连续阶段：相子翻转（phason flip）、盾状缺陷的聚集（aggregation）与分解（decomposition）。这些转变由势能梯度（potential energy gradients）驱动，并伴随结构对称性（structural symmetry）的提升。

Abstract: Understanding defect evolution is essential to the structural stability of quasicrystals, yet the kinetics of defect repair remain poorly understood. Here, by combining the string method and the spring pair method, we determine the minimum energy path from defective to defect-free dodecagonal quasicrystals using a particle model with the Lennard-Jones-Gauss potential. We find that defect annihilation proceeds via three stages: phason flip, aggregation and decomposition of shield-like defects. These sequential transformations are driven by potential energy gradients and accompanied by an increase in structural symmetry. The three stages act synergistically in promoting defect annihilation, offering new insights into the microscopic repair mechanisms of quasicrystals.

### [73] [Multiple Softening Q-vectors Driving a Cascade of CDW Phases in $\mathrm{1T-VSe}_{2}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13458)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 原始1T-VSe₂单层存在多个虚频声子模式，对应主导不稳定波矢；第一代CDW相中仍有部分结构保持动力学不稳定，进一步发生对称性降低扭曲（symmetry-lowering distortions）形成更大的超结构。多种不同的中间CDW态通过不同路径最终汇聚到同一个低能稳定的$2\sqrt{3}\times4$构型，且这些路径对应的终态能量几乎简并。

Conclusion: 研究建立了统一的声子驱动级联机制（phonon-driven cascade mechanism）来解释单层1T-VSe₂中的层级式CDW形成，为理解低维量子材料中竞争有序相（competing ordered phases）提供了系统性的理论框架。

Abstract: Charge density wave (CDW) formation in two-dimensional materials is governed by complex competing lattice instabilities that remain incompletely understood. Here, we investigate the structural evolution of monolayer $\mathrm{1T-VSe}_{2}$ using first-principles electronic and phonon calculations. The pristine phase exhibits several imaginary-frequency phonon modes associated with dominant instability wave vectors $\mathrm{Q}_{CDW}$, which generate the first-generation CDW phases. Subsequent phonon analyses reveal that several of these intermediate structures remain dynamically unstable and undergo further symmetry-lowering distortions into larger superstructures. Through iterative phonon-driven relaxations, we identify multiple transformation pathways that converge toward the same low-energy $2\sqrt{3}\times4$ CDW configuration. Although these pathways originate from distinct intermediate CDW states, they ultimately reach nearly degenerate energetically stable phases, demonstrating that different phonon-driven routes can lead to the same ground-state configuration. The results establish a unified phonon-driven cascade mechanism for hierarchical CDW formation in monolayer $\mathrm{1T-VSe}_{2}$ and provide a systematic framework for understanding competing ordered phases in low-dimensional quantum materials.

Abstract: Further development of nuclear power plant technology relies heavily on materials durability under operating conditions. Estimating the materials performance in the operando tests is crucial. Experimental nanomechanical analysis was supported by MD simulations. The results indicate that the hardness of the amorphous coating experiences a gradual, constant decrease with temperature, while the Young modulus value remains constant in the whole temperature range. Observed phenomena confirm the increasing plasticity of the material and it is postulated to be related to the bond-switching mechanism that accelerates at high temperatures. The post-mortem transmission electron microscopy characterization confirmed that the loaded material was non-crystalline over the entire range of the indentation temperatures. The thermal stability of the structure was further studied in-situ up to 1050C by X-ray diffraction. The implemented methodology allowed us to follow the dynamic process of phase transitions occurring in the material above 650C. First, thermally activated crystallization was observed at 700C. Intermediate alumina phases were present up to 950C, while above this temperature, exclusively the thermodynamically stable alpha-Al2O3 was observed. The in-situ high-temperature characterization of the evolution of thin films boosts the understanding of the application limits of the coating systems at elevated temperatures. The added value is that the paper demonstrates the potential usefulness of combining high-temperature techniques to characterize the complete behavior of thin films at elevated temperatures.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RuO₂被视作金属交变磁体（metallic altermagnet）的典型候选材料，在高速高能效自旋电子学（spintronics）领域具有潜在应用价值，但其磁基态（magnetic ground state）因相互矛盾的实验报道而存在持续争议。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论结合动力学平均场理论（density functional theory combined with dynamical mean-field theory, DFT+DMFT）方法研究RuO₂中的电子关联效应。

Result: DFT+DMFT捕获了关键的动力学关联效应，得到的光谱函数和光学电导率与实验定量吻合；RuO₂处于顺磁-交变磁相边界（paramagnetic-altermagnetic phase boundary）和巡游-局域化转变（itinerant-localized crossover）附近，磁基态高度易受外部扰动影响；约0.5%的最小压缩应变即可驱动系统进入交变磁相。

Conclusion: 动力学关联效应（dynamical correlation effects）是RuO₂高度可调磁基态的关键驱动力，该发现阐明了已有实验观测相互矛盾的根源。

Abstract: RuO$_2$ has been regarded as a prototypical candidate for metallic altermagnet, offering a potential platform for high-speed and high-efficiency spintronics. However, the magnetic ground state of RuO$_2$ remains a topic of active debate due to conflicting experimental reports. In this work, we investigate the effect of electron correlations in RuO$_2$ using density functional theory combined with dynamical mean-field theory (DFT+DMFT). In contrast to previous DFT-based studies, DFT+DMFT captures essential dynamical correlation effects, yielding spectral functions and optical conductivities in excellent quantitative agreement with experiments, and further reveals that RuO$_2$ resides in the close vicinity of both the paramagnetic-altermagnetic phase boundary and the itinerant-localized crossover, rendering the magnetic ground state highly susceptible to external perturbations. Indeed, even a minimal compressive strain of $\sim$0.5% is sufficient to drive the system into an altermagnetic phase. These findings elucidate the origin of the conflicting experimental observations and reveal that dynamical correlation effects are the key driving force behind the highly tunable magnetic ground state of RuO$_2$.

Abstract: Dopant distribution in two-dimensional semiconductors is typically assumed to be stochastic, limiting deterministic defect engineering. Here, we show that non-equilibrium growth kinetics can be harnessed to define dopant-driven strain architectures in vanadium-doped WS$_2$ monolayers. Using synchrotron X-ray fluorescence, we identify preferential vanadium incorporation, anti-correlated with tungsten content, along crystallographic bisectors. An adsorption-growth-diffusion model with a single kinetic parameter quantitatively captures the dopant segregation arising from preferential corner adsorption and limited diffusion during chemical vapor deposition growth. Hyperspectral Raman imaging demonstrates mechanically induced vibrational responses, revealing localized tensile strain ($\varepsilon \approx0.70\%$) channels associated with the anisotropic dopant distribution. This regime is marked by the depletion of W-site-sensitive in-plane modes and the emergence of a localized $J2$ mode (210~cm$^{-1}$), which our ab-initio calculations attribute to antiphase V$-$V oscillations. These findings establish kinetic segregation as a route to deterministic chemical and strain architectures in 2D semiconductors, enabling programmable defect landscapes and strain engineering during synthesis.

### [78] [OpenAaaS: An Open Agent-as-a-Service Framework for Distributed Materials-Informatics Research](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13618)
*Peng Kang,Bixuan Li,Xiaoya Huang,Shuo Shi,Weiqiao Zhou,Zhen Li,Yu Liu,Lei Zheng*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 针对材料科学领域“最后一英里”问题——缺乏跨机构安全整合模型与数据的基础设施，本文提出OpenAaaS，一个基于“代码流动、数据静止”（code flows, data stays still）原则的开源分层分布式Agent-as-a-Service框架，通过主智能体（Master Agent）规划任务、子智能体（Sub-agent）执行近数据计算，在保障数据主权的前提下实现跨域多智能体协作。两则案例验证（文献分析Agent评分4.66/5.0；高熵合金数据库服务）表明该框架可有效支持苛刻服役环境下材料智能设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管材料基因组计划催生了众多集中式平台（SaaS/PaaS/IaaS），且大语言模型（LLMs）与自主智能体（autonomous agents）为科学研究提供了强大推理能力，但存在关键的“最后一英里”问题：缺乏能够跨机构边界安全组合这些模型与数据资产的组织性基础设施（organizational infrastructure）。高性能结构/功能材料（如高温合金、耐辐射钢、耐蚀涂层）的开发依然依赖长期迭代、高领域知识与机制复杂性，超出了单体智能体系统和传统集中式平台的能力范围。

Method: 提出开源分层分布式Agent-as-a-Service框架OpenAaaS，核心原则为“代码流动，数据静止”（code flows, data stays still）。主智能体（Master Agent）负责复杂研究任务的规划与分解，无需直接访问子智能体的数据与计算资源；子智能体（Sub-agent）作为近数据执行节点部署，保留对本地数据集、专有算法与专用硬件的完全主权，确保原始数据不离其所属域。

Result: 案例一：AlphaAgent——基于证据的材料文献分析执行器，在深度分析问题上相比单次检索增强生成（single-pass RAG）基线达到4.66/5.0评分。案例二：超大规模六元高熵合金描述符数据库服务——在严格数据主权约束下实现了安全的近数据执行与特定领域科学工作流。

Conclusion: OpenAaaS通过智能体集体（agent collectives）建立了一条通往“有组织的研究”（organized research）的原则性路径，为下一代材料智能设计平台提供了可扩展的基础框架。

Abstract: The Materials Genome Initiative catalyzed the proliferation of centralized platforms--SaaS, PaaS, and IaaS--that aggregate computational and experimental resources for accelerated materials discovery. In parallel, breakthroughs in large language models (LLMs) and autonomous agents have created powerful new reasoning capabilities for scientific research. Yet a critical "last mile" problem remains: while we possess world-class models and vast repositories of materials data, we lack the organizational infrastructure to compose these capabilities securely across institutional boundaries. The development of structural and functional materials for harsh service environments--high-temperature alloys, radiation resistant steels, corrosion-resistant coatings--remains characterized by long-term iteration, mechanistic complexity, and high domain expertise--demands that exceed both monolithic agent systems and traditional centralized platforms. To address this gap we propose OpenAaaS, an open-source hierarchical and distributed Agent-as-a-Service framework that enables organized multi-agent collaboration for intelligent materials design. OpenAaaS is built on a single foundational principle: code flows, data stays still. A Master Agent plans and decomposes complex research tasks without requiring direct access to subordinate agents' managed data and computational resources. Sub-agents, deployed as near-data execution nodes, retain full sovereignty over local datasets, proprietary algorithms, and specialized hardware. This architecture guarantees that raw data never leaves its domain of origin while enabling cross-scale, cross-domain secure integration of previously isolated materials intelligence silos. We validate the framework through two representative case studies: (i) AlphaAgent, an evidence-grounded materials literature analysis executor that achieves 4.66/5.0 on deep analytical questions against single-pass RAG baselines; and (ii) an ultra-large-scale hexa-high-entropy alloy descriptor database service that demonstrates secure near-data execution and domain-specific scientific workflows under strict data-sovereignty constraints. OpenAaaS establishes a principled pathway toward "organized research" via agent collectives, offering a scalable foundation for next-generation materials intelligent design platforms. All source code is available at https://github.com/Wolido/OpenAaaS.

### [79] [Layer thickness dependent band gap of MBE grown single- to few-layer MoS$_{2}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13637)
*Maciej Bazarnik,Thorsten Deilmann,Marta Przychodnia,Anika Schlenhoff*

TL;DR: 本文通过扫描隧道谱学（scanning tunnelling spectroscopy）测量了分子束外延（molecular beam epitaxy）生长在石墨烯/Ir(111)上的1–5层MoS₂的能带结构。发现随着层数增加，带隙急剧减小甚至低于体材料值；导带钉扎效应在4层以上消失。结合密度泛函理论（density functional theory）与GW计算表明，样品生长条件引入了额外的屏蔽效应（screening）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过渡金属二硫属化物（transition metal dichalcogenides）作为二维半导体在器件应用中日益重要，其能带工程尤为关键。MoS₂的带隙随层数变化（从体材料的间接带隙转变为单层的直接带隙），且实验已证实从体材料减薄至双层时，间接跃迁出现强蓝移。然而，对于更薄层数范围内带隙演化行为的精确实验测量仍待深入，尤其是生长条件可能引入的额外效应尚不清楚。

Method: 采用分子束外延（molecular beam epitaxy, MBE）在石墨烯/Ir(111)衬底上原位生长1–5层的MoS₂样品；利用扫描隧道谱学（scanning tunnelling spectroscopy, STS）测量不同层数样品的能带结构；将实验结果与密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）和GW计算进行对比分析。

Result: 发现MoS₂的带隙随层数增加而急剧减小，甚至低于体材料的带隙值；导带钉扎（conduction band pinning）效应在层数超过4层时消失。

Conclusion: 实验数据与DFT及GW计算对比表明，样品生长条件引入了额外的屏蔽效应（screening），这是导致带隙异常减小及导带钉扎行为变化的原因。

Abstract: In light of the rise of transition metal dichalcogenides as 2D semiconductors for device applications, band engineering becomes very important from an application point of view. In many of these materials, such as the canonical example of MoS$_{2}$, the semiconductor band gap depends on the layer number. It changes from indirect to direct as it evolves from a bulk semiconductor to a monolayer. Interestingly, it was predicted and experimentally confirmed that, by thinning the material from bulk to a bilayer, the indirect transition shows a strong blue-shift. Here, we present the results of scanning tunnelling spectroscopy measurements on MoS$_{2}$ that has been grown \textit{in situ} via molecular beam epitaxy on graphene on Ir(111) at thicknesses ranging from 1 to 5 layers. We find a drastic decrease of the band gap with increasing layer number, to values even below the band gap in bulk. We also observe that the pinning of the conduction band vanishes above 4 layers. Comparing our experimental data with density functional theory and \textit{GW} calculations indicates that an additional screening is introduced by the sample growth conditions.

### [80] [High-Pressure XRD Study of Ti-3Al-2.5V Titanium Alloy: Intermediate Transition Pressure and Composition Trends in Ti-Al-V Alloys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13658)

Method: 采用高压 X 射线衍射（X-ray diffraction）实验，使用不同的压力传递介质（pressure-transmitting media），对 Ti-3Al-2.5V、纯 Ti 和 Ti-6Al-4V 三种材料进行测量，并基于状态方程（equation-of-state）分析体弹模量。
