Conclusion: 合金化主要影响相变压力而非压缩性（compressibility），弹性性质与相稳定性之间存在解耦（decoupling）关系，表明可通过调节成分来调控 Ti-Al-V 基合金的高压相变行为。 

Abstract: High-pressure X-ray diffraction experiments were performed on Ti-Al-V alloys to investigate the effect of composition on structural stability, focusing on Ti-3Al-2.5V and comparing with pure Titanium and Ti-6Al-4V. Measurements using different pressure-transmitting media show a phase transition in Ti-3Al-2.5V at 17-19 GPa, intermediate between pure Ti (5-10 GPa) and Ti-6Al-4V (~30 GPa). Despite variations arising from the choice of pressure medium, the transition pressure shows a clear and systematic increase with higher Al and V content. Equation-of-state analysis indicates that the bulk modulus remains nearly unchanged across compositions. This suggests a decoupling between elastic properties and phase stability, with alloying primarily affecting the transition pressure rather than compressibility. These results highlight the role of composition in tuning high-pressure phase transformations in Ti-Al-V based alloys.

### [81] [Nonlinear dynamic elastic moduli from equilibrium stress fluctuations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13703)
*F. E. Garbuzov,Y. M. Beltukov*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该论文推导了适用于线性和非线性动态模量（linear and nonlinear dynamic moduli）的瞬态时间关联函数（transient-time correlation function）表达式，可从平衡态分子动力学（equilibrium molecular dynamics）模拟中计算这些模量，填补了非线性时变模量缺乏涨落公式的空白。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 弹性模量与粘弹性模量的涨落公式（fluctuation formulas）允许从平衡态分子动力学模拟中计算这些模量，无需显式的非平衡形变协议。然而，尽管准静态模量（quasi-static moduli）和线性动态模量（linear dynamic moduli）的涨落公式已建立完善，但控制有限时变应变下非简谐粘弹性响应（anharmonic viscoelastic response）的非线性时变模量（nonlinear time-dependent moduli）尚无对应的涨落公式。

Method: 从无旋运动的DOLLS/SLLOD运动方程出发，推导了线性和非线性动态模量的瞬态时间关联函数表达式。所得公式涉及应力张量（stress tensor）与玻恩-动能项（Born-kinetic terms）的平衡时间关联。

Result: 推导出的涨落公式在适当极限下能够恢复已知的准静态模量和线性动态模量的结果。

Conclusion: 该工作首次建立了非线性时变模量的涨落公式，拓展了涨落公式方法在非线性粘弹性响应研究中的适用范围。

Abstract: Fluctuation formulas for elastic and viscoelastic moduli allow their computation from equilibrium molecular dynamics simulations, avoiding explicit nonequilibrium deformation protocols. While such expressions are well established for the quasi-static moduli, and also the linear dynamic moduli, no fluctuation formula exists for the nonlinear time-dependent moduli that govern anharmonic viscoelastic response under finite time-dependent strains. In this work we derive transient-time correlation function expressions for both the linear and the nonlinear dynamic moduli, starting from the DOLLS/SLLOD equations of motion for irrotational motion. The resulting formulas involve equilibrium time correlations of the stress tensor and Born-kinetic terms, and they recover the known quasi-static and linear dynamic results in the appropriate limits.

### [82] [Giant optical spin-orbit interactions in ferroelectric van der Waals waveguides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13707)
*Ding Xu,Saeed Rahmanian Koshkaki,Vicente Galicia,Chun-Ying Huang,Victoria Quirós-Cordero,Jakhangirkhodja A. Tulyagankhodjaev,André Koch Liston,Daniel G. Chica,Emma Lian,Amirhosein Amini,Yongseok Hong,Taketo Handa,P. James Schuck,Xiaoyang Zhu,Xavier Roy,Arkajit Mandal,Milan Delor*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光学自旋-轨道相互作用（optical spin-orbit interactions, SOI）为实现片上偏振控制和光束转向提供了途径。然而，在亚微米尺度上实现足够强的光学SOI和非线性效应——这是密集光子集成（dense photonic integration）的前提——仍然是一个未解决的挑战。

Method: 采用高双折射的范德华（van der Waals, vdW）波导作为芯片兼容平台，重点研究铁电半导体NbOI₂，该材料具有创纪录的光学非线性和介电各向异性（dielectric anisotropy）。使用飞秒光学显微镜（femtosecond optical microscopy）成像光传播和谐波转换，超越全内反射（total internal reflection）极限。基于微观光-物质相互作用模型（microscopic light-matter interaction model）进行定量分析。

Result: 在NbOI₂薄片波导中实现了亚微米尺度的巨大光学自旋分裂（optical spin-splitting），通过光学自旋霍尔效应（optical spin Hall effect）实现了光学自旋电流的空间分离，与微观模型定量一致。利用光学自旋-动量锁定（optical spin-momentum locking）实现了偏振控制波导转向。在多种vdW波导中验证了观察结果，并经验性地确认了介电各向异性与几何自旋分裂之间的标度律（scaling law）。

Conclusion: 高各向异性范德华波导可作为密集集成光-自旋电子技术（opto-spintronic technologies）的理想平台，克服了亚微米尺度上光学SOI和非线性效应不足的关键限制。

Abstract: Optical spin-orbit interactions (SOI) link photonic spin to momentum, offering a route toward on-chip polarization control and beam steering. Nevertheless, achieving sufficient optical SOI and nonlinearities on sub-micrometer scales - a prerequisite for dense photonic integration - remains an outstanding challenge. Here, we show that highly birefringent van der Waals (vdW) waveguides provide an ideal, chip-compatible platform to address this limitation. We focus on the ferroelectric semiconductor NbOI2, which exhibits record optical nonlinearities and dielectric anisotropy. Using femtosecond optical microscopy, we image light propagation and harmonic conversion beyond the total internal reflection barrier over tens of micrometers in NbOI2 slab waveguides. We report giant optical spin-splitting through the optical spin Hall effect, which facilitates spatial separation of optical spin currents on sub-micrometer scales, in quantitative agreement with a microscopic light-matter interaction model. We further leverage optical spin-momentum locking to realize polarization-controlled waveguide steering. We generalize these observations across various vdW waveguides and empirically confirm a scaling law linking dielectric anisotropy to geometric spin-splitting. Our results establish highly anisotropic vdW waveguides as an ideal platform for densely integrated opto-spintronic technologies.

</details>


### [83] [Chiral molecule-induced contributions to ferromagnetic resonance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13805)
*Jurgen Lindner,Pedro Contreras-Gallardo,Abhishek Singh,Ruslan Salikhov,Anna Semisalova,Olav Hellwig,Rodolfo Gallardo,Anna Lewandowska-Andralojc,Kilian Lenz,Aleksandra Lindner*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过宽带铁磁共振谱（broadband ferromagnetic resonance spectroscopy）实验，研究了手性分子界面（chiral molecular interfaces）对垂直磁各向异性Co/Ni多层膜磁化动力学的影响。实验未观察到手性环境引起的共振场或线宽变化；通过发展区分平衡态自由能修正与非平衡态CISS自旋扭矩（spin torque）的宏自旋描述（macrospin description），提出了从铁磁共振实验中分离手性界面能量修正与扭矩驱动动力学效应的判别标准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性诱导自旋选择性（chirality-induced spin selectivity, CISS）领域虽已广泛探讨静态磁性质，但手性对动态磁响应（dynamic magnetic response）的影响仍未被充分研究。本文旨在填补这一空白，系统探究手性分子界面如何影响具有垂直磁各向异性（perpendicular magnetic anisotropy, PMA）的Co/Ni多层膜的磁化动力学（magnetization dynamics）。

Method: 采用宽带铁磁共振谱（broadband ferromagnetic resonance spectroscopy）比较裸膜（bare/reference films）与分子功能化杂化样品（molecule-functionalized hybrid samples）的磁化动力学行为。基于实验结果，发展了一种宏自旋描述（macrospin description），用于区分两种机制：一是通过改变自由能景观（free-energy landscape）及有效场（effective field）影响共振条件的平衡态修正（MIPAC型效应），二是通过类阻尼非平衡扭矩（damping-like non-equilibrium torques）改变有效阻尼率的非平衡态CISS自旋扭矩。

Result: 实验方面：与裸膜参照样品相比，分子功能化杂化样品的共振场（resonance field）和线宽（linewidth）均未观察到可归因于手性环境（chiral environment）的可测量变化。理论分析表明：平衡态修正主要通过改变自由能景观及有效场来移动共振条件；非平衡态类阻尼扭矩则提供了改变有效阻尼率（effective damping rate）的独立通道。

Conclusion: 本文建立了在铁磁共振（ferromagnetic resonance, FMR）实验中清晰区分手性界面诱导的能量修正（chiral-interface-induced energy modifications）与扭矩驱动动力学效应（torque-driven dynamical effects）的判别标准。该理论框架为后续研究手性分子界面在磁化动力学中的作用提供了方法论基础。

Abstract: Despite extensive research on chirality-driven spin selectivity, most studies have focused on static magnetic properties, while the influence of chirality on the dynamic magnetic response remains largely unexplored. Here, we investigate how chiral molecular interfaces affect magnetization dynamics in thin Co/Ni multilayers with perpendicular magnetic anisotropy using broadband ferromagnetic resonance spectroscopy. A comparison between bare (reference) films and molecule-functionalized (hybrid) samples reveals no measurable changes in either the resonance field or the linewidth that could be attributed to the presence of the chiral environment. Motivated by our findings we develop a macrospin description that distinguishes equilibrium modifications of the magnetic free-energy landscape (MIPAC-type effects) from non-equilibrium, CISS-induced spin torques. Our analysis shows that equilibrium modifications primarily shift the resonance condition via changes to the free energy landscape and thereby the effective field, whereas damping-like non-equilibrium torques provide a distinct channel for varying the effective damping rate. This approach establishes clear criteria for disentangling chiral-interface-induced energy modifications from torque-driven dynamical effects in ferromagnetic resonance experiments.

</details>

### [84] [Deep Learning as Neural Low-Degree Filtering: A Spectral Theory of Hierarchical Feature Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13612)
*Yatin Dandi,Matteo Vilucchio,Luca Arnaboldi,Hugo Tabanelli,Florent Krzakala*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出神经低度滤波（Neural Low-Degree Filtering, Neural LoFi），一种基于梯度训练的风格化极限，将层级特征学习显式化为迭代谱过程。该框架解耦了各层动力学，每层基于当前表示选择与标签存在最大可访问低度相关（low-degree correlation）的方向，从而为深度学习的多层特征学习提供了可解的替代机制和核空间解释，并通过实验验证其优于懒训练（lazy regime）基线、恢复有意义的滤波器，且与实际数据上早期梯度下降的特征发现对齐。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度神经网络如何从数据中学习有用的内部表示仍是深度学习理论中的核心开放问题。现有理论框架（如懒训练 regime）难以解释多层特征学习（multi-layer feature learning）的层级涌现机制，需要一种可解析描述特征逐层选择与构建过程的数学框架。

Method: 引入神经低度滤波（Neural LoFi），一种梯度训练的风格化极限（stylized limit），其中层级特征学习被显式化为迭代谱过程（iterative spectral procedure）。在该极限下，各层动力学解耦：给定当前表示，下一层选择与标签存在最大可访问低度相关（maximal accessible low-degree correlation）的方向。该方法同时提供了核空间（kernel-space）解释。

Result: 理论层面，Neural LoFi预测了表示逐层选择的机制，解释了给定样本复杂度（sample complexity）下概念涌现的方式，并给出了深度通过低度组合性（low-degree compositionality）从旧特征逐步构建新特征的具体机制。实验层面，在全连接和卷积架构上，Neural LoFi优于懒随机特征基线（lazy random-feature baselines），恢复了有意义的结构化滤波器，并与实际数据集上早期梯度下降的特征发现对齐。

Conclusion: Neural LoFi为超越懒训练 regime 的多层特征学习提供了数学显式框架，揭示了低度相关性在层级特征构建中的核心作用，并为理解深度学习的特征涌现与样本效率提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: Understanding how deep neural networks learn useful internal representations from data remains a central open problem in the theory of deep learning. We introduce Neural Low-Degree Filtering (Neural LoFi), a stylized limit of gradient-based training in which hierarchical feature learning becomes an explicit iterative spectral procedure. In this limit, the dynamics at each layer decouple: given the current representation, the next layer selects directions with maximal accessible low-degree correlation to the label. This yields a tractable surrogate mechanism for deep learning, together with a natural kernel-space interpretation. Neural LoFi provides a mathematically explicit framework for studying multi-layer feature learning beyond the lazy regime. It predicts how representations are selected layer by layer, explains how emergence of concepts arises with given sample complexity,and gives a concrete mechanism by which depth progressively constructs new features from old ones through low-degree compositionality. We complement the theory with mechanistic experiments on fully connected and convolutional architectures, showing that Neural LoFi improves over lazy random-feature baselines, recovers meaningful structured filters, and predicts representations aligned with early gradient-descent feature discovery with real datasets.

</details>


### [85] [Reducing cross-sample prediction churn in scientific machine learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13826)
*Gordan Prastalo,Kevin Maik Jablonka*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出“跨样本预测差异（cross-sample prediction churn）”概念，指同一模型在不同训练数据采样下对同一测试样本预测标签的不一致性。在9个化学基准测试中，两个独立引导采样训练的分类器在聚合准确率上差异很小（1.3–4.2个百分点），但对8.0–21.8%的测试分子给出不同标签。标准参数侧方法（深度集成、MC Dropout、随机权重平均）无法降低该差异，而数据侧方法（K-引导装袋和本文提出的双引导（twin-bootstrap）方法）可有效降低。作者主张科学机器学习基准报告应将跨样本预测差异作为与预测性能并列的指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 科学机器学习（scientific machine learning）报告仅关注预测性能（predictive performance），但未检验同一预测是否能在不同的训练数据采样下重现，导致模型可靠性评估存在盲区。

Method: 在9个化学基准数据集上，训练两个独立引导采样（bootstrap）的分类器，定义同一测试样本上两个分类器预测标签的不一致性为跨样本预测差异（cross-sample prediction churn）。对比参数侧方法（深度集成、MC Dropout、随机权重平均）与数据侧方法（K-引导装袋及本文提出的双引导方法）对该指标的缓解效果。双引导方法将两个网络在独立引导采样上联合训练，并添加对称KL散度（sym-KL consistency loss）作为一致性损失。

Result: 两个独立引导采样训练的分类器在聚合准确率上差异仅为1.3–4.2个百分点，但对8.0–21.8%的测试分子标签不一致。参数侧方法无法降低跨样本预测差异；K-引导装袋（K-bootstrap bagging）在不损失准确率的情况下将差异率削减40–54%（但需要K倍ERM计算量）。双引导（twin-bootstrap）方法在匹配2倍ERM计算量时，相比装袋（K=2）进一步降低中位45%的差异。

Conclusion: 跨样本预测差异应作为与预测性能并列的指标纳入科学机器学习基准报告，因为参数侧方法与数据侧方法在聚合准确率这一指标上无法区分，而二者恰恰在跨样本预测差异上表现不同。

Abstract: Scientific machine learning reports predictive performance. It does not report whether the same prediction would survive a different draw of training data. Across $9$ chemistry benchmarks, two classifiers trained on independent bootstraps of the same training set agree on aggregate accuracy to within $1.3\text{--}4.2$ percentage points but disagree on the class label of $8.0\text{--}21.8\%$ of test molecules. We call this gap \emph{cross-sample prediction churn}. The standard parameter-side techniques (deep ensembles, MC dropout, stochastic weight averaging) do not reduce this gap; two data-side methods do. The first is $K$-bootstrap bagging, which cuts the rate $40\text{--}54\%$ on every dataset at no accuracy cost ($K{\times}$-ERM compute). The second is \emph{twin-bootstrap}, our proposal: two networks trained jointly on independent bootstraps with a sym-KL consistency loss between their predictions, which at matched $2{\times}$-ERM compute reduces churn a further median $45\%$ beyond bagging-$K{=}2$. Cross-sample prediction churn deserves a column alongside predictive performance in scientific-ML benchmark reports, because without it the parameter-side and data-side methods are indistinguishable on the metric they actually differ on.

</details>

### [86] [Incommensurate Spin-Density Waves in a Frustrated Maple-Leaf Lattice Ferromagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12592)
*Paul L. Ebert,Yasir Iqbal,Alexander Wietek*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过精确对角化（exact diagonalization）和变分计算，研究了枫叶晶格（maple-leaf lattice）上自旋1/2海森堡模型（Heisenberg model）中铁磁性的破坏方式，发现铁磁边界不存在零场自旋向列相（spin-nematic phase），但存在不可公度自旋密度波（incommensurate spin-density-wave）区域；在红宝石晶格（ruby-lattice）边界上，一个投影Z2 Ansatz能较好地重现有限尺度的能量和自旋关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受Na₂Mn₃O₇中混合铁磁-反铁磁相互作用的启发，研究枫叶晶格上海森堡模型中铁磁性如何在混合相互作用下被破坏，并探索竞争基态（如自旋向列相、自旋液体等）的存在性。

Method: 采用精确对角化（exact diagonalization）方法分析有限团簇上的基态性质；同时使用完全对称的Gutzwiller投影阿布里科索夫费米子（Abrikosov-fermion）U(1)和Z2变分态进行测试。

Result: 铁磁边界上未发现零场自旋向列相（spin-nematic phase），而是在此区域观察到不可公度自旋密度波（incommensurate spin-density-wave）关联，其序矢量连续演化；相图还包括共线奈尔态（collinear Néel）、倾斜120°态（canted 120°）和六方单线态（hexagonal-singlet）区域，中间存在难以分类的区域。投影U(1)和Z2变分态均无法描述这些未解析区域；但在红宝石晶格边界上，一个投影Z2 Ansatz能准确重现共线奈尔相与六方单线态之间有限尺度的能量和自旋关联。

Conclusion: 枫叶晶格中铁磁边界附近的主要竞争态是不可公度自旋密度波而非自旋向列相，且解析区域以外的中间区域可能不存在简单的自旋液体（spin-liquid）描述；红宝石晶格边界上的投影Z2态为理解相边界附近的量子行为提供了有效的变分描述。

Abstract: We study how ferromagnetism breaks down in the spin-$\tfrac12$ nearest-neighbor Heisenberg model on the maple-leaf lattice with ferromagnetic $J_t,J_d$ and antiferromagnetic $J_h$, motivated by the mixed ferro-antiferromagnetic interactions in Na$_2$Mn$_3$O$_7$. Exact diagonalization shows that the ferromagnetic boundary does not feature a zero-field spin-nematic phase on the clusters studied here, but an extended regime of incommensurate spin-density-wave correlations with continuously evolving ordering vector. The phase diagram also contains collinear Néel, canted $120^\circ$, and hexagonal-singlet regimes, separated by regions that remain difficult to classify from exact diagonalization alone. Variational tests of fully symmetric Gutzwiller-projected Abrikosov-fermion U(1) and $\mathbb{Z}_2$ states find no competitive spin-liquid description of the interior unresolved regions. By contrast, on the ruby-lattice boundary we identify a point between the collinear Néel and hexagonal-singlet phases where a projected $\mathbb{Z}_2$ Ansatz reproduces the finite-size energy and spin correlations with good accuracy.

</details>


### [87] [Lattice Gauging Interfaces and Noninvertible Defects in Higher Dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12601)
*David Hofmeier,Giovanna Pimenta,Weiguang Cao*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文在更高维度的格点模型中系统研究了规范接口（gauging interface）及其缺陷后裔（defect descendant），通过引入运动算符（movement operator）解决了约束希尔伯特空间依赖于接口位置的问题，并应用于凝聚缺陷分析、规范映射重构以及子群规范中的混合反常诊断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在具有广义对称性（generalized symmetry）的高维格点模型中，规范接口的拓扑性质受到约束希尔伯特空间（constrained Hilbert space）对接口位置依赖性的干扰，现有框架无法清晰地描述其拓扑本质。本文旨在解决这一障碍并建立统一的格点框架。

Method: 构造了规范 $\mathbb Z_2^{(0)}$ 对称性（$(2+1)d$）和 $\mathbb Z_2^{(1)}$ 对称性（$(3+1)d$）的显式接口哈密顿量（interface Hamiltonian），并引入运动算符作用于公共的无约束希尔伯特空间（unconstrained Hilbert space），用以同时输运接口哈密顿量和相关约束条件。该框架进一步推广至子群规范（subgroup gauging），以 $\mathbb Z_2\subset\mathbb Z_4$ 为例进行分析。

Result: 通过运动算符重建了规范映射（gauging map），并分析了有限区域规范（finite-region gauging）所得的凝聚缺陷（condensation defect）。在子群规范情形下，发现所得对偶对称性（dual symmetry）携带混合反常（mixed anomaly），该反常可通过凝聚缺陷上的对称性分数量子化（symmetry fractionalization）在格点中诊断。

Conclusion: 本文为高维系统中由规范产生的拓扑接口、凝聚缺陷及相关反常提供了一个显式的格点框架，弥合了约束希尔伯特空间依赖性带来的理论描述困难。

Abstract: We study gauging interfaces and their defect descendants in lattice models with generalized symmetries in higher dimensions. We construct explicit interface Hamiltonians for gauging a $\mathbb Z_2^{(0)}$ symmetry in $(2+1)d$ and a $\mathbb Z_2^{(1)}$ symmetry in $(3+1)d$. In higher dimensions, and especially in the presence of higher-form symmetries, the topological nature of gauging interfaces is obscured by the fact that the constrained Hilbert space depends on the location of the interface. We resolve this by introducing movement operators acting on a common unconstrained Hilbert space, which transport both the interface Hamiltonians and the associated constraints. As applications, we analyze condensation defects obtained from finite-region gauging and reconstruct the gauging map from movement operators. Finally, we apply the same framework to subgroup gauging, focusing on the example of gauging $\mathbb Z_2\subset \mathbb Z_4$. This produces a dual symmetry carrying a mixed anomaly, which we diagnose on the lattice through symmetry fractionalization on condensation defects. Our results provide an explicit lattice framework for studying topological interfaces, condensation defects, and the associated anomalies arising from gauging in higher-dimensional systems.

</details>


### [88] [Imaging Interacting Two-Dimensional Anisotropic Electrons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12761)
*Ziyu Xiang,Jianghan Xiao,Hongyuan Li,Woochang Kim,Tianle Wang,Zhihuan Dong,Takashi Taniguchi,Kenji Watanabe,Michael P. Zaletel,Steven G. Louie,Michael F. Crommie,Feng Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究利用非侵入式扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunnelling microscopy）直接观测了单层1T-ReSe₂中二维各向异性维格纳晶体（anisotropic Wigner crystal）及其量子熔化（quantum melting）过程，首次实验证实了各向异性电子形成斜方维格纳晶格（oblique Wigner lattice）的预测，并发现沿轻质量方向的一维熔化导致形成近晶型电子液晶（smectic electron liquid crystal）中间相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管理论上长期预测，具有各向异性有效质量（anisotropic effective mass）的电子会形成斜方维格纳晶体而非各向同性体系常见的三角晶格（triangular lattice），但这一物理现象在实验上极少被探索。本工作旨在利用单层ReSe₂作为平台，直接实验观测各向异性维格纳晶体及其量子熔化行为。

Method: 采用非侵入式扫描隧道显微镜直接成像技术，对门控单层1T-ReSe₂（monolayer 1T-ReSe₂）中的各向异性电子波函数（anisotropic electron wavefunction）及其形成的维格纳晶体进行可视化观测。

Result: 成功成像了单个电子的各向异性形状，其波函数沿轻质量方向（light-mass direction）显著拉长；低电子密度下，这些电子结晶为斜方维格纳晶格；随密度增加，量子涨落（quantum fluctuations）沿轻质量方向增长更快，驱动晶体发生一维熔化（one-dimensional melting），形成沿一个方向有序、另一方向熔化的近晶态电子液晶（smectic electron liquid crystal），介于电子固体（electron solid）和费米液体（Fermi liquid）相之间。

Conclusion: 本工作建立了单层ReSe₂作为研究各向异性关联电子（anisotropic correlated electrons）、量子熔化以及耦合一维电子链（coupled one-dimensional electron chains）的平台，填补了各向异性维格纳晶体实验研究的重要空白。

Abstract: We directly visualize a two-dimensional anisotropic Wigner crystal and its quantum melting in monolayer 1T-ReSe2 using non-invasive scanning tunnelling microscopy. In crystals with anisotropic effective mass, an electron's quantum wavefunction becomes elongated along the light-mass direction to reduce kinetic energy. At low electron density, such anisotropic electrons are predicted to form an oblique Wigner crystal rather than the familiar triangular lattice of isotropic systems. Despite longstanding theoretical interest, this physics has been little explored experimentally. Here we first image the anisotropic shape of individual electrons in gated monolayer ReSe2, whose wavefunctions are strongly elongated along the light-mass direction. At low density, these electrons crystallize into an oblique Wigner lattice. As the density increases, quantum fluctuations grow more rapidly along the light-mass direction than along the heavy-mass direction, driving a one-dimensional melting of the crystal. The resulting state retains order along one direction but melts along the other, consistent with a smectic electron liquid crystal between the electron solid and Fermi liquid phases. Our work establishes monolayer ReSe2 as a platform for studying anisotropic correlated electrons, quantum melting, and coupled one-dimensional electron chains.

</details>

Abstract: Developing non-perturbative methods to reveal exotic properties of strongly correlated fermionic systems remains one of the most essential tasks of theoretical physics. Tensor network methods with Grassmann algebra offer powerful numerical tools for fermionic many-body systems in the coherent-state path-integral representation. Despite their vast potential for both condensed-matter and particle-physics communities, Grassmann tensor network methods are somewhat underexploited in practical simulations. In this work, we provide a detailed, self-contained introduction to Grassmann tensor network methods, from the basics of the Grassmann tensor operations to the Grassmannization of typical tensor network algorithms. ### [90] [Reentrant behavior and possible $2/3$ magnetization plateau on the double-trillium langbeinite K$_2$Ni$_2$(SO$_4$)$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13263)
*Matías G. Gonzalez,Yurii Skourski,Johannes Reuther,Ivica Živković*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究基于实验脉冲磁场测量与经典蒙特卡洛模拟，揭示了langbeinite家族化合物K₂Ni₂(SO₄)₃在低场和中场下的系列相变，并发现了一个由1/3相（强耦合trillium格子）和全极化相（弱耦合trillium格子）组成的2/3磁化平台特征，尽管经典极限下预期不存在平台，但系统倾向于稳定该自旋构型，形成穹顶结构并导致重入现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: K₂Ni₂(SO₄)₃属于langbeinite家族，包含两个相互交织的S=1 trillium格子（强耦合与弱耦合），其高度受挫的海森伯哈密顿量（highly-frustrated Heisenberg Hamiltonian）使其在参数空间中接近自旋液体区域（spin-liquid region），因此研究其在外加磁场下的磁化行为有助于理解该体系中可能存在的量子自旋液体与磁有序之间的竞争。

Method: 研究人员将实验中通过脉冲磁场（pulsed magnetic fields）最高达40 T测得的磁化过程与经典蒙特卡洛模拟（classical Monte Carlo calculations）结果进行对比分析。

Result: 发现该体系在低场和中场区域存在一系列相变；揭示了一个2/3磁化平台特征，该平台由强耦合trillium格子的1/3相与弱耦合trillium格子的全极化相（fully polarized phase）共同构成；在经典极限下虽无平台存在，但发现了一个显著的穹顶结构（dome structure），表明系统倾向于稳定该自旋构型，并导致重入现象（reentrant phenomenon）；该平台样相在单个trillium和tetratrillium格子的经典海森伯模型中同样存在。

Conclusion: 该工作表明，2/3平台相可能广泛存在于langbeinite家族的双trillium化合物中，并为进一步在量子极限下探索trillium及双trillium材料中的平台相提供了实验和理论基础。

Abstract: K$_2$Ni$_2$(SO$_4$)$_3$ is a member of the langbeinite family, consisting of two intertwined $S=1$ trillium lattices, out of which one is strongly coupled (strong-TL) and the other is weakly coupled (weak-TL). Further inter-trillium interactions give rise to a highly-frustrated Heisenberg Hamiltonian. Despite ordering at low temperatures, K$_2$Ni$_2$(SO$_4$)$_3$ lies close in parameter space to a spin-liquid region that surrounds the tetratrillium limit, where each triangle belonging to strong-TL turns into a tetrahedron by connecting to a single spin from weak-TL. Here, we compare the experimentally determined magnetization process using pulsed magnetic fields up to $40$ T with classical Monte Carlo calculations, uncovering a series of phase transitions at both low and intermediate fields. Furthermore, we reveal a signature of a $2/3$ magnetization plateau consisting of a $1/3$ phase on strong-TL and a fully polarized phase on weak-TL. Although in the classical limit no plateau is expected, we find a very prominent dome structure reflecting the tendency of the system to stabilize this particular spin configuration. The presence of a dome leads to a reentrant phenomenon in which the system recovers the Hamiltonian symmetries when increasing the magnetic field. Finally, we show that this plateau-like phase is also present in the classical Heisenberg model on the single trillium and tetratrillium lattices, indicating its possible presence in the large family of double-trillium langbeinite compounds. Our findings motivate future studies on the presence of the plateau phase in the quantum limit of both trillium and double-trillium materials within the langbeinite family.

</details>


### [91] [Invertible Symmetry and Spontaneous Duality Breaking in the Transverse-Field Ising Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13363)
*José Dupont,Jasper van Wezel*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文证明横场伊辛模型（transverse-field Ising model）的对偶性（self-duality）在开边界条件下可以成为精确对偶，并由一个可逆算子实现，同时揭示了该精确对偶导致的自发对偶破缺（spontaneous duality breaking）现象，即数学上等价的模型在物理实现中对局部扰动的敏感性不同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 横场伊辛模型的对偶性作为现代物理学组织原则的典型范例，其标准形式并不精确——原模型与对偶模型具有不同的对称性和基态数目，且由非可逆算子实现。本文旨在构建一种可实现精确对偶的模型设置，并探讨其物理后果。

Method: 将边界条件从周期性改为开放（open boundary conditions），使得模型允许由一个唯一的可逆算子（invertible operator）实现精确对偶。通过分析量子临界点（quantum critical point）处对称性的可逆性、边缘自由度（edge degree of freedom）的存在性，以及原模型与对偶模型对空间局部扰动的不同敏感性，论证了精确对偶的成立及其物理含义。

Result: 在开边界条件下实现了精确对偶，该对偶由可逆算子实现，量子临界点处的对称性也是可逆的；精确对偶必然伴随异常边缘自由度的出现，实现了基于对偶而非拓扑（topology）的体-边对应（bulk-boundary correspondence）；原模型中的全局对称性自发破缺在对偶系统中等价于局域对称性自发破缺，但这一表观上与Elitzur定理（Elitzur's theorem）矛盾的现象可通过两种模型对局部扰动敏感性的差异加以解释。

Conclusion: 虽然原模型与对偶模型在数学上完全等价，但其物理实现并不等价；这种由任意小的环境影响引起的涌现差异被称为自发对偶破缺（spontaneous duality breaking），类似于对称性的自发破缺。

Abstract: The self-duality of the transverse-field Ising model is an archetype for dualities that, alongside symmetry and topology, are used as an organizing principle throughout modern physics. This duality, however, is not exact. The original and dual models have different symmetries and numbers of ground states, and the duality is implemented by a non-invertible operator giving rise to a non-invertible symmetry at the quantum critical point. Here, we show that by adjusting the model to accommodate open rather than periodic boundary conditions, it allows for an exact duality implemented by a unique invertible operator. In the model with exact duality, the symmetry at the quantum critical point is also exact, and hence invertible. Moreover, we find that the exact duality necessitates the presence of an anomalous edge degree of freedom, thus realizing a duality rather than topology based bulk-boundary correspondence. Finally, the exactness of the duality implies that the spontaneous breakdown of a global symmetry in terms of the original model can equivalently be described as spontaneously breaking a local symmetry in the dual system. We show that this seeming contradiction of Elitzur's theorem can be explained by the original and dual models obtaining different sensitivities to spatially local perturbations in any physical implementation of the Hamiltonian. Although the dual partners are mathematically equivalent, their physical implementations therefore are not. In analogy to the spontaneous breakdown of symmetries, we term this emergent distinction due to arbitrarily small environmental influences spontaneous duality breaking.

</details>


### [92] [Magnetic fields in monoclinic $α$-RuCl$_3$ reveal rhombohedral inclusions underlying apparent oscillations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13444)
*Hamza Nasir Daniel Balazs,Muhammad Nauman,Ezekiel Horsley,Subin Kim,Young-June Kim,K. A. Modic*

TL;DR: 本文通过研究α-RuCl₃单斜相纳米晶体的磁致磁化率测量，发现先前归因于量子自旋液体（QSL）的场诱导现象实际上源于样品中单斜相和菱方相共存导致的多个反铁磁（AFM）相边界位移，而非真正的非磁性相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: α-RuCl₃作为Kitaev量子自旋液体候选材料，其场诱导现象因材料温度依赖的晶体结构和应变诱导堆叠无序而存在争议。最近其晶体结构随温度和样品尺寸的变化已被澄清，因此有必要重新评估其磁性质与自旋液体特征之间的关联。

Method: 本研究在纳克级单斜相单晶上进行高分辨率磁致磁化率（magnetotropic susceptibility）测量，并在多个晶面内绘制反铁磁相边界随温度、磁场和取向的变化。

Result: 单斜相相图与菱方相相似，但系统性地向更高转变温度和临界场偏移。在B∥a方向观察到两阶段抑制反铁磁有序，表明存在一个中间有序相（类似菱方相中的ZZ2相）。此前在面内磁场下超出反铁磁区域观测到的转变实际上源于与单斜包裹体相关的多个位移反铁磁相边界，而非非磁性相。

Conclusion: 先前归因于量子自旋液体的特征实际上是由于高温单斜相到低温菱方相的不完全转变所致。该结果强调了结构对称性和样品均匀性在解释α-RuCl₃及相关二维量子磁体场诱导现象中的关键作用。

Abstract: The majority of research on $α$-RuCl$_3$ has focused on applying in-plane magnetic fields to suppress antiferromagnetic order and induce a quantum spin liquid (QSL). However, this effort has been complicated by the materials temperature-dependent crystal structure and sensitivity to strain-induced stacking disorder, making interpretation of field-induced phenomena contentious. The crystal structure of $α$-RuCl$_3$ has recently been clarified as a function of temperature and sample size, motivating a reassessment of its magnetic properties and connection to proposed spin-liquid signatures. Here, we show that the monoclinic structure can be isolated in nanogram-scale crystals, enabling the study of Kitaev physics in a new regime. We focus on a structurally well-defined monoclinic crystal at low temperature and perform high-resolution magnetotropic susceptibility measurements in several crystal planes. Mapping the AFM phase boundary versus temperature, field, and orientation, we find the monoclinic phase diagram closely resembles rhombohedral crystals but is systematically shifted to higher transition temperatures and critical fields. For $B \parallel a$, we observe a two-step suppression of AFM order, indicating an intermediate ordered phase analogous to the ZZ2 phase reported in rhombohedral samples. Our results show that transitions previously observed beyond the AFM regime under in-plane fields arise from multiple shifted AFM phase boundaries associated with monoclinic inclusions, rather than non-magnetic phases. These findings indicate that features attributed to a QSL are instead due to an incomplete transition from the high-temperature monoclinic to the low-temperature rhombohedral structure. They also highlight the role of structural symmetry and sample homogeneity in interpreting field-induced phenomena in $α$-RuCl$_3$ and related two-dimensional quantum magnets.

### [93] [Lieb-Schultz-Mattis theorem from gauge constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13606)
*Bhandaru Phani Parasar*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文在一维链上构造了一个耦合有物质的 $\mathbb{Z}_2 \times \mathbb{Z}_2$ 规范理论，发现在高斯定律子空间中存在一个U(1)对称性，进而导出Lieb-Schultz-Mattis（LSM）定理，排除了平凡有能隙基态的可能性，并在特定参数点发现了一个无能隙点，其激发可用约束下的自由狄拉克费米子描述，两点关联函数呈现 $\propto \cos{(\pi r)}\,r^{-2/9}$ 的渐近行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在研究一维链上 $\mathbb{Z}_2 \times \mathbb{Z}_2$ 规范理论在高斯定律子空间（Gauss law subspace）中的基态物理，探索规范约束如何产生新的对称性并导致非平凡的低能物理。

Method: 构造了一维链上耦合有物质的 $\mathbb{Z}_2 \times \mathbb{Z}_2$ 规范理论，在高斯定律子空间中分析系统的对称性结构，并利用Lieb-Schultz-Mattis（LSM）定理排除平凡有能隙基态。在特定参数点处分析了无能隙激发的自由狄拉克费米子（free Dirac fermions）描述，并计算了局域规范不变量的两点关联函数。

Result: 在高斯定律子空间中发现了一个U(1)对称性，其生成元与晶格平移对易但与晶格反射反对易，从而导出一个LSM定理：若哈密顿量具有平移和反射不变性，则系统不可能存在平凡有能隙基态，必须要么是自发对称破缺（SSB）基态，要么是无能隙基态。在特定参数点系统无能隙，激发可用带有总费米子数约束的自由狄拉克费米子描述，两点关联函数渐近行为为 $\propto \cos{(\pi r)}\,r^{-2/9}$。

Conclusion: 展示了获得LSM型定理的一种新机制：负责该定理的对称性源自规范理论的运动学约束（kinematic constraints）。该模型也是研究自发对称破缺相中拓扑缺陷（topological defects）相图的自然平台。

Abstract: We construct a $\mathbb{Z}_2 \times \mathbb{Z}_2$ gauge theory coupled to matter on a one-dimensional chain, aiming to study the ground-state physics in the Gauss law subspace. We show that the theory in the Gauss law subspace has a U$(1)$ symmetry whose generator commutes with lattice translations, but anticommutes with the lattice reflection operator. This leads to a Lieb-Schultz-Mattis (LSM) theorem that always rules out a trivial gapped ground state in the Gauss law subspace, if the hamiltonian is invariant under translations and reflection. Any point in the parameter space must realize a either a spontaneously symmetry broken (SSB) ground state, or a gapless ground state. Imposing the Gauss law is pivotal for the existence of the U$(1)$ symmetry, and hence of the LSM theorem. We thus demonstrate a novel mechanism to obtain an LSM-type theorem, wherein the symmetry responsible for the theorem originates from the kinematic constraints of a gauge theory. We identify a point in the parameter space at which the system is gapless. At the gapless point, the excitations admit a description in terms of free Dirac fermions with a constraint on the total fermion number. The asymptotic behavior of the two-point correlation function of the simplest local gauge-invariant quantity at the gapless point is found to be $ \propto \cos{(πr)}\,r^{-2/9}$, where $r$ is the lattice separation between the two points. This model is also a natural platform to study phase diagram topological defects residing in families of SSB phases.

### [94] [Parallel Scan Recurrent Neural Quantum States for Scalable Variational Monte Carlo](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13807)
*Ejaaz Merali,Mohamed Hibat-Allah,Mohammad Kohandel,Richard T. Scalettar,Ehsan Khatami*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用自回归递归波函数（autoregressive recurrent wave functions）结合近年来并行化递归计算（parallelizable recurrence）的进展，构建了名为并行扫描递归神经量子态（parallel scan recurrent neural quantum states, PSR-NQS）的变分拟设（variational ansätze）。该方法可在变分蒙特卡洛（variational Monte Carlo）框架下高效训练，适用于一维和二维空间。

Result: 在基准测试中取得准确结果。通过迭代重训练（iterative retraining），该方法可处理规模达$52\times52$的二维自旋晶格（spin lattice），且结果与已有的量子蒙特卡洛（quantum Monte Carlo）数据保持一致。

Conclusion: 递归架构（recurrent architectures）是实现可扩展神经量子态模拟（scalable neural quantum state simulations）的一种实用且有前景的途径，能够在中等的计算资源条件下运行。

Abstract: Neural-network quantum states have emerged as a powerful variational framework for quantum many-body systems, with recent progress often driven by massively parallel architectures such as transformers. Recurrent neural network quantum states, however, are frequently regarded as intrinsically sequential and therefore less scalable. Here we revisit this view by showing that modern recurrent architectures can support fast, accurate, and computationally accessible neural quantum state simulations. Using autoregressive recurrent wave functions together with recent advances in parallelizable recurrence, we develop variational ansätze, called parallel scan recurrent neural quantum states (PSR-NQS), which can be trained efficiently within variational Monte Carlo in one and two spatial dimensions. We demonstrate accurate benchmark results and show that, with iterative retraining, our approach reaches two-dimensional spin lattices as large as $52\times52$ while remaining in agreement with available quantum Monte Carlo data. Our results establish recurrent architectures as a practical and promising route toward scalable neural quantum state simulations with modest computational resources.

### [95] [Phase-resolved field-space distance bounds in ekpyrotic, bouncing and cyclic cosmologies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12579)
*Marcin Postolak*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文针对非暴胀（non-inflationary）平滑过程（如火劫、反弹和循环宇宙模型），提出了一个相位分辨的距离准则（phase-resolved distance criterion），将不变标量距离分解为火劫平滑、熵-曲率转换、反弹和反弹后贡献。通过引入BKL（Belinski-Khalatnikov-Lifshitz）各向异性抑制等约束，推导出参数ε_ek的下界，并提出了可用于观测检验的主条件（master condition）和曲率约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 暴胀模型中的Lyth bound（Lyth界）将原初张量振幅与暴胀场位移联系起来，但火劫（ekpyrotic）、反弹（bouncing）和循环（cyclic）模型中不存在类似的普适关系。为此，需要为这些非暴胀平滑过程建立一种场空间距离预算（field-space distance budget）的类比框架。

Method: 提出相位分辨距离准则，将不变标量距离分解为火劫平滑、熵-曲率转换、反弹和反弹后四个贡献。引入三类约束：BKL各向异性抑制的参数化条件、基于塔楼态逻辑（tower of states logic）的截断修正距离预算、以及来自残余等曲率扰动（residual isocurvature）和非高斯性（non-Gaussianity）的观测转换窗口。进一步提出主条件导出参数ε_ek的下界，并对弯曲标量场空间中的尺度不变熵扰动导出曲率约束。

Result: 在火劫收缩的典型相位中恢复了已知的小场标度（small-field scaling）并推广为总预算不等式。小总距离和观测到的红谱倾斜（red tilt）似乎指向超快滚火劫（ultra-fast-roll ekpyrosis）、锐转弯、短时或强修正反弹，以及/或者标量流形显著的负截面曲率（negative sectional curvature）。

Conclusion: 所提出的距离准则和约束条件为火劫、反弹和循环模型提供了一种可观测检验的场空间距离预算框架，并展示了如何将距离预算与观测数据对接进行测试。

Abstract: The inflationary Lyth bound relates the primordial tensor amplitude to the inflaton field excursion. There is no analogous universal relationship in the case of ekpyrotic, bouncing, and cyclic models because scalar and tensor perturbations depend on entropy conversion, matching through the bounce and the specific mechanism that violates or evades the null energy condition. Nevertheless, the background kinematics fulfills a useful non-inflationary analogue: a field-space distance budget. In this study, we propose a phase-resolved distance criterion for a non-inflationary smoothing process and decompose the invariant scalar distance into ekpyrotic smoothing, entropy-to-curvature conversion, bounce, and post-bounce contributions. Then, we impose BKL anisotropy suppression as an additional constraint on the ekpyrotic phase. In the canonical phase of the ekpyrotic contraction, we recover the known small-field scaling and generalize it to total budget inequality. We impose three requirements: a BKL (Belinski-Khalatnikov-Lifshitz) anisotropy suppression that is parameterized separately, a phenomenological cutoff-corrected distance budget inspired by tower of states logic, and observational conversion windows from residual isocurvature and non-Gaussianity. Furthermore, we propose a new master condition that provides a lower bound on the value of the parameter $ε_{\rm ek}$ that depends on the remaining distance available after conversion and the cosmological bounce. We also derive a curvature constraint for scale-invariant entropy perturbations in curved field space which shows that the small total distance and the observed red tilt seem to indicate ultra-fast-roll ekpyrosis, sharp turns, short or strongly modified bounces, and/or significant negative sectional curvature of the scalar manifold. Finally, we demonstrate methods for testing the distance budget against observational data.

### [96] [How much dark matter really matters?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12593)
*Jenny Wagner*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文指出，在强引力透镜（strong gravitational lensing）重建暗物质（dark matter）分布时，传统预定义质量密度模型会高估暗物质含量；消除这些模型偏差后，观测数据直接约束的是透镜质量体的局域性质，从而质疑了当前对暗物质必要性的估算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强引力透镜是示踪暗物质（dark matter）的关键探针。现有重建方法依赖预定义的质量密度模型（mass-density model），可能导致对暗物质含量的系统性高估。文章旨在揭示模型选择如何扭曲观测推断，并追问有多少暗物质是真实必要的，有多少是人为引入的。

Method: 文章采用分析方法论（analytical approach），通过对比标准重建（standard reconstructions）中预定义质量密度模型与去除模型后的直接约束，论证模型选择对暗物质含量估算的系统性影响。

Result: 结果表明，预定义质量密度模型会高估（over-estimate）透镜质量体中的暗物质含量；消除这些模型后，观测直接约束的是透镜质量体的局域性质（local properties）。

Conclusion: 强引力透镜效应中究竟需要多少暗物质，以及有多少是模型选择人为造成的，这一问题仍有待回答，提示需重新审视当前重建方法的可靠性。

Abstract: Strong gravitational lensing is a key probe to trace dark matter. It assumes that mass curves spacetime so that light from a background source is deflected on its way to the observer. If dark matter contributes the major part to a massive cosmic structure, reconstructing the latter from strong-lensing observables allows us to infer characteristics of dark matter. Standard reconstructions fit a pre-defined mass-density model to the data. In this essay, I show how these mass models over-estimate the dark-matter contents of light-deflecting masses. Eliminating these models from the reconstruction reveals that observations directly constrain local properties of light-deflecting masses. How much dark matter is really needed in strong-gravitational-lensing effects and how much do we make up by our model choices?

</details>


### [97] [Inspiral gravitational waveforms from charged compact binaries with scalar hair](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13036)
*Antonio De Felice,Shinji Tsujikawa*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在爱因斯坦-标量-麦克斯韦（Einstein-scalar-Maxwell, ESM）理论框架下，系统研究了带电致密双星系统的引力波波形。通过引入单个参数b统一描述广义相对论的偏离，推导了包含标量、矢量辐射的频域波形，并利用双脉冲星轨道周期衰减数据对模型参数给出了严格约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在ESM理论中，致密天体（黑洞、中子星、奇异致密天体）可同时携带矢量荷与标量荷（后者作为次级“毛发”由前者诱导产生），这为超越广义相对论（general relativity）的引力波（gravitational wave）信号提供了新的理论来源。现有研究缺乏对这些带电双星系统引力波波形的统一描述，因此需要建立一个完整框架以连接理论预测与观测约束。

Method: 将双星系统建模为具有标量场依赖质量的带电点粒子，在近区推导保守动力学，在远区计算辐射场。利用稳相近似（stationary phase approximation）从张量、标量、矢量三种辐射的能量通量构造频域波形。标量和矢量荷质比差异导致的偶极辐射（dipole radiation）贡献领先的−1阶后牛顿（post-Newtonian）修正，偏离广义相对论的程度由单个参数b统一刻画。

Result: 张量波形通过有效动力学和辐射反激驱动的相位演化得到修正，标量与矢量模则引入额外的能量损失通道。双脉冲星轨道周期衰减数据已对中子星双星系统的参数b给出了严格约束，并进一步评估了黑洞-黑洞、中子星-中子星、奇异致密天体-奇异致密天体双星在ESM理论中实现时b的取值。

Conclusion: 该工作为带电致密双星系统的引力波特征提供了一个统一的理论框架，并表明利用当前和未来的观测数据可以检验暗扇区（dark-sector）标量与矢量荷的存在。

Abstract: We investigate gravitational waveforms from compact binary systems in Einstein-scalar-Maxwell (ESM) theories, where a scalar field $φ$ couples to a $U(1)$ gauge field $A_μ$ through a field-dependent function $μ(φ)$. In this framework, compact objects -- black holes (BHs), neutron stars (NSs), and exotic compact objects (ECOs) -- can carry both vector and scalar charges, with the latter arising as secondary hair induced by the former. Modeling the binary as electrically charged point particles with scalar-field-dependent masses, we derive the conservative dynamics in the near zone and compute the radiative fields in the far zone. The tensor waveform is modified through the effective dynamics and radiation-reaction-driven phase evolution, while scalar and vector modes introduce additional energy-loss channels. From the energy fluxes of tensor, scalar, and vector radiation, we construct the frequency-domain waveform using the stationary phase approximation. Dipole radiation sourced by differences in scalar and vector charge-to-mass ratios yields a leading $-1$ post-Newtonian correction. The deviation from general relativity is characterized by a single parameter $b$, which controls both amplitude and phase modifications. We further examine constraints from the orbital-period decay of binary pulsars, showing that current observations already place stringent bounds on $b$ for neutron star binaries. In addition, we evaluate $b$ for representative BH-BH, NS-NS, ECO-ECO binaries realized in ESM theories. Our results provide a unified framework for gravitational-wave signatures of charged compact binaries and offer a means of testing dark-sectorscalar and vector charges with current and future observations.

</details>


### [98] [The Gravitational Spectral Radio Forest: A Signature of Primordial Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13042)
*P. George Christopher,K. Hari,S. Shankaranarayanan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出通过将星际氢原子作为时空曲率的量子传感器，探测小行星质量级别的原初黑洞（Primordial Black Hole, PBH）作为暗物质候选体的引力特征。研究聚焦于H II区，发现PBH的黎曼潮汐张量（Riemann tidal tensor）会导致束缚氢原子的2P_{3/2}能级发生对称分裂，将9.9 GHz吸收线重塑为一个带宽约2 GHz的引力光谱射电森林（gravitational spectral radio forest）。考虑氢原子在邦迪半径（Bondi radius）内的吸积及其密度平方发射度量后，吸收谱得到增强。该特征为即将开展的射电巡天提供了高对比度的观测目标，以约束暗物质成分中的PBH种群。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有暗物质候选体（如弱相互作用大质量粒子, WIMP）尚未被直接探测到，促使研究者探索原初黑洞（Primordial Black Hole, PBH）作为替代方案。然而，小行星质量级别的PBH难以通过传统引力透镜或电磁辐射信号进行有效探测。本文旨在利用星际氢原子作为量子传感器，从微观能级分裂中提取PBH的引力特征，从而开辟新的探测路径。

Method: 将星际中性氢视为量子传感器，分析PBH的黎曼潮汐张量（Riemann tidal tensor）对氢原子精细结构能级的影响。研究聚焦于H II区域，计算了PBH引力场下2P_{3/2}态的对称分裂效应。进一步引入氢原子在邦迪半径（Bondi radius）内的活跃吸积过程，以及由此产生的密度平方发射度量（density-squared emission measure）对吸收谱的增强贡献。

Result: PBH的潮汐效应将氢原子里德伯线（9.9 GHz吸收线）重塑为一个带宽约2 GHz的引力光谱射电森林（gravitational spectral radio forest）。氢原子在邦迪半径内的吸积过程导致吸收谱相对增强。该特征具有较高的对比度，适合作为未来射电巡天的观测目标。

Conclusion: 该引力光谱射电森林提供了一种具体、高对比度的可观测信号，用于约束暗物质成分中的原初黑洞（PBH）种群。该方案有望通过即将开展的射电巡天项目获得实验检验，从而推动对PBH作为暗物质候选体的理解。

Abstract: We propose a novel gravitational signature to detect Primordial Black Hole (PBH) dark matter by treating interstellar hydrogen as a quantum sensor for spacetime curvature. Focusing on H II regions, we demonstrate that the Riemann tidal tensor of an \emph{asteroid-mass} PBH induces a symmetric splitting of the $2P_{3/2}$ state in bound hydrogen atoms. This relativistic effect redistributes $9.9\,\mathrm{GHz}$ absorption line into a gravitational spectral radio forest with a bandwidth $\sim 2\,\mathrm{GHz}$. By accounting for active accretion of Hydrogen atoms and the resulting density-squared emission measure within the Bondi radius, we find a relatively enhanced absorption spectrum. This feature presents a concrete, high-contrast target for upcoming radio-surveys to constrain PBH populations in the dark matter sector.

</details>


### [99] [Fixing the Renormalization of Inflationary Loops via Ward Identities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13325)
*Cheng-Jun Fang,Zong-Kuan Guo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于大规范对称性（large gauge symmetry）导出精确的Ward恒等式（Ward identities），对非吸引子暴涨（non-attractor inflation）中曲率扰动（curvature perturbations）的重整化（renormalization）程序施加严格的模型无关约束，从而系统性地解决了近期超慢滚动暴涨（ultra-slow-roll inflation）中一圈修正（one-loop corrections）的理论分歧。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非吸引子暴涨中量子圈修正（quantum loop corrections）对曲率扰动的评估存在理论歧义，核心困难在于重整化对消项（renormalization counterterms）中不受约束的有限贡献以及正则化方案（regularization scheme）依赖性。需要建立一种系统性的框架来消除这些理论不确定性。

Method: 基于背景-扰动分离（background-perturbation split）的大规范对称性，通过路径积分形式（path integral formalism）推导出精确的Ward恒等式。这些恒等式对重整化程序施加严格的、模型无关（model-independent）的约束。

Result: Ward恒等式非微扰地（non-perturbatively）控制功率谱（power spectrum）的红外演化（infrared evolution），前提是紫外完备化（ultraviolet completion）尊重该对称性。该框架为超慢滚动暴涨中一圈修正的理论分歧提供了系统性解决方案。

Conclusion: 基于对称性的方法能够系统性地解决非吸引子暴涨中量子圈修正的理论歧义问题，为未来相关研究提供了坚实的理论基础。

Abstract: Evaluating quantum loop corrections to curvature perturbations in non-attractor inflation presents theoretical ambiguities. A crucial aspect of this challenge lies in the unconstrained finite contributions in renormalization counterterms and regularization scheme dependence. In this work, we derive exact Ward identities via the path integral formalism based on the large gauge symmetry of the background-perturbation split. These identities are shown to impose strict, model-independent constraints on the renormalization procedure. Provided the ultraviolet completion respects this symmetry, the Ward identities non-perturbatively govern the infrared evolution of the power spectrum. This symmetry-based framework offers a systematic resolution to recent theoretical discrepancies concerning one-loop corrections in ultra-slow-roll inflation.

</details>

### [101] [Observational signatures of misaligned double-ring and double-torus configurations around a Schwarzschild black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13459)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用广义相对论射线追踪（general-relativistic ray tracing）方法，对绕史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）的双环-双环面系统进行模拟，计算频移图（frequency-shift maps）、观测屏上的热辐射通量图（bolometric flux maps）以及相应的谱线轮廓（spectral line profiles）。

Result: 两个非共面发射结构产生特征性的多峰谱线轮廓（multi-peak spectral profiles）和非对称热辐射通量分布（asymmetric bolometric-flux distributions），这些特征在谱线轮廓形态和热辐射通量的α轮廓（α-profiles）上均有体现。

Conclusion: 非共面多成分吸积结构产生的上述观测特征可作为简单的诊断特征（diagnostic features），用于识别此类复杂吸积构型。

Abstract: We investigate the observational signatures of an idealized double-ring and double-torus system orbiting a Schwarzschild black hole, allowing the two emitting components to have mutually inclined symmetry axes. Using general-relativistic ray tracing, we construct frequency-shift maps, bolometric flux maps on the observer's screen, and the corresponding spectral line profiles of the emitted radiation. The single equatorial torus is used as a reference configuration in order to isolate the effect of the second emitting component and of the mutual misalignment of the two structures. We show that the presence of two non-coplanar emitting structures produces characteristic multi-peak spectral profiles and asymmetric bolometric-flux distributions. These signatures are imprinted both in the line-profile morphology and in the $α$-profiles of the bolometric flux, providing simple diagnostic features of non-coplanar multi-component accretion structures.

### [102] [Quantum resolution of the Schwarzschild singularity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13508)
*Vishnulal Cheriyodathillathu,Tanmay Patil,Saurya Das,Soumen Basak*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在经典背景几何与玻姆（Bohmian）量子轨迹的半经典框架中重新审视史瓦西奇点，通过Madelung-Bohm分解将量子修正运动等价于一个与史瓦西度规共形关联的有效度量中的测地运动，并证明该有效时空在坐标变换下光滑延拓且测地完备，表明固定经典背景上的量子动力学无需完整的量子引力理论即可正则化史瓦西奇点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典广义相对论中史瓦西（Schwarzschild）时空存在曲率奇点，该奇点预示着物理学定律的失效。本文旨在探索是否可以在不依赖完整量子引力（quantum gravity）理论的前提下，通过半经典（semiclassical）方法中量子效应来消除或正则化该奇点。

Method: 采用Klein-Gordon波包的Madelung-Bohm分解（Madelung-Bohm decomposition），将量子修正运动描述为在一个与史瓦西度规共形相关（conformally related）的有效度量中的测地运动，共形因子由波函数振幅决定。通过求解$r\to 0$附近的波函数方程来确定该共形因子。

Result: 在合适的坐标下，内部区域可光滑延拓（extends smoothly），有效时空的曲率不变量（curvature invariants）有限，且该有效时空是测地完备（geodesically complete）的，从而消除了史瓦西奇点。

Conclusion: 固定经典背景上的量子动力学（quantum dynamics on a fixed classical background）可以在不引入完整量子引力理论的情况下正则化史瓦西奇点，这为奇点问题提供了一条新的半经典解决途径。

Abstract: We revisit the Schwarzschild singularity in a semiclassical setting where the background geometry is classical and quantum effects enter through Bohmian (quantal) trajectories associated with a Klein Gordon wave packet. Using the Madelung-Bohm decomposition of the Klein Gordon wavefunction, we show that the quantum-modified motion is equivalent to geodesic motion in an effective metric conformally related to Schwarzschild, with a conformal factor fixed by the wavefunction amplitude. Solving the wavefunction equation near $r\to 0$ determines this factor and yields finite curvature invariants, in suitable coordinates the interior extends smoothly and the effective spacetime is geodesically complete. This suggests that quantum dynamics on a fixed classical background can regularize the Schwarzschild singularity without a full theory of quantum gravity.

### [103] [When Weak Fields Arent Weak: Post-Newtonian effective theory and the Dark Matter Puzzle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13557)
*Marco Galoppo,Giorgio Torrieri*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文论证后牛顿理论（post-Newtonian theory）作为广义相对论在弱场慢速极限下的有效展开并不可靠；在多体相对论动力学中，全局守恒荷缺失与非可积性（non-integrability）会导致对非均匀曲率中角动量交换的强敏感性，从而破坏有效理论展开中的幂次计数（power counting）。作者基于有效场论（effective field theory）的一般原理，推导出一个明确的失效判据，并为弱场质量推断提供了可控的系统框架，该结果与天体物理和宇宙学中的暗物质难题相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 后牛顿理论通常被视为广义相对论在弱场和慢速极限下可靠的有效展开，但作者认为这种信念可能误导了对理论适用范围的判断。

Method: 作者从有效场论的一般原理出发，分析多体相对论动力学中全局守恒荷缺失与非可积性对有效展开的影响，并推导出后牛顿截断失效的明确判据。

Result: 发现即使局部势场和速度很小，多体系统中的角动量交换仍会破坏幂次计数（power counting），导致后牛顿截断不可靠；并给出了一个明确的失效界限判据。

Conclusion: 该研究为弱场下的质量推断提供了可控的系统性框架，其结论对天体物理和宇宙学中的暗物质问题具有重要关联。

Abstract: Post-Newtonian theory is considered a reliable effective expansion of General Relativity in the weak-field and slow-motion limit. We argue that such a belief is misplaced. In generic many-body relativistic dynamics, the absence of globally conserved charges in the region of interest and non-integrability can drive strong sensitivity to angular-momentum exchange across inhomogeneous curvature, invalidating naive power counting in an effective theory expansion. Building on general lessons from effective field theory, we derive an explicit breakdown criterion that delineates when post-Newtonian truncations become unreliable despite small local potentials and velocities. This supplies a controlled systematic for weak-field mass inference, relevant to the dark matter puzzle in astrophysics and cosmology.

</details>


### [104] [Cosmological horizons in regular bouncing backgrounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13636)
*M. Gasperini*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文指出，宇宙学中关于标准减速膨胀阶段无全局事件视界（global event horizons）、加速膨胀阶段无粒子视界（particle horizons）的常见论断并不必然成立。原因在于这类视界是时空几何的非局域性质，依赖于宇宙学背景的完整过去与未来历史。论文通过正则反弹（regular bounce）将最终标准膨胀与初始曲率增长阶段连接，给出了多种不同场景的示例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挑战宇宙学中广为接受的断言，即减速膨胀阶段必然无全局事件视界而加速膨胀阶段必然无粒子视界，指出该断言忽视了视界作为时空几何非局域性质（non-local properties）所依赖的完整历史信息。

Method: 通过构造理论示例，展示将最终标准膨胀（即减速膨胀、曲率递减）阶段经由正则反弹连接至初始（可能无限延伸的）曲率增长阶段的不同宇宙学场景，以此检验视界的存在性条件。

Result: 发现上述常见论断并不总是成立：视界的存在与否取决于宇宙学背景的完整（过去与未来）历史，而非仅由当前膨胀状态决定。所提供的多种反弹宇宙学场景显示，标准膨胀阶段同样可以存在全局事件视界。

Conclusion: 宇宙学视界的存在性不能仅由当前膨胀阶段（减速或加速）简单判定，必须考虑时空背景的完整演化历史。正则反弹宇宙模型为重新审视视界概念提供了有效框架。

Abstract: It is often stated that a phase of standard, decelerated cosmological expansion is characterised by the absence of global event horizons, while a phase of accelerated expansion is associated with the absence of particle horizons. This is not necessarily true because such horizons, being non-local properties of the spacetime geometry, depend on the full (past and future) history of the given cosmological background. We provide examples of various different scenarios for the case in which the final asymptotic phase of standard expansion and decreasing curvature is connected, through a regular bounce, with an initial (and possibly infinitely extended in time) regime of growing curvature.

</details>


### [105] [Quantum Field Theory of Black Hole Perturbations with Backreaction VI. Apparent Horizons, Quasi-Local Mass and Effective Classical Metrics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13714)
*Jonas Neuser,Thomas Thiemann*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文发展了一种从第一性原理出发、规范不变的黑洞微扰论方法，计算了至二阶的视界形状与约化相空间动力学，并展示了如何通过量子期望值构造有效经典度规，进而修正彭罗斯图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有黑洞微扰论缺乏同时满足第一性原理、规范不变性、且能处理任意阶反作用（back reaction）效应的统一框架；蒸发黑洞的物理描述尤其依赖视界（apparent horizon）这一观测者依赖的概念，需要更系统的微扰处理。

Method: 采用规范不变的第一性原理微扰论方法，将反作用效应纳入至二阶；通过约化相空间（reduced phase space）变量描述动力学，并由此重构完整的四维度规；在量子理论中取度规的期望值，获得有效经典度规并分析其因果结构。

Result: 得到了约化相空间至二阶的显式动力学表达式；确定了表观视界至二阶的形状；展示了如何从约化相空间变量重构完整四维度规；给出了量子修正彭罗斯图（Penrose diagram）的可视化方法。

Conclusion: 该工作为蒸发黑洞的量子描述提供了微扰框架，指出表观视界面积在量子理论中因霍金蒸发（Hawking evaporation）而减小，并展望了在约化相空间形式下进行量子化及其对视界面积的影响。

Abstract: In a recent series of papers we developed a first-principle and gauge invariant approach to black hole perturbation theory valid to any order. We included back reaction effects to tackle the situation of evaporating black holes and obtained an explicit expression for the dynamics of the reduced phase space to second order. The physics of evaporating black holes is in particular encoded by apparent horizons, an observer dependent generalisation of the event horizon. We determine the shape of the apparent horizon to second order in the perturbations. The area of the apparent horizon is an interesting observable which is expected to decrease in the quantum theory due to Hawking evaporation. We show how the full four dimensional metric can be reconstructed in terms of the reduced phase space variables. In the quantum theory, taking expectation values of this metric, we obtain an effective classical metric, whose causal structure can then be visualised in a quantum corrected Penrose diagram. We conclude with an outlook into the quantisation procedure in the reduced phase space formalism and the implications on the area of the apparent horizon.

</details>


### [106] [Cosmological perturbations in the theory of gravity with non-minimal derivative coupling. I. Modes of perturbations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13732)
*R. I. Kamalitdinov,S. V. Sushkov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在非最小导数耦合引力理论框架下，推导了平坦FLRW宇宙中标量、矢量和张量扰动模式的完整演化方程，并发现所有扰动模式（包括矢量模式）在准德西特暴胀阶段均被放大，这与标准弗里德曼宇宙学行为截然不同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究具有非最小导数耦合（non-minimal derivative coupling）的引力理论中的宇宙学微扰行为，探索该理论是否能产生与标准宇宙学不同的早期扰动演化特征。

Method: 采用具有平坦空间FLRW度规的各向同性均匀宇宙模型，在包含耦合项 $ηG^{μν}\nabla_μφ\nabla_νφ$ 的Horndeski拉格朗日量框架下，推导出标量、矢量和张量扰动模式的完整演化方程组，并在渐近情形下进行解析分析，随后构建精确数值解描述模式的完整演化。

Result: 所有扰动模式（包括矢量模式）在准德西特（quasi-de Sitter）暴胀阶段均被放大，这一行为与标准弗里德曼宇宙学（Friedmann cosmology）中矢量模式衰减的特征有根本性区别。

Conclusion: 非最小导数耦合项在早期主导宇宙演化并产生无需精细调节势能的暴胀阶段，后期自然过渡到标准宇宙学演化。该机制下所有扰动模式的放大为早期宇宙结构形成提供了不同于传统暴胀图景的演化路径。

Abstract: We consider perturbations in the isotropic and homogeneous cosmological model with the spatially flat Friedmann-Lemaitre-Robertson-Walker metric in the framework of the theory of gravity with non-minimal derivative coupling. The Lagrangian of the theory contains the coupling term $ηG^{μν}\nabla_μφ\nabla_νφ$ and represents the particular example of a general Horndeski Lagrangian, which results in second-order field equations. It is known that the non-minimal derivative coupling crucially changes scenarios of the Universe evolution on early times. In particular, the $η$-term is dominating on early times and leads to a primary quasi-de Sitter (inflationary) stage which needs no fine-tuned potential. On late times the influence of non-minimal derivative coupling on the Universe evolution completely disappears, and this naturally leads to the transition to the standard cosmological evolution (post-inflationary stage). We have derived a complete set of equations which describe an evolution of scalar, vector and tensor modes of perturbations. All modes are analyzed analytically in two asymptotic cases, and then we construct exact numerical solutions which describe an entire evolution of the modes. We show that all modes, including vector ones, are amplified in the quasi-de Sitter (inflationary) stage, and such the behavior is cardinally distinct from that in Friedmann cosmology.

</details>


### [107] [Thin Accretion Disks around Rotating Charged Black Holes in an Effective Higher-Curvature Spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13797)
*Mohammad Hassani,Kourosh Nozari,Sara Saghafi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了一个由旋转带电黑洞（rotating charged black hole）周围薄吸积盘（thin accretion disk）的结构与辐射性质，该黑洞由有效高曲率启发时空（effective higher-curvature-inspired spacetime）描述，是Kerr-Newman几何的现象学变形。通过引入类似高斯-博内（Gauss-Bonnet）的有效参数α变形度量函数Δ，发现增大α会使最内稳定圆轨道（ISCO）向内移动，增强盘的辐射通量与温度，而电荷Q则抑制这些量，表明吸积盘可作为探测强引力效应的敏感探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准广义相对论下Kerr或Kerr-Newman黑洞的吸积盘模型已被广泛研究，但高曲率修正（higher-curvature corrections）对吸积盘观测特征的影响尚未充分探索。本文旨在构建一种不依赖具体引力理论的现象学框架，通过有效参数α描述高曲率变形，系统研究其对吸积盘结构和辐射性质的调制作用，从而为未来观测检验强引力物理提供理论判据。

Method: 采用运动学方法（kinematical approach），基于测试粒子运动（test-particle motion）推导圆形轨道的比能量（specific energy）、比角动量（specific angular momentum）和角速度（angular velocity）。进而分析变形参数α与电荷Q对最内稳定圆轨道（ISCO）、辐射效率（radiative efficiency）、辐射通量（radiation flux）、温度（temperature）以及盘的微分光度（differential luminosity）的影响。

Result: 增大参数α使ISCO向内移动，并增强盘的辐射通量和温度；电荷Q的存在则因静电效应（electrostatic effects）抑制这些量。吸积盘的辐射特征对α和Q的取值敏感，呈现出与标准Kerr情形显著偏离的观测信号。

Conclusion: 有效高曲率变形（effective higher curvature deformations）的旋转黑洞时空可以在吸积盘辐射中产生可观测的偏离，表明吸积盘可作为强引力效应（strong-gravity effects）的灵敏探针，且该结论不依赖于具体的底层引力理论（underlying gravitational theory）。

Abstract: We investigate the structure and emission properties of a thin accretion disk around a rotating charged black hole described by an effective higher-curvature-inspired spacetime, constructed as a phenomenological deformation of the Kerr Newman geometry. In this framework, the deformation is introduced through a modification of the metric function $Δ$ by an effective Gauss-Bonnet-like parameter $α$, such that the spacetime reduces to the standard Kerr Newman solution in the limit $α\to 0$. Adopting a kinematical approach, we use test-particle motion to derive the specific energy, specific angular momentum, and angular velocity of circular orbits, and analyze the effects of the parameters $α$ and charge $Q$ on the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO), radiative efficiency, radiation flux, temperature, and differential luminosity of the disk. We find that increasing $α$ shifts the ISCO inward and enhances the disk's radiation flux and temperature, while the presence of charge suppresses these quantities due to electrostatic effects. Our results demonstrate that effective higher curvature deformations of rotating black hole spacetimes can lead to observable deviations from the Kerr case, highlighting accretion disks as sensitive probes of strong-gravity effects without relying on a specific underlying gravitational theory.

</details>


### [108] [Analytical Fluxes from Generic Schwarzschild Geodesics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13847)
*Majed Khalaf,Chris Kavanagh,Ofri Telem*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种解析方法，用于计算任意偏心率下束缚史瓦西测地线（bound Schwarzschild geodesics）的引力波通量（gravitational-wave fluxes）。该方法通过在切比雪夫基（Chebyshev basis）中系统地展开辐射的傅里叶系数，将其约化为之前量子谱方法（Quantum Spectral Method）中推导的类开普勒傅里叶系数之和。由于不依赖小偏心率展开，该方法适用于大范围束缚偏心轨道。在15后牛顿（PN, post-Newtonian）展开输入下的数值验证表明，该方法在弱场和强场情形下均能达到高精度，为极端质量比旋近（EMRI, extreme-mass-ratio inspiral）建模中的频域通量计算提供了解析路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 计算任意偏心率下束缚史瓦西测地线的引力波通量是极端质量比旋近建模的关键环节；现有方法多依赖小偏心率展开，适用范围受限，且频域通量的解析计算仍面临挑战。

Method: 提出一种解析方法，将辐射的傅里叶系数在切比雪夫基中展开，通过代数变换将其降为量子谱方法中已知的类开普勒傅里叶系数之和；该方法不依赖于小偏心率展开，因而适用于任意偏心率的束缚轨道，并使用15后牛顿展开的输入进行数值实现与验证。

Result: 在弱场情形 $(p,e)=(12.5,0.5)$ 下，总通量的相对精度达到 $10^{-5}$；在强场情形 $(p,e)=(10,0.8)$ 下，所选主导模式的加权逐模误差低于 $10^{-6}$。

Conclusion: 该解析方法为极端质量比旋近建模中的频域通量计算提供了一条有效的解析途径，且在高偏心率及强场区域均具有良好精度。

Abstract: We present an analytic method for computing gravitational-wave fluxes from bound Schwarzschild geodesics with arbitrary eccentricity. Our approach systematically expands the Fourier coefficients of the emitted radiation in a Chebyshev basis, allowing them to be reduced to sums of Keplerian-like Fourier coefficients previously derived in the Quantum Spectral Method. Because the construction does not rely on a small-eccentricity expansion, it applies to a broad range of bound eccentric orbits. As an illustration, we implement the method using a $15$PN-expanded input and find that it reproduces the total flux for the case $(p,e)=(12.5,0.5)$ to relative accuracy $10^{-5}$, while for the stronger-field case $(p,e)=(10,0.8)$ it yields weighted mode-by-mode errors below $10^{-6}$ for the selected dominant modes analyzed. These results provide an analytic route to frequency-domain flux calculations relevant to EMRI modeling.

</details>

### [109] [Inpainting over the cracks: challenges of applying pre-merger searches for massive black hole binaries to realistic LISA datasets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13738)
*Gareth Cabourn Davies,Ian Harry*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文演示并比较了两种在大合并前识别大质量黑洞双星（massive black hole binaries）的方法——零延迟滤波（zero-latency filter）与首次使用的“修补”（inpainting）技术。在LISA数据挑战集Sangria-HM上成功恢复14个信号，并证明inpainting方法能在数据存在缺口及重叠信号场景下有效工作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实现大质量黑洞并合的多信使（multi-messenger）观测是LISA的核心科学目标之一。在合并且前数小时、数天乃至数周内提前识别事件并提供更新的天区定位，对于触发电磁波段（electromagnetic）后随观测至关重要。

Method: 本文采用两种方法进行合并前识别：一是零延迟滤波方法（zero-latency filter approach）；二是首次引入的“修补”（inpainting）技术。两种方法均应用于LISA数据挑战集2a——Sangria-HM数据集。此外，通过人为引入3天数据缺口以及处理重叠信号区域来测试方法鲁棒性。

Result: 两种方法成功恢复了数据集中预期可在合并前至少半天识别的14个信号。inpainting方法即使在合并前14天存在3天数据缺口的情况下仍能成功恢复信号。在处理重叠信号区域（10天内多个信号合并）时，通过移除已确认的强信号，成功识别出同一时段内更微弱的信号。

Conclusion: 零延迟滤波与inpainting方法均可有效实现大质量黑洞双星的合并前识别。inpainting方法在处理数据缺口和重叠信号等复杂场景下展现出明显优势，为LISA多信使天文学（multimessenger astronomy）的关键技术路径提供了有力支撑。

Abstract: A key science target of the Large Interferometer Space Antenna (LISA) is to carry out multi-messenger observations of massive black hole binaries, observing the merger simultaneously in gravitational waves and with electromagnetic observatories. Identifying that a merger is happening and providing an updating estimate of the sky location in the hours, days and weeks before the merger is critical to enable electromagnetic observations of the merger event. In this work we demonstrate and compare two methods for premerger identification of massive black hole binaries; a zero-latency filter approach and, for the first time, an approach using an ``inpainting'' technique. We apply these methods to the LISA Data Challenge dataset 2a--Sangria-HM--and demonstrate the successful recovery of the 14 signals in the dataset that we expected to be identifiable at least half a day before merger. We show that the inpainting method can identify premerger signals even when gaps are present in the data, demonstrating the recovery of a signal even when 3 day-long data gaps are added to the 14 days preceding merger. Finally, we explore the challenge of overlapping signals, using a region of overlapping signals in the Sangria-HM dataset, all of which merge within a 10-day window, and show how removing signals that have been confidently identified from the data allows us to identify quieter signals in the same period.

</details>

### [110] [Random Access Code protocols: Quantum advantage related to intraparticle entanglement-based contextuality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13350)
*Nilaj Saha,Sumit Mukherjee,Dipankar Home*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过利用单粒子的内禀纠缠（intraparticle entanglement）——例如同一粒子的自旋/偏振与路径自由度之间的纠缠——来研究随机存取码（RAC）协议中成功概率的量子增强。研究发现，基于非上下文性（noncontextuality）假设导出的贝尔型不等式（Bell-type inequality）的量子违背幅度，与内禀纠缠辅助的n比特RAC协议的成功概率量子增强程度定量对应，且最大成功概率对应最大量子违背。该对应可通过单粒子干涉实验进行检验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究未从两个重要视角探索随机存取码（RAC）协议中成功概率的量子增强：一是未研究利用单粒子内部两个可共轭测量自由度之间的纠缠（内禀纠缠，intraparticle entanglement）；二是未建立预测/观测到的量子优势与底层量子资源之间的明确定量对应关系。本文旨在同时解决这两方面问题。

Method: 将RAC协议重新表述为基于单粒子内禀纠缠（例如自旋/偏振与路径自由度之间）的形式，并利用从非上下文性（noncontextuality）假设导出的贝尔型不等式（Bell-type inequality）进行分析。所需的实验装置为仅需维持单粒子相干性（coherence）的单粒子干涉系统（interferometric setup）。

Result: 分析表明，贝尔型不等式的量子力学违背（quantum-mechanical violation）幅度——标志着一种量子上下文性（quantum contextuality）——与任何内禀纠缠辅助的n比特RAC协议中成功概率的量子增强程度定量一致（quantitatively commensurate）。具体而言，量子n↦1 RAC协议的最大成功概率对应于相关贝尔型不等式的最大量子违背。

Conclusion: 本文建立了RAC协议量子优势与单粒子内禀纠缠及量子上下文性之间的定量对应关系，该对应关系可通过易于实现的单粒子干涉装置进行实验检验，为理解量子资源在信息处理中的角色提供了新的视角。

Abstract: The quantum enhancement of success probability in the Random Access Code (RAC) protocols remains unexplored from two important perspectives. First, the use of entanglement between two co-measurable degrees of freedom of a single particle (intraparticle entanglement) in achieving such quantum enhancement has not been investigated. Second, no explicit quantitative correspondence has been established between the predicted/observed quantum advantage and the underlying quantum resource responsible for it. In this work, we address both these aspects simultaneously by harnessing a single-particle resource. For this purpose, the RAC protocol is formulated in terms of intraparticle entanglement between, for instance, spin/polarization and path degrees of freedom of a single particle. Within this framework, a relevant Bell-type inequality, derived from the assumption of noncontextuality for single particle path-spin measurements, is used. Based on these ingredients, the formulated analysis reveals that the magnitude of quantum-mechanical violation of such Bell-type inequality, signifying a form of quantum contextuality, is quantitatively commensurate with the quantum enhancement of success probability in any intraparticle entanglement-assisted $n$-bit RAC protocol. In particular, the maximal success probability of a quantum $n \mapsto 1$ RAC protocol corresponds to the maximal quantum violation of the relevant Bell-type inequality. This correspondence is empirically testable using a readily implementable single-particle interferometric setup requiring coherence preservation only for a single particle.

</details>


### [111] [Berry-Phase-Induced Chirality in Thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13685)
*Zhaoyu Fei,Yu-Han Ma*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过发展耗散绝热微扰展开（dissipative adiabatic perturbation expansion），发现贝里相位（Berry phase）可以诱导出在退相干（decoherence）条件下仍存活的手性功差（chiral work difference）。该手性特征从幺正（unitary）区域中的干涉热力学阿哈罗诺夫-玻姆效应（interferometric thermodynamic Aharonov-Bohm effect）演化为耗散区域中的无条纹信号。作者在两能级系统中阐释了该框架，并评估了其实验可行性，从而澄清了量子几何（quantum geometry）在热力学几何化表述中的作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 几何相位（geometric phase）是孤立量子系统的基础概念，但其在开放系统中的热力学角色尚未被揭示。本文旨在填补这一空白，探索贝里相位在耗散环境中的热力学效应。

Method: 作者发展了一种耗散绝热微扰展开方法，用以分析开放量子系统中的几何相位效应。在此基础上，通过两能级系统（two-level system）的模型化计算，考察了贝里相位诱导的手性功差及其在不同退相干强度下的演化行为。

Result: 发现存在一种贝里相位诱导的手性功差，该功差在退相干条件下仍然存活。该手性特征从幺正区域中的干涉热力学阿哈罗诺夫-玻姆效应逐步转变为耗散区域中的无条纹信号。

Conclusion: 本工作阐明了量子几何在热力学几何化表述（geometric formulation of thermodynamics）中的关键作用，并为未来在开放量子系统中实验观测几何热力学效应提供了理论基础与可行性评估。

Abstract: Geometric phases are foundational to isolated quantum systems, yet their thermodynamic role in open systems remains unrevealed Developing a dissipative adiabatic perturbation expansion, we discover a Berry-phase-induced chiral work difference that survives decoherence. This chirality evolves from an interferometric thermodynamic Aharonov-Bohm effect in the unitary regime to a fringe-free signal in the dissipative regime. We illustrate this framework in a two-level system and assess its experimental feasibility. Our findings clarify the role of quantum geometry in the geometric formulation of thermodynamics.

</details>


### [112] [Microscopic Origins of Collapse Models: Decoherence from Graviton Bremsstrahlung](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12955)
*Moslem Zarei*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用量子玻尔兹曼方程（QBE）分析费米子在引力子发射下的空间叠加态行为，推导退相干率（decoherence rate）并建立定量指标连接叠加稳定性与空间分离、粒子质量及引力耦合强度，为引力诱导的波函数坍缩提供了细致的理论框架，并讨论了对耗散连续自发定域化（CSL）模型等坍缩模型的实验检验意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 部分坍缩模型（collapse models）提出引力效应会导致质量分布叠加态不稳定进而引发波函数坍缩，但该机制缺乏从量子场论（quantum field theory）出发的定量分析框架。本文旨在填补这一空白，通过量子玻尔兹曼方程（QBE）系统研究引力诱导退相干（gravity induced decoherence）的具体依赖关系。

Method: 使用量子玻尔兹曼方程（QBE）分析处于空间叠加态（spatial superposition）的费米子（fermion）在引力子（graviton）发射过程中的动力学行为；引入定量指标（quantitative measure）将叠加态稳定性与空间分离距离、粒子质量和引力耦合强度联系起来；通过考察QBE中的碰撞项（collision term）推导退相干率（decoherence rate）的具体参数依赖关系。

Result: 推导出了退相干率（decoherence rate），并明确了其如何依赖于空间分离、粒子质量及引力耦合等参数。研究建立了一个将量子场论（quantum field theory）与坍缩模型（collapse models）衔接起来的细致框架。

Conclusion: 该结果为理解引力诱导退相干（gravity induced decoherence）提供了详细的理论框架。研究结论对引力诱导波函数坍缩（gravitationally induced wave function collapse）的实验检验具有参考价值，并有望推广至耗散连续自发定域化（CSL）模型等更广泛的坍缩模型类别。

Abstract: Some collapse models proposed that gravitational effects cause the instability of mass distribution superpositions, leading to wave function collapse. In this paper, we utilize the quantum Boltzmann equation (QBE) to analyze the behavior of a fermion in a spatial superposition under graviton emission. We introduce a quantitative measure that links the stability of the superposition to the spatial separation, particle mass, and gravitational coupling. By examining the collision term in the QBE, we derive the decoherence rate and show how it depends on these parameters. Our results provide a detailed framework for understanding gravity induced decoherence, bridging the gap between quantum field theory and collapse models. We also discuss the implications of these findings for experimental tests of gravitationally induced wave function collapse and the broader class of collapse models known as dissipative continuous spontaneous localization (CSL) model.

</details>


### [113] [No chaos required: traversable wormhole signals survive 98% coupling deletion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13241)
*Sagar Dubey*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文通过在 coupled Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev (SYK) 模型中系统性地破坏量子混沌（quantum chaos），证明可穿越虫洞（traversable wormhole）协议中的传输信号 C(t) 仅由系统间耦合强度 mu 控制，与内部混沌无关，因此该信号诊断的是耦合保真度而非全息动力学（holographic dynamics）。这一不变性意味着可以丢弃98%的哈密顿量耦合项，将每个 Trotter 步的量子门数降低约50倍，使更大规模的虫洞模拟实验变得可行。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 最近的研究质疑可穿越虫洞协议中的传输信号 C(t) 是否真正反映全息动力学，因为类似信号也出现在一般热化系统中。本文旨在澄清该信号的实际探测对象，通过破坏SYK模型中的量子混沌，观察信号在混沌-可积转变过程中的行为。

Method: 采用随机删除耦合（random coupling deletion）的方式系统性地破坏SYK模型中的量子混沌，监控跨越混沌到可积（chaos-to-integrable）转变过程中的传输信号。对N=10的双SYK模型进行精确对角化（exact diagonalization），每种稀疏度使用50个无序实现（disorder realization），并辅以Krylov子空间扩展至N=20。

Result: 在50倍的稀疏化范围内，系综平均的峰值高度变化小于1.1%，而底层谱统计从高斯幺正系综（Gaussian-unitary-ensemble）转变为亚泊松统计（sub-Poisson statistics）。对系统间耦合 mu 进行的1200次扫描确认，信号仅由 mu 控制，与内部混沌无关。热场双态（thermofield double state）在稀疏化下仍保持其热结构。

Conclusion: 传输信号诊断的是系统间耦合保真度（inter-system coupling fidelity）而非全息动力学，未来的量子模拟实验需要独立的混沌诊断来支撑引力解释。实际应用中，98%的哈密顿量耦合项可以丢弃（幸存项需方差重缩放），在N=10时每个Trotter步的门数减少约50倍，使更大规模的可穿越虫洞模拟实验变得可行。

Abstract: The traversable wormhole protocol in coupled Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev (SYK) systems produces a transmission signal C(t) widely interpreted as evidence of holographic dynamics. Recent work has questioned this interpretation, showing that similar signals arise in generic thermalizing systems. We address what the signal actually probes by systematically destroying quantum chaos in the SYK model via random coupling deletion, while monitoring the transmission signal across the chaos-to-integrable transition. Using exact diagonalization of the doubled SYK model at N=10 with 50 disorder realizations per sparsity, supplemented by Krylov-subspace extensions to N=20, we find that the ensemble-averaged peak height varies by less than 1.1% across a 50-fold sparsification range, even as the underlying spectrum transitions from Gaussian-unitary-ensemble to sub-Poisson statistics. A 1,200-instance sweep over the inter-system coupling mu confirms that the signal is controlled by mu alone, with no dependence on internal chaos. We further verify that the thermofield double state retains its thermal structure under sparsification despite substantial changes to the state vector, providing a structural explanation for the invariance. These results indicate that the transmission signal diagnoses inter-system coupling fidelity rather than holographic dynamics, and that future quantum-simulation experiments require independent chaos diagnostics to substantiate gravitational claims. As a practical consequence, the invariance implies that 98% of the Hamiltonian's coupling terms can be discarded (with variance rescaling of the survivors), reducing the gate count per Trotter step by approximately 50x at N=10 and bringing larger traversable-wormhole simulations within experimental reach.

</details>


### [114] [Universal Design and Physical Applications of Non-Uniform Cellular Automata on Translationally Invariant Lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13379)
*Xiang-You Huang,Jie-Yu Zhang,Peng Ye*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文发展了一种高阶非均匀元胞自动机（NUCA）算法，可同时适用于欧几里得与双曲格子，通过在双曲{5,4}格子上生成子系统对称性保护拓扑相、模拟有向逾渗过程等应用，展示了该算法的广泛适用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双曲格子（hyperbolic lattices）具有恒定负曲率与非阿贝尔平移对称性，是研究格子几何与物理相互作用的丰富平台，但格子规模的指数增长与非平凡平移对称性使得基于欧几里得格子（Euclidean lattices）的方法无法直接适用，这一局限在均匀元胞自动机（CA）中尤为突出。

Method: 发展了一种高阶非均匀元胞自动机（non-uniform cellular automata, NUCA）算法，通过格子变形（lattice-deforming）过程将非平凡的几何数据纳入非均匀更新规则中，使其同时适用于平移不变的规则欧几里得格子和双曲格子。

Result: 在双曲{5,4}格子上：通过线性NUCA生成了在欧几里得格子上无法实现的、与规则或不规则子系统对称性相关的子系统对称性保护拓扑态（SSPT states）及自发子系统对称性破缺态；设计了多点奇异关联子（multi-point strange correlators）以检测非平凡SSPT态，并导出了非阿贝尔平移不变NUCA生成模型的充分条件。将NUCA推广至非均匀克利福德量子元胞自动机（CQCA），生成了双曲簇态的子系统对称性。通过概率性NUCA模拟有向逾渗（DP）过程，数值估计了逾渗阈值与相图。

Conclusion: 本文发展的NUCA算法有效解决了双曲格子上因指数增长的格点规模与非平凡平移对称性带来的计算困难，为在双曲几何中探索新型拓扑相与临界现象提供了通用工具。

Abstract: Lattice geometry profoundly shapes physical phenomena such as subsystem symmetry and directed percolation (DP). Among various lattice geometries, hyperbolic lattices are characterized by constant negative curvature and non-Abelian translation symmetry, offering a rich platform for investigating this geometry-physics interplay. However, the exponentially growing lattice size and nontrivial translation symmetry make approaches developed for Euclidean lattices incompatible, a limitation particularly evident in uniform cellular automata (CA). To resolve this, we develop a higher-order non-uniform cellular automata (NUCA) algorithm applicable to both translationally invariant regular Euclidean and hyperbolic lattices. In the algorithm, the non-uniform update rules incorporate nontrivial geometric data through a lattice-deforming procedure. We demonstrate the broad applicability of our algorithm to hyperbolic lattices through several applications on the hyperbolic $\{5,4\}$ lattice. By applying a linear NUCA, we generate subsystem symmetry-protected topological (SSPT) states and spontaneous subsystem symmetry-breaking states associated with regular or irregular subsystem symmetries unattainable on Euclidean lattices. We design the multi-point strange correlators to detect nontrivial SSPT states and derive a sufficient condition for non-Abelian translationally invariant NUCA-generated models. Furthermore, by generalizing the NUCA to non-uniform Clifford quantum cellular automata (CQCA), we generate subsystem symmetries of the hyperbolic cluster state, extending the established correspondence between translationally invariant CQCA and subsystem symmetries. Moreover, we simulate the DP process via a probabilistic NUCA that inherits the treelike structure of the lattice, and numerically estimate percolation thresholds and the phase diagram.

</details>
