### [115] [Coherent control of spinmons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12588)
*Johanne Bratland Tjernshaugen,Florinda Viñas Boström,Jeroen Danon,Jacob Linder,Karsten Flensberg,Antonio L. R. Manesco*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为“自旋子（spinmon）”的新超导量子比特设计，通过将transmon与束缚安德烈夫准粒子（Andreev quasiparticle）的自旋纠缠，利用塞曼场（Zeeman field）解除Kramers简并，并通过静电门控和AC磁通驱动实现全量子比特控制，从而避免传统超导量子比特在不同噪声通道之间的保护/敏感权衡，并验证了其对磁通噪声和电荷噪声的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统超导量子比特在抑制某些噪声源时往往会增加对其他退相干通道（decoherence channels）的敏感性，存在一种保护/敏感权衡（tradeoff）。本文旨在探索一种避免这种权衡的编码路径。

Method: 将量子信息编码在transmon的量子态与束缚安德烈夫准粒子（Andreev quasiparticle）自旋的纠缠态中，构造出自旋子（spinmon）器件。引入塞曼场（Zeeman field）解除Kramers简并，并通过静电门控（electrostatic gates）和AC磁通驱动（AC flux drive）实现两种全量子比特控制方案。

Result: 计算了自旋子的相干时间（coherence times），并验证了该量子比特对磁通噪声（flux noise）和电荷噪声（charge noise）的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 自旋子设计能够规避传统超导量子比特在噪声保护与敏感性之间的权衡，为实验实现提供了多种方向，具有较好的噪声鲁棒性。

Abstract: The protection of superconducting qubits from certain noise sources often comes at the cost of increased sensitivity to other decoherence channels. Here, we explore a route to avoid this tradeoff by encoding quantum information in quantum states of a transmon entangled with the spin of a trapped Andreev quasiparticle. We term such devices spinmons. We lift the spinmon Kramers degeneracy by introducing a Zeeman field and develop two routes for full qubit control via electrostatic gates and an AC flux drive, providing multiple directions for experimental implementations. Finally, we compute coherence times and verify the qubit robustness against flux and charge noise sources.

</details>


### [116] [Coupled Topological Interface States and Phonon Molecules in GaAs/AlAs Superlattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12635)
*S. Sandeep,O. Colmegna,C. Xiang,E. R. Cardozo de Oliveira,K. Papatryfonos,M. Morassi,A. Lemaitre,N. D. Lanzillotti-Kimura*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文在GaAs/AlAs分布布拉格反射镜（DBR）超晶格中，基于Su-Schrieffer-Heeger（SSH）框架下的拓扑界面态，实验展示了可调谐的拓扑声子分子及扩展链结构，并通过时域泵浦-探测瞬态反射率测量验证了其GHz频段的耦合行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用一维超晶格中拓扑保护（topologically protected）的界面态，构建可调控的耦合纳米声子系统，突破孤立界面态的功能局限，为GHz频段纳米声子架构提供鲁棒的平台。

Method: 通过拼接三个具有交替拓扑的超晶格，在Su-Schrieffer-Heeger（SSH）框架下利用带反转（band inversion）和Zak相位（Zak phase）调控，构建耦合界面态；采用分子束外延（molecular beam epitaxy）生长GaAs/AlAs异质结构，并通过时域泵浦-探测瞬态反射率测量（time-domain pump-probe transient reflectivity）进行实验观测，辅以传输矩阵（transfer-matrix）计算和解析模型。

Result: 实现了两个耦合界面态的杂化对称和反对称模式，其分裂可在数十GHz范围内通过中心DBR反射率进行调谐；进一步构建了最多N=6个耦合界面态的链，形成窄拓扑微带（topological miniband），同时保持界面强局域性。实验观测与传输矩阵计算及解析模型吻合。

Conclusion: 拓扑界面态可作为工程化耦合声子系统及GHz频段可调谐纳米声子架构的鲁棒平台，拓展了拓扑声子学（topological phononics）在纳米尺度声子操控中的应用潜力。

Abstract: Topological interface states in one-dimensional superlattices provide spatially localized phonon modes protected by the topology of the underlying band structure. In GaAs/AlAs distributed Bragg reflectors (DBRs), such states can be engineered through band inversion between superlattices with opposite Zak phases within the Su-Schrieffer-Heeger (SSH) framework. Here, we demonstrate topological phonon molecules and extended chains formed by coupled nanophononic interface states. By concatenating three superlattices with alternating topology, we realize two coupled interface states that hybridize into symmetric and antisymmetric modes, whose splitting can be tuned over tens of gigahertz by varying the reflectivity of the central DBR. Extending this concept, we engineer chains of up to N=6 coupled interface states that form narrow topological minibands while remaining strongly localized at the interfaces. We experimentally observe these coupled states in molecular-beam-epitaxy-grown GaAs/AlAs heterostructures using time-domain pump-probe transient reflectivity measurements, and reproduce their behavior using transfer-matrix calculations and a simple analytical model for the mode splitting. These results establish topological interface states as a robust platform for engineering coupled phononic systems and tunable nanophononic architectures in the GHz regime.

### [117] [Direct-write electrochemical nanofabrication of ultrasmall graphene devices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12660)
*Xiao Liu,Colm Durkan*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 石墨烯纳米带（Graphene nano-ribbons, GNRs）因其优异的电学和热学性能以及尺寸可调带隙，是下一代超小型化器件的有前途的沟道材料，但传统光刻和电子束光刻方法在集成到晶体管技术中时面临高成本和复杂工艺等挑战。

Method: 采用电化学原子力显微镜光刻（electrochemical atomic force microscopy lithography），在交流偏压（alternating current bias）条件下，对石墨烯进行直写图案化，无需电极辅助，实现特征尺寸低于10纳米的精确纳米级图案。

Result: 该方法相较于传统光刻和电子束光刻，具有更高分辨率、更低缺陷密度、无污染处理，以及原位纳米级器件修饰和表征能力。

Conclusion: 本研究为推进基于GNR的纳米电子学提供了一种高效策略，有望克服现有制造瓶颈。

Abstract: Graphene nano-ribbons, GNRs, are promising channel materials for next-generation ultra-miniaturised devices due to their exceptional electrical and thermal properties which arise from their atomic thickness, as well as their ability to have a size-dependent band-gap [1-9]. However, despite extensive efforts to reliably fabricate narrow GNR-based field-effect transistors [10-12], their integration into conventional transistor technologies remains hindered by challenges such as high fabrication costs and complex processing requirements [13, 14]. In this study, we present a direct-write, relatively low-cost and robust approach for fabricating sub-10 nm GNR-based FETs using electrochemical atomic force microscopy lithography with an alternating current (AC) bias, obviating the need for electrodes. We also explain the underlying electrochemical process and provide a model which can be used to describe it. Leveraging the high-precision positioning capability of AFM, this method enables precise nanoscale graphene patterning with feature sizes below 10nm. Compared with conventional lithographic techniques, photo- and electron-beam lithography i.e., PL & EBL, respectively [2, 15-20], it offers higher resolution, lower defect density, contamination-free processing, and the capability for in situ nanoscale device modification and characterisation. This work provides an efficient strategy for advancing GNR-based nanoelectronics.

### [118] [Negative Differential Resistance and Ultra-High TMR in Altermagnetic Tunnel Junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12711)
*Sajjan Sheoran,Luke Keenan,Declan Nell,Stefano Sanvito*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文利用非平衡格林函数结合密度泛函理论，预测轨道有序交替磁体（altermagnet）KV2Se2O构成的隧道结在低偏压下会出现显著的负微分电阻（negative differential resistance）效应，并伴随着隧穿磁电阻（tunneling magnetoresistance）的符号反转，表明交替磁隧道结可用于低偏压强非线性响应应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管交替磁体（altermagnet）在隧道结中可替代铁磁体（ferromagnet）并展现出巨大隧穿磁电阻、超快开关和低功耗功能，但大多数研究集中在线性响应（linear-response）区，而有限偏压（finite bias）下的非线性行为尚未被充分探索。

Method: 采用非平衡格林函数（non-equilibrium Green's functions, NEGF）结合密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）进行第一性原理计算，构建基于轨道有序交替磁体KV2Se2O的隧道结模型。

Result: 在平行构型（parallel configuration）下，电流随偏压先急剧上升后下降，在约0.14 V时几乎完全被抑制，产生显著的低偏压负微分电阻；反平行构型（antiparallel configuration）则呈现单调电流-电压曲线。此外，在0.13 V处观察到隧穿磁电阻的巨大增幅及符号反转（sign inversion）。

Conclusion: 交替磁隧道结（altermagnetic tunnel junction）可在低偏压下实现强非线性响应，具备在需要低电压非线性功能的应用中作为器件的潜力。

Abstract: Altermagnets can replace ferromagnets in tunnel junctions, yielding large tunneling magnetoresistance, ultrafast switching, and low-power functionality. While most studies explore the linear-response regime, interesting features emerge at finite bias, where the peculiar electronic structure of altermagnets gives rise to complex non-linear behaviour. Using non-equilibrium Green's functions implemented with density functional theory, we predict that a large low-bias negative differential resistance can be observed in an altermagnetic tunnel junction. Our proposed junction incorporates the orbital-ordered altermagnet KV2Se2O, whose quasi-2D Fermi surface plays a crucial role in realizing the negative differential resistance. Upon the application of a finite bias voltage, the current in the parallel configuration first increases sharply and then decreases, to be almost completely suppressed at around 0.14 V. At the same time, the antiparallel configuration displays a monotonic current-voltage curve. This behaviour, in addition to the negative differential resistance, supports a large tunneling magnetoresistance with sign inversion at 0.13 V. Our results suggest that altermagnetic tunnel junctions can be used as components in applications requiring strong non-linear response at low bias.

</details>


### [119] [Terahertz detection within charge density wave state](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12949)
*Zhi Li*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文从理论上论证了电荷密度波（charge density wave, CDW）材料凭借其集体电子响应，可突破传统半导体探测器在1 THz以上因德鲁德极限（Drude limit）导致的性能退化。通过施加静态偏置电场，能够连续调节CDW态的太赫兹共振吸收频率（0至截止频率），并将非线性整流电流提升一个数量级以上，从而为室温下工作的下一代超快太赫兹探测器提供了理想候选方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 太赫兹（Terahertz, THz）技术虽可实现多Tbps的卫星通信，但传统半导体探测器在1 THz以上因自由电子的德鲁德极限（Drude limit）而出现根本性性能退化，亟需新的材料体系突破这一瓶颈。

Method: 采用理论分析方法，研究电荷密度波（charge density wave, CDW）材料的集体电子响应，并考察静态偏置电场对CDW态太赫兹共振吸收频率及非线性整流电流的调控作用。

Result: 静态偏置电场可将CDW态的THz共振吸收频率从0连续调谐至截止频率（cutoff frequency），同时使非线性整流电流（nonlinear rectification current）提升一个数量级以上。

Conclusion: CDW材料凭借其前所未有的电场可调谐性（electric-field tunability），成为下一代室温工作、超快太赫兹探测器的理想候选材料。

Abstract: Terahertz (THz) technology enables multi-Tbps satellite communications, but conventional semiconductor detectors suffer from fundamental performance degradation above 1 THz due to the Drude limit of free electrons. Here, we theoretically demonstrate that charge density wave (CDW) materials offer a paradigm-shifting solution via their collective electronic response. We show that a static bias electric field can continuously tune the THz resonant absorption frequency of CDW states from 0 to cutoff frequency, and enhance the nonlinear rectification current by more than one order of magnitude. This unprecedented electric-field tunability makes CDW materials ideal candidates for next-generation ultrafast THz detectors working at room-temperature.

### [120] [Observation of end-to-end pumping in a quasiperiodic Fibonacci-type photonic chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13116)
*Arnob Kumar Ghosh,Ang Chen,Ashraf El Hassan,Patric Holmvall,Mohamed Bourennane,Annica M. Black-Schaffer*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 首先采用紧束缚模型（tight-binding formalism）进行数值模拟，证明仅通过链的微小结构变化即可将局域泵浦态在系统两端之间转移；随后在耦合光波导阵列（coupled optical waveguides）中实验实现该拓扑泵浦，光传播在近轴近似（paraxial approximation）下由紧束缚模型有效描述，从而实现理论与实验的直接对应。

Result: 数值模拟与实验均证实：将光注入系统一端的一个波导中，即可激活一个局域泵浦态；随着光沿波导阵列传播，该泵浦态被成功传输至另一端。进一步证明，该泵浦过程对结构形变（如波导阵列中的受控缺陷）保持鲁棒。

Conclusion: 准周期斐波那契型光子晶格（quasiperiodic Fibonacci-type photonic lattice）是一种鲁棒且实验可行的平台，可用于免于无序（disorder-resilient）的态传输。

Abstract: Topological pumps offer a promising route to operate as connecting buses, supplying efficient and robust connectivity between non-neighboring elements in a network. Here, we investigate a finite quasiperiodic Fibonacci-type photonic chain and demonstrate its ability for end-to-end pumping, with only small and simple changes to the system. First, we use a tight-binding formalism to numerically show that a localized pumping state can be transferred between opposite ends of the system, with only a small structural change to the chain. Then, we experimentally implement this topological pump in an array of coupled optical waveguides, where light propagation is effectively described by the tight-binding model under the paraxial approximation, enabling direct correspondence between theory and experiment. We numerically simulate and experimentally demonstrate pumping by injecting light into a single waveguide at one end of the setup, which activates a localized pumping state. As the light propagates along the wave guide array, it is also pumped to the other end. We further show that pumping remains robust against structural deformation, such as controlled defects in the waveguide array. Our results establish that quasiperiodic Fibonacci-type photonic lattices are a robust and experimentally viable platform for disorder-resilient state transfer.

### [121] [Highly Efficient Exciton Modulation in MoSe$_2$/PdSe$_2$ Heterostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13211)
*Petr Rozhin,Emma Contin,Danae Katrisoti,Till Weickhardt,Muhammad Sufyan Ramzan,Micol Bertolotti,Nouha Loudhaief,Bing Wu,Zdeněk Sofer,Takashi Taniguchi,Kenji Watanabe,Leonardo Puppulin,Stefano Dal Conte,Caterina Cocchi,Ioannis Paradisanos,Giancarlo Soavi,Giovanni Antonio Salvatore,Domenico De Fazio*

Conclusion: 层间电子耦合（interlayer electronic coupling）可以将激子布居重新导向辐射性通道，从而在不依赖化学修饰或应变的条件下有效增强二维半导体发光效率。

Abstract: Controlling exciton recombination in atomically thin semiconductors is central to their optoelectronic functionality, as the competition between radiative and non-radiative decay channels governs emission efficiency. Existing approaches, such as defect passivation, chemical doping, dielectric engineering, and strain tuning, primarily aim to suppress non-radiative losses. Here, we report a pronounced $\sim$6-fold enhancement of room-temperature A-exciton emission in a type-I MoSe$_2$/PdSe$_2$ van der Waals heterostructure, yielding a photoluminescence quantum yield of 6 %, compared to $\sim$1 % for as-exfoliated monolayer MoSe$_2$. This enhancement is accompanied by strong quenching of the B-exciton, consistent with interlayer electronic coupling that redistributes exciton populations toward the radiative A-exciton channel. Power- and temperature-dependent measurements reveal a suppression of exciton-exciton annihilation and a crossover to quenched emission at low temperature, indicating a redistribution of exciton relaxation pathways. Photoluminescence excitation spectroscopy further reveals a broadband enhancement spanning 450-725 nm, ruling out a resonance-specific mechanism. These results demonstrate that interlayer electronic coupling can be used as an efficient means to redirect exciton populations toward radiative channels, enhancing emission efficiency in two-dimensional semiconductors without chemical modification or strain.

### [123] [Reconfigurable chiral superconductivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13303)

Conclusion: 本研究将菱方石墨烯确立为可重构手征超导性（CSC）和基于可控等自旋纹理的超低功耗电子功能器件的独特平台。

Abstract: Rhombohedral multilayer graphene at high displacement fields hosts superconductivity emerging from a spin valley polarized quarter metal, with transport signatures suggestive of time reversal symmetry (TRS) breaking and chiral superconductivity (CSC). Here we use nanoscale SQUID on tip magnetometry to image isospin-polarized domains in rhombohedral pentalayer graphene and establish CSC via spatially resolved thermodynamic detection of TRS breaking. We find that the density at which domain walls proliferate at elevated temperatures coincides with the onset of CSC, indicating an underlying transition in the parent state that both induces superconductivity and reduces domain wall energy. We further show that the chiral domain structure in the superconducting phase is inherited from the isospin-polarized parent state. Strikingly, the CSC phase exhibits multiple transport regimes governed by configurations of chiral domains separated by highly resistive domain walls. We demonstrate deterministic, ultra low current control of these domains, enabling reversible switching between states of opposite chirality a defining CSC property absent in other superconductors. These results establish rhombohedral graphene as a unique platform for reconfigurable CSC and ultra low power electronic functionality based on controllable isospin textures.

### [124] [Thermoelectric enhancement from an asymmetric spectral-conductivity cusp in spin-1 chiral fermions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13323)

Method: 采用线性响应理论（linear-response theory）与自洽玻恩近似（self-consistent Born approximation）进行理论计算，并构建了一个最小尖峰模型（minimal cusp model）来隔离和阐明尖峰结构对热电增强的核心机制。

Result: 发现光谱电导的不对称尖峰显著增强了电子热电响应，在低温下同时提升了塞贝克系数（Seebeck coefficient）和电子品质因数（electronic figure of merit）。平庸带曲率的增大进一步强化了这种尖峰诱导的增强效应，尽管相应的态密度（density of states）反而变得更为平滑。增强效果在尖峰尖锐、高度不对称、且尖峰能量处光谱电导值较小时最为显著。

Conclusion: 光谱电导的不对称尖峰结构是增强自旋-1手性费米子体系热电响应的关键因素，其物理机制可以通过最小尖峰模型得到有效解释，为设计高性能热电材料提供了新的理论思路。

Abstract: A recent study showed that, in spin-1 chiral fermion systems composed of two linearly dispersing bands and one trivial band, impurity scattering produces an asymmetric cusp in the spectral conductivity. We demonstrate that this asymmetric cusp markedly enhances the electronic thermoelectric response. Using linear-response theory within the self-consistent Born approximation, we find low-temperature enhancements in both the Seebeck coefficient and the electronic figure of merit. Increasing the curvature of the trivial band further strengthens this cusp-induced enhancement, even though the corresponding density of states becomes smoother. To clarify this mechanism, we introduce a minimal cusp model for the spectral conductivity and show that the enhancement is most pronounced when the cusp is sharp and strongly asymmetric, and when the spectral conductivity at the cusp energy is small.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将模型简化为一组耦合谐振子，进而求解系统的本征频率。针对一种极化（polarization）模式使用自能方法，针对垂直极化模式则采用适用于经历了秩一更新的矩阵的特征值求解方法。

Conclusion: 多模分析揭示了单模近似所低估的物理效应，证明在谐振器-电子系统相互作用中必须考虑高阶模式才能准确描述回旋频率的软化行为。

Abstract: The use of resonators to modify the behavior of electromagnetic systems demonstrates its potential for application in a wide range of problems. However, existing theoretical studies often resort to the single-mode approximation, rarely considering a second resonator mode. In this paper, we show that including a large number of resonator modes in the model significantly enhances the softening effect of the cyclotron frequency of a two-dimensional electron system. We address this problem by demonstrating the possibility of reducing the system to a set of coupled harmonic oscillators and finding the eigenfrequencies of the oscillators. ### [126] [An Effective Scaling Framework for Non-Adiabatic Mode Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13376)
*A. M. Tishin*

TL;DR: 本文针对结构介质中的非绝热参量激发，提出了一种引入非线性频率调节器U的理论框架。通过非绝热性参数与非线性频谱失谐的竞争分析，揭示了强非线性振荡系统中非绝热参量放大的饱和现象：当非线性调节足够强时，指数模式增长被动态抑制，系统进入有界低占据态。数值验证展示了从双曲放大到频谱封锁（spectral blockade）诱导的有界响应的交叉行为，表明非线性频谱稳定化可能是驱动结构介质中有幅值非绝热动力学的一般机制。

Method: 引入非绝热性参数（non-adiabaticity parameter）作为时间局域诊断量，通过标度比（scaling ratio）分析其与非线性频谱失谐（nonlinear spectral detuning）之间的竞争。在扩展的100能级玻色子福克基（bosonic Fock basis）中进行数值验证。

Result: 强非线性振荡系统可实现非绝热参量放大（non-adiabatic parametric amplification）的饱和：当非线性调节器足够强时，指数模式增长被动态抑制，系统演化为有界低占据态。数值上观察到从双曲放大动力学向有界响应的交叉，伴随频谱封锁（spectral blockade）和高阶模式占据的抑制。

Conclusion: 非线性频谱稳定化（nonlinear spectral stabilization）可能是驱动结构介质中有限幅值非绝热动力学的通用机制。

Abstract: This study proposes an effective theoretical framework for non-adiabatic parametric excitation in structured media, incorporating a nonlinear frequency regulator U as a stabilizing mechanism. We introduce the non-adiabaticity parameter as a time-local diagnostic for driven non-stationary systems and analyze its competition with nonlinear spectral detuning through the scaling ratio. The principal physical result is that strongly nonlinear oscillatory systems can exhibit saturation of non-adiabatic parametric amplification: when the nonlinear regulator becomes sufficiently strong, exponential mode growth is dynamically suppressed and the excitation evolves toward a bounded low-occupancy regime. Using numerical verification in an expanded 100-level bosonic Fock basis, we demonstrate a crossover from hyperbolic amplification dynamics toward an effectively bounded response associated with spectral blockade and suppression of higher-order mode occupation. These results suggest that nonlinear spectral stabilization may represent a general mechanism for finite-amplitude non-adiabatic dynamics in driven structured media.

### [127] [Probing Floquet topological phases via non-Hermitian skin effect of reflected waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13563)

Method: 采用离散时间散射形式（discrete-time scattering formalism），分析Floquet陈绝缘体（Floquet Chern insulator）的散射问题。通过边界共振机制，建立反射矩阵的非厄米绕数（non-Hermitian winding number）与体Floquet不变量的关联。

Result: 发现反射波的NHSE依赖于入射波所在的准能量间隙，产生间隙依赖的Goos-Hänchen位移。进一步证明，对动量积分的GH位移可定量给出相应能隙的Floquet拓扑不变量。

Conclusion: 该工作揭示了驱动系统中反射波的频率依赖型非厄米趋肤效应，并提供了一个识别非平衡拓扑（non-equilibrium topology）的实空间散射方法。

Abstract: Periodically driven systems host topological phases without static analogs, such as the anomalous Floquet phase characterized by trivial bulk bands yet robust boundary modes. In this work, we investigate the scattering problem of a Floquet Chern insulator and reveal the non-Hermitian skin effect (NHSE) of reflected waves. Using a discrete-time scattering formalism, we demonstrate how the non-Hermitian winding number of the reflection matrix is linked to the bulk Floquet invariant via boundary resonances. This reflected-wave NHSE relies on which quasienergy gap the incident wave resides in, leading to a gap-dependent Goos-Hänchen (GH) shift. We further show that the momentum-integrated GH shift quantitatively yields the Floquet topological invariant of the corresponding gap. Our work highlights a frequency-dependent NHSE of reflected waves in driven systems and provides a real-space scattering approach to identify non-equilibrium topology.

</details>


### [128] [Cryogenic microwave frequency combs based on quantum paraelectric superconducting resonators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13571)
*Prasad Muragesh,Harikrishnan Sundaresan,Madhu Thalakulam*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文报道了一种基于钛酸锶（SrTiO₃）量子顺电相的全电气、片上、低温微波频率梳，利用其类Pockels效应实现腔相位调制，从而产生频率梳，并通过电场连续调控介电常数以控制工作频段，具备与低温量子技术集成的超小型化潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微波频率梳对于低温量子技术（如半导体及超导量子比特、量子电学计量学）至关重要，但现有方案依赖复杂、高功率的光学系统，无法满足低功耗、低温片上量子技术的需求。

Method: 利用钛酸锶（SrTiO₃）在量子顺电相（quantum paraelectric phase）中的类Pockels效应，在超导微波腔中通过场诱导有效二阶非线性系数χ(2)实现腔相位调制，从而产生微波频率梳。

Result: 实现了全电气、片上、低温运行的微波频率梳；通过外加电场连续调控SrTiO₃的介电常数（在量子顺电态下超过20,000），可控制频率梳的工作频率范围；超高的介电常数使器件具备超小型化设计能力。

Conclusion: 该全电气、片上微波频率梳无需复杂光学系统，可直接与低温量子技术集成，为微波频段的量子技术提供了一种低功耗、可调控、超小型化的频率梳方案。

Abstract: A frequency comb, known for its precision as an "optical ruler", features an evenly spaced spectral pattern. While these combs are vital in photonic quantum technologies, their microwave counterparts are now highly sought after for cryogenic quantum technologies, including semiconducting and superconducting qubits and quantum electrical metrology, which mainly operate in the microwave regime. However, microwave combs are still largely underexplored, and typically rely on complex, high-power optical systems incompatible with the low-power, cryogenic on-chip quantum technologies. In this manuscript, we present an all-electrical, on-chip, cryogenic microwave frequency comb on Strontium Titanate (SrTiO$_3$), exploiting its Pockels-like effect in its quantum paraelectric phase. Our device, utilizing a superconducting microwave cavity, generating the frequency comb via cavity phase modulation enabled by the field-induced effective $χ(2)$ of SrTiO$_3$. The ability to continuously vary the dielectric constant of SrTiO$_3$ by the application of electric field, in its quantum paraelectric phase, makes it possible to control the comb's operating frequency range. The exceptionally high dielectric constant of SrTiO$_3$, > 20,000 in its quantum paraelectric state, enables an ultra-miniature design and on-chip integration with cryogenic quantum technologies.

</details>


### [129] [Enhanced Near-Field Thermal Radiation Driven by Multiple Corner and Edge Modes in Subwavelength Square Nanowires](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13712)
*Jose Ordonez-Miranda,Minggang Luo,Michele Diego,Roman Anufriev,Victor Guillemot,Masahiro Nomura,Sebastian Volz*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过涨落电动力学（fluctuational electrodynamics）模拟发现，亚波长方形截面 SiC 纳米线之间的近场热辐射由多重拐角和边缘共振（multiple corner and edge resonances）主导，而非平面表面的单一表面声子极化激元（surface-phonon-polariton）通道。这些共振位于 SiC 的 Reststrahlen 带内，随纳米线变细而红移，并在分离间隙与纳米线厚度接近时实现热导的四倍增强，为几何调控的近场热传递提供了新平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统近场热辐射研究主要关注平面结构中的表面声子极化激元（surface-phonon-polariton）通道，但亚波长非平面几何（如方形纳米线）中是否存在更丰富的共振模式尚不清楚。本文旨在探索方形截面纳米线的拐角和边缘共振对近场热辐射的贡献及其调控机制。

Method: 采用涨落电动力学（fluctuational electrodynamics）模拟方法，对方形截面 SiC 纳米线之间的近场热辐射进行数值计算，分析其共振模式、光谱特征及热导随几何参数的变化规律。

Result: 方形纳米线的近场热辐射由多重拐角和边缘共振（multiple corner and edge resonances）主导，而非单一表面声子极化激元（surface-phonon-polariton）通道。共振频率位于 SiC 的 Reststrahlen 带内，且随纳米线厚度减小而红移。当分离间隙与纳米线厚度大致相等时，热导出现四倍增强，该增强由尺寸约束（dimensional confinement）与线间耦合（interwire coupling）之间的平衡决定。

Conclusion: 方形纳米线可作为几何调控近场热传递（geometry-controlled near-field heat transfer）的通用平台，在纳米尺度热管理和能量转换中具有应用潜力。

Abstract: We demonstrate that the near-field thermal radiation between subwavelength SiC nanowires with square cross sections is dominated by multiple corner and edge resonances rather than the single surface-phonon-polariton channel of planar surfaces. Fluctuational electrodynamics simulations reveal that these resonances lie within the SiC Reststrahlen band, redshift for thinner nanowires, and yield a four-fold enhancement of thermal conductance. This maximum enhancement occurs when the separation gap nearly matches the nanowire thickness, balancing dimensional confinement and interwire coupling. These findings establish square nanowires as a versatile platform for geometrycontrolled near-field heat transfer in nanoscale heat management and energy conversion.

</details>


### [130] [Shubnikov-de Haas Characterization of Superconductor-Semiconductor Heterostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13722)
*A. M. Zimmerman,Saeed Fallahi,Sergei Gronin,Tyler Lindemann,Patrick Sohr,Ray Kallaher,Alejandro Alcaraz Ramirez,Georg W. Winkler,Samuel M. L. Teicher,William Cole,Sebastian Heedt,Eoin O'Farrell,Gijs de Lange,Roman Lutchyn,Michael J. Manfra,John Watson*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文报道了一种利用Shubnikov-de Haas（SdH）振荡测量来提取混合超导体-半导体纳米结构中关键材料参数的新方法，包括量子阱载流子密度、自旋-轨道耦合强度以及输运和量子散射时间。最重要的是，通过分析金属-半导体耦合对二维电子气散射时间的影响，可以在无需任何器件制备或mK温度测量的条件下快速获取邻近效应超导能隙（proximity-induced superconducting gap）的信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混合超导体-半导体纳米结构是凝聚态物理（condensed matter physics）和量子信息处理研究的重要基础，其进展高度依赖对自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）、能带偏移（band offsets）和材料无序（disorder）等本征材料参数的表征、控制和优化能力。现有方法往往需要复杂的器件制备和极低温（mK）测量，亟需一种更简便的参数提取手段。

Method: 利用Shubnikov-de Haas（SdH）振荡测量方法，对Al薄膜下方InAs量子阱中的二维电子气（2DEG）与金属电子态耦合的异质结构进行全磁阻数据分析，从而提取量子阱载流子密度、自旋-轨道耦合强度以及输运散射时间（transport scattering time）和量子散射时间（quantum scattering time）。

Result: 提取的二维电子气散射时间受到金属-半导体耦合强度的影响，利用这一关联可在无需任何器件加工或mK温度测量的条件下快速获取邻近效应超导能隙（proximity-induced superconducting gap）的信息。

Conclusion: 该简单测量方法能够获得丰富的信息，可作为混合材料优化的一个重要工具。

Abstract: Hybrid superconductor-semiconductor nanostructures are a central component for research spanning condensed matter physics and quantum information processing. Continued progress relies critically on the ability to characterize, control, and optimize several intrinsic material properties including spin-orbit coupling, band offsets, and disorder in a device-relevant stack that necessarily couples the electronic states of a superconducting metal film and a semiconductor. Here we report a new method to extract fundamental material parameters utilizing simple Shubnikov-de Haas (SdH) oscillation measurements in heterostructures in which metallic electronic states are coupled to a two-dimensional electron gas (2DEG) residing in an InAs quantum well beneath an aluminum thin film. Proper analysis of the full magnetoresistance data facilitates extraction of the quantum well carrier density, spin-orbit coupling strength, and both transport and quantum scattering times. Most importantly, the extracted scattering times in the 2DEG are impacted by the metal-semiconductor coupling strength allowing us to quickly gain information on proximity-induced superconducting gap without any fabrication or mK measurements. The wealth of information that is accessed with these simple measurements positions this methodology as an important tool for hybrid materials optimization.

</details>


### [131] [Magnetization-dependent and stacking-tunable Edelstein effect in two-dimensional magnet 2H-VTe2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13763)
*Weiyi Pan,Jaroslav Fabian*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 基于第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）和对称性分析（symmetry analysis），本文证明了埃德尔斯坦效应（Edelstein effect）可本征地存在于二维面内铁磁半导体2H-VTe2中，其自旋积累行为强烈依赖于磁化取向，并且通过改变堆叠构型（AB/BA堆叠）可实现额外自旋分量的可逆切换，为高效自旋轨道扭矩器件提供了新平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 埃德尔斯坦效应在磁性系统中可通过电流诱导的自旋积累与内禀磁序耦合实现磁化翻转，在自旋电子器件中极具应用前景。在二维磁性系统中实现并调控该效应，对发展高效率、多功能自旋电子学器件尤为重要。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算与对称性分析相结合的方法，研究单层和双层2H-VTe2中埃德尔斯坦效应的行为，分析不同磁化取向和堆叠构型（AB/BA堆叠）下的自旋积累组分。

Result: 在具有D3h晶体对称性的单层2H-VTe2中，当磁化沿+x（+y）方向时，仅允许时间反演偶（time-reversal-even）z分量和时间反演奇（time-reversal-odd）y(x)分量的自旋积累。在AB或BA堆叠的双层体系中，对称性降为C3v，出现额外自旋分量（如dSy_even、dSz_odd等），且这些分量可通过层间滑动在AB/BA构型间可逆切换。

Conclusion: 研究加深了从对称性和第一性原理角度对二维磁性系统中电流诱导自旋积累的理解，并指出2H-MX2材料体系是实现本征可调埃德尔斯坦效应、用于高效自旋轨道扭矩（spin-orbit torque）器件的理想平台。

Abstract: The Edelstein effect in magnetic systems enables magnetization switching via the coupling between current-induced spin accumulation and intrinsic magnetic order, and is therefore highly promising for next-generation spintronic devices. Realizing and manipulating the Edelstein effect in two-dimensional (2D) magnetic systems is particularly desirable for achieving high-efficiency and multifunctional spintronic applications. In this work, based on first-principles calculations and symmetry analysis, we demonstrate that the Edelstein effect can intrinsically arise in the 2D in-plane ferromagnetic semiconductor 2H-VTe2, with its behavior strongly dependent on the magnetization orientation. For monolayer 2H-VTe2 with D3h crystal symmetry, under an applied current along the +x direction, only the time-reversal-even z component and the time-reversal-odd y(x) component of the spin accumulation are allowed when the magnetization is aligned along +x (+y). For ferromagnetic bilayer 2H-VTe2 in AB or BA stacking, where the crystal symmetry is reduced to C3v, additional spin components emerge with the presence of in-plane magnetization. Specifically, for magnetization along +x (+y), besides dSz_even and dSy_odd (dSz_even and dSx_odd), extra components such as dSy_even and dSz_odd (dSy_even) become allowed. Notably, these additional components can be reversibly switched by changing the stacking configuration from AB to BA via interlayer sliding. Our results not only deepen the understanding of current-induced spin accumulation in 2D magnetic systems from both symmetry and first-principles perspectives, but also identify 2H-MX2 materials as a promising platform for realizing intrinsic and tunable Edelstein effects in high-efficiency spin-orbit torque devices.

</details>
